Atrochratar annsin na mic lasna h-aithrib & na h-aithri lasna maccu & na braithri la araile.
Ro tuitsetar iarum cenn i cenn & taeb re taeib i ruma na ratha iarsin, go ro linsat ar-ruadbuinne fola & a n-uanfad cro an muir impo, co n-derna aenclar crodercc di.
Ba foruallach forniata, ba tremait tarcaisnech an feogad do bertsat na fir sin for a m-bidbadaib icc faghbail bais, ar nir' bo mied leo a airechad da m-bidbadaib forru comad lainni leo betha ina bas.
Ba h-ainiarmurtach tra in galach sin muinnteri Cesair ettorru fein, ar airm i m-batar na D laech acht becc ni terna eludach bethadh no ainfer innisin sccél dip, acht attrochratar comthuitim for lar na rathae i rabatar.
Ni raibe isin bith riemh lucht aenlunga fuair in n-imforcraidh urdurcais no clua no molta dara n-eisi.
Ro tencsat muinter Poimp iet arsin ina n-dumada dímora do collaip ruste ruamanta for lar na ratha.
Tainic a n-gus & a n-aiccned forta.
Ro eirig tróige & triamainiu mór ina cridib ic a n-decsain.
As edh ro raidset gurbo h-ingnad adbul, & gur'bo machtnughud mor leo daoine isin doman do cartain a tigerna fon samail sin ed ón iet fein dia marbad fein ar a seirc.
Ro tairrngedh iarum an raith docum tiri occo, & ro h-adnaicit cuirp na laecraidhe leo i n-inis Soloin fo fochlaidhiph na caladh.
Conid remscél do remscelaip catha moir na Tessaili co n-icci sin.
Martra muintire Vuilt ainm an scéoil.
Aidid Curio.
Nirsa timmiu innasin an t-imairecc irgaili ro fas i c-crichaib na h-Affraici iter muinteraib na rig cetna.
I S amlaidh tarla sin ed ón airri da airrigib ro cuir Cesair co n-da leigion da mhiledhaib immailli fris, d'iarraid loin dó co h-inis Saird ocus co h-inis Siccil for muir Torrein, amal atrubartmar remainn, Curio a ainm inn airrig.
O rainic Curio co h-inis Siccil as fair deisidh lais techt i cricha na h-Affraici d'iarraidh indmais indti & da scarad fri nert Poimp ica m-bai i forlamus co n-icci sin.
Ro taithmigh iarum a longa a murrusc deiscertach insi Siccil imach, & ro toccbait a fáinbreiti siuil forta, & ro gabatar co menmnach la fiugair na gaeithe indes ic mall-ascnam in mara do cum criche na h-Affraici gach n-direch, gur' gab cuan & caladphort i comfocraib sencathrach na Cartagini isin Affraic.
Tainic Curio fo tir annsin, & ro gab longphort for bru srotha Ticcir edh imcian o chuan an mara suas.
Cein batar na sloig ic suidiugud i l-longpuirt, tainic Curio co n-úathad da saenmuinntir leis do remughad & d'airddecsaini tulaig uraird bai os cind an longphuirt.
Bend sleibe moir ocus garball clochda & cairrci cenngarba imda osin tulaig sin.
Ba h-uraibinn an t-inadh sin, & ba h-inadh fairccsina isin tir uile é.
Ro gab Curio acc siubal gacha cnuic d'araili ann iarsin, co torracht ainfer do lucht in tire ina dochom.
Saigis Curio coir comraid fair, & freccrais an t-occlaech affracda é.
‘I Ndot eolach isin tir-si, a occlaigh?’
for Curio.
‘Am eolach on am,’ olse.
‘An fil senchus a dind & a cnoc & a cathrach let?’
for Curio.
‘Ata amal ro faccsat ar n-aithri & ar senaithri linn dano,’ ar an t-occlach.
‘Caide ainm na tulca-sa i tam immorro?’
for Curio, ‘& ainm na cairrci-si for ar cul?’
‘Carrac Anteus ainm na cairrcci tra,’ for an t-oclaech, ‘& Tulach na Gleca ainm na tulcu-sa for a tai.’
‘Cidh ni dia filet na h-anmanna sin fortha?’
for Curio.
‘Man bad eimhilt lat ro inneosainn deit uili do leir,’ for an t-óclaech affracda.
‘Innis commin,’ for Curio.
‘Coraidh ingnad bai isin tir-si gan athair, gan mathair daenna occa,’ ol se, ‘acht a geineamain a crislach an talman cene.
Anteus mac Terrae a ainm.
Ba mór a nert inn fir sin.
Ni cumcedh duine na daoini coimleng friss.
Innuair ticced dith neirt do nos-leicced 'na ligi fria lar.
O no thaidhledh a thaeb an talmain ticced a nert fein do, co l-linta do calmatus dermair é o mhathair bhunaidh ed ón on talmain.
Acht ni riccedh somh a les com-minic sin iter, air ni fogbaithe neach no fuilngedh a nert cena.
Atrocratar acaide in tire leis, & nach long no taidhled in cuan-sa this ni tintadh slan uad; gurro fasaigedh in ferand-sa uile do na lamta a tadall do muir no do tir.’
O ro fasaigedh in tir immi is ed ba tuara do, feoil oss & fiadmil & mathghaman & leoman do neoch no marbadh fein ic cuairt in fasaig cach dia.
I S edh ba tegdais & ba leaba ligi do, uamdorus dilenn mór fil isin carraic-si thall.
Ni bidh tugha no craibredh no pell no brothrach no breccan no crocenn anmanna fui isin lepaid sin, acht a thaeb frisin talam nocht cenae.
Ticced calmatus mór do-som desin co m-ba nert nua ar gach lo leis tre tadall a mathar bunaidh ed ón in talam.
I S uadh sin atberar Carracc Antei frisin carraicc & Uaim Antei frisin uama fil inti.
Rainic tra clu & urdarcus in uilc sin fo cethair-aird an domain fa deoidh.
Rainic in clu cetna co h-airm i r-raibe in t-anclund & ind ail bratha & in fer nach fuilngti comlund, in milid merdana mormenmnach, in t-occlaech ard allata andiarraidh ed ón Hercuil mór mac Ampitrionis.
O 'tcuala Hercuil ieram in n-ainceis-sin icc indredh na h-Affraicci, ni ro damhair do can a innsaiged, fo bith ba h-e a bes, gach inad isin domun i cluinedh torathar no olc difulaincc do bith tocht da saigid occus a dichor ass.
Tainic ieram fo test in torathair.
Cien gairit bai no co toracht in tir-si & gur' sir an ferann uile, & co tainic for fuillecht in coradh docom a leabtai.
Ni bai Antei i fus annsin, acht bai i c-cuairt in ferainn amal ba gnath bes do.
O na fuair Ercul é, deisidh ina suide i m-mullach na tilca-sa for a filti-si sund.
Nir'bo cian in urnaide dó ann intan atconnairc in coraidh seachai docom a uamha, & ualach mór fair do cesaib & do croicnib mathgaman & leoman.
Taidbris Antei for Hercuil, & do bert da aire é, ar ba ferrdha denam an laich atconnairc.
Teit iarum dia uama & cuirid a eire ossfeola de for lar, & gabaid for ongad-comailt a cuirp do ola & do neithib inmaraib eli, & do methrad slemunrighin, co nar'bo sleimne lam for iascc no aigred ina for gach m-ball de.
Do rocht Antei iarum co h-airm i m-boi Hercuil isin tulaig-si, & foccrais cor gleaca fair.
Ba h-adma eolach Ercail isin ceird sin, ar ro ghnathaigh co mor a denam i cluichi oenaig Olimp.
Atract Hercuil & ro cuir a arma uadh, & ro cuir dano de for lar ina farrad croicenn in leomain bai imme, ed ón leoman ro marb-som fein i fidneimed Neimi.
Scuchais cach go araili dib iarsin, & snadmait ar-righthe, & do berat combloscc calma, gur' ben tul-etain caich fria araile dibh amal bloisccbeim comlad rigduini fria h-ursaind.
Ro sinset occus ro naiscset a n-doiti rigremra romora dar braigtib occus dar muinelaibh occus dar formnaib araili.
Ba comrac dá coimtren sin.
Ba borp an buaidredh-mesccadh.
Ba ferrda an fasccud-tarraincc do bert cach for araile dib.
Ba h-ingnad mor & ba machtnugud adbul la gach fer dib nech isin domun da freccra amlaid sin.
Air atar la gach fer dib ni boi fer a frestal isin bith.
Ro gab Hercuil ic coiccill a neirt co mor ina aghaidh, & ni dernae acht a congbail cena fris.
Ro gab Anteus immorro icc airimirt a brig gan dichell ina aghaidh sium, co tainic a allus, & gor' luathaigh a anal, & cur tercaighsett a seitrigthe gleaca ed ón a O ro airig Hercuil sin ro duin a dá doitrigid im cael a droma, & tucustair tendad & tarraing-drutad tren-talcair fair, gurro dlúthaigh a bruinne fria bruinne, & go ro cuir a smeich dar a muinel, & co tuc glun ina gabal do, gur ro bris a ferda uili, & tuc urcur fo comus dé 'arsin co tarla ina lige for lar uadh.
O ro tadaill a taeb in talmain ro suig co h-athlam a allus fo cétóir, & ro atnuauigh a briga, & tucc clisedh calma fair, gorro scail rigti in miled imme, & ro eirig co seitreach dar Hercuil.
Ba saeth mór la Hercail sin, & ro saoil nach claefedh iter e.
Immacomrainic doib doridisi.
Ba doidngi do Hercuil commór don cur sin e innas don cur reimi.
Ni fuair riem baramail an comlainn sin.
Ni bai uair bad cora da easccairdib subachus inas in uair sin ar nertmaire in cuingid comlainn tarla ina agaidh.
Araisin forerigh Hercuil co ferrda in coimleng tanaisi fris, gur gab for a énirtniugud commor.
O ro airigh iarum Anteus a briga & a nert ic traethad leiccid fein asa deoin e docom lair, go ro eirig fo cetoir cona brigaib nuae ann.
Do beir Hercuil aicne fair 'arsin, conidh tre tadall in talman ticctis a brigha & ticced a calmattus do.
Ro gap Hercuil co seitriuch for a farrach, arsin, no cur' triall Anteus a leiccin fri lar dorisi.
Frithailis Ercuil co h-athlam é, occus dúinidh a dá doitrigidh imbe, & nos-toccaibh i n-airde co nar' tadaill a cosa in talmain iter, & asbert friss: ‘Fuirigh it sesom amlaidh sin,’ for Hercuil, ‘ar ni leiccfither duit tadall in talman festa.
Toit cuccum-sa i l-let-sa.’
Iss ed sin asbert Ercuil, & toccbaidh ind airdde co h-opunn é & faiscciditer a rightea & a taeba, co n-derni smirammair da cnamaib immedhon a croicind, & ni ro leicc co lar e no gur cuir a chride ina lommannaib fola & ina cubarcaepaib cro dara beolu sechtair.
Fuair Anteus bas la Hercuil don gleic sin isin tulaig-si, conid desin atberar Tulach na Gleca di o sin anall.
‘Is uasal in t-ainmniugud sin tra,’ for Curio.
‘Fo gabar ainm as uaisle di-siu ina sin,’ for in t-occlach affracda ‘ed ón Tulach inn Athlongphuirt ainm eli di.’
‘Cid ni da ta side dano?’
for Curio.
‘Ni ansa,’ for in t-occlach affracda ‘ed ón Scip Affracain co n-ocbaid na Roma immailli fris ro suidigsiot longphort immon tulaig-si & 'mo bruigib in t-srotha-sa tis airm a suidhigter for longphort-sa innossae.
Nach faicci fein slicht na tochalta & inad in fail & buna na cuailled & aite na m-machad & torainn in morlongcphuirt fós ann?
I S as so ro creachadh occus ro h-indredh inn Affraic uili leiss, & ro delaraigedh a slóig & ro croth in tir uile.’
‘Amae, a occlaig,’ for Curio, ‘cia h-ainm in cathair lethrainte mor ut tall ar ar n-incaibh.
Inni in Cartagin í?’
‘I S isi on eiccin,’ for in t-occlaech affracda.
‘Cid edh ni fo cainblath forraccaib Scip í?’
for Curio.
‘Ro ba menmnach linmar cidh iter occbad in baili sin,’ for in t-occlach affracda, ‘& ro mudaigit uile la Scip iat, & ro trasccrait muir na cathrach leis, co fil fon m-blath atcithi-si.’
Tainic faeilti mor ocus sonairte aiccnid do Curio de sin, ar ba celmaine maith leis a teccmáil isin longphort as ar' cloedh inn Affraic la Scip.
Tainic iarum co subach somenmnach docom a muinntire, & deisidh ettorra ina longphort.
Bai airri togaidhe fri lama Poimp for in n-Affraic in tan sin, Varus a ainm.
Ro cuala side Curio do rochtain isind Affraic.
Ro tinoilit fo cetoir leis a milidh & ina m-bai d'occbaidh na Roman uili ina fochair tes.
Bai ócclaech lanmaith dano i r-righi ic na h-Affracdaib fein in tan cettnae sin, Iuba ainm in rig sin.
Ni bai for Affraic riem ri bad uilliu ferann inas, ar bai fo a mamus o turccbail greiniu, & o sleib Athalaint innair co crichaib na h-Aissia sair, & o bord tuaiscertach mara Torrein atuaid co crichaib deiscertacha an teintide fo des.
Ba h-escara bunaidh do Curio in fer isin, ar ro fobair Curio a aithrigad som an tan bai cumachta & commas isin t-senad Romanach occo.
O 'tcuala Iuba iarum a beith-siumh isin Affraic, ro tinoilit a sloig da saigid do digail a ancride for Curio, & dano bai do troma & do teinni na rige Romanda for in Affraic gurbo lainne leis congnam icc denam eissídha na Romanach innas icc denam a sida.
Do roctatar iaram sloig imda ilarda re h-edh n-atgairit do saigid Iuba annsin.
Do rochtatar amh annsin na h-Autolapecda.
Do rochtatar na Numecda.
Dorochtatar ann na Getulda daine sin na gnathaigit dillata fothu iter.
Do roctatar ann popuil duba na Muretae.
Do rocht ann popul na Marmarda.
Do rocht ann popul na Nasamonda.
Do rocht ann popul na n-Gartamantecda.
Do rocht ann popul na Matarcta.
Do rocht ann popul na Masili, & lucht na h-Affraici uile arcena.
Tainic tra Iuba ri na n-Affracda cusin t-socraiti móir sin gur' gab longphort i n-imel in maige i m-boi Curio.
Tainic Vair in t-airri cona sochraiti leis, gur' gab longphort isin cinn aile don maig cétna.
O 'tclos do Curio in t-sochraite mor sin do taidecht ina docom, rus-lion oman & imeccla re h-imat na slog do dechatar in n-aires catha dó, & ar a med ro ba menmarc leis ancraide a aithrigtha do digail do Iuba fair, & dano nir'bo tairisi leis toct i n-imclaidbed catha a n-agaid a namat lasin m-bretaig sloig tarla ina farrad, air ni do miledaib bunaidh Cesair iatt, acht commascach sloig ro tecclamait a cathair Corpin & asna caistiellaip aile ro gab Cesair isin Ettail.
Araisin ni ro airig neach for Curio an crithoman sin do beith fair, acht do roini do degglor & do danacht aiccnid & do sonairte urlabra i fiadnaisi a slogh, conar' sailset nach smuainedh eccla ina menmain.
I S i ierum comairli ro túir ma menmain, danacht do denam & a slog do breith leis gan fuirech docum a namat, ardaig na beith acht oen comairli occo o ro soistis aít inn imairicc ed ón an cath do gnimh.
La sodain ro cind ar an comhairle sin, & ro eit a arma, & tucc a slogha fon arm-gaiscced leis asin longphort immach for lar-medon in maige.
I S annsin do rola airri na h-Affraice doib ed ón Vair, cona muinntir eineach i n-inchaip for in muig & se icc saigid in longphuirt i m-boi Curio.
Atar leis is ann fogebad é.
Immacomrainic doib annsin & ferthair gleo ainmin etrocar ettarra, cur raemid for Vair cona muintir docum a scor, co ro tuairccsett muinter Curio na drommanna doib gan anadh gan impodh, nocur tairmiscset daingne in longphuirt iatt.
Ro h-indised do Iuba do airdrig na h-Affraici sin.
Ba faeilihd leiside gan cosccur Curio do breith ina eccmais fein, & gan maidm catha fair noco roised-sium ina docom.
I Msaei Curio co cosccur mor & co failte dermair da longphort fen in n-aidce sin.
I S i comairli do roini Iuba ri Affraici, taidecht ind aidce sin fo cetoir cona slógaib leis asin longphort amach, & imsaei reimi co taei tostach taithenach, co rainic fanglenn mór bai ind eitermedon an muighe, co n-derna costadh catha annsin, co tainic dobursoilsi na maitne muiche arna barach.
O tainic iarum cetsoilsi in laei cuicci, ro ordaig a sloga & do roine catha coraigte dib & ro indill co h-infoilgide i n-glacaib in glennai & i m-mamannaip na tulach batar imbi.
Ro cuir a marcsluag & Saburra tanaisi rig na Nimdecda rempo docom longphuirt Curio do saigid debta for lucht in longphuirt & da m-breccad leis docom na cathetarnaide ro coraig in ri fora cind.
Ni bai samail na ceilge sin ro ordaigh-siumh acht amal do gnither selg na n-aspiti i crichaib na h-Eigipti tes.
Cineli nathrach sin, & lecca logmara ina n-incaib, & a n-aitriubh fein i scailpib carracc & i n-uamtollaib talman.
In cu bís fo tograim do beir a erball isin fochlae talman i m-bi nathir dibh.
O 'tcí in nathir fosgadh in erbaill do beir a cend dar in foclla immach.
Glacaid in cu de fordorus na fochlai a scornaigh i l-leith anníar da n-neim, conid fon innas sin bregthar asa aiti ed ón I S fon samail sin dano ro cuir Iuba ri Affraici uathaichi marcsluaigh do celgad Curio & da thochuriudh asa longphort docom in t-sloigh moir ro innill for a cind.
Nirbo cealg gan conach in celg sin tra. arro urail Curio for a marcsluagh teacht isin aidchi remi asna scoraib seachtair guro taistlitis redhi an muighi resin slogh araill.
O ro thaithni cetsoillsi na maidni muichi iarum ro forcongair for a sluagaib uili ergi, & dataegat asa scoruibh seachtair, & tuargabsat idna catha forro, & do tennat a n-deaghaidh na marcach isin magh.
O rainic marcsluag Curio gu lar an muighi do rala Saburra & marcsluagh na n-Affracda focétoir Fossaigit immaireach n-ugra forro nogur rainic Curio cona muintir uili da saighidh.
La sodain faemait na h-Affracda teiced ceilgi rompo docum an glenna i m-badar na catha coraighthi for a cind.
O 'tconnairc Curio cona muntir sin, ro gabsat co dichra duthrachtach ica slaighi 'na n-diaidh, gur rancadar larmedon in glenna.
Co cualadar glaedh-beccedaigh na stocc slescamm slemansolus & fogurnuall na cornn & na n-adarc & na cuislenn catha, & co facadar na h-oincoin obeli & na mergeda ailli eiteacha & gristaithneamh na n-arm n-áichthide n-urnocht os na cathaibh coraightibh do gach aird & do gach airchinn dib anair & anníar, annes & atuaidh rompo & ina n-diaidh, co n-dernad crotimcill & amdabhach nemi & buaili bodba do cathaibh na n-Affracda immon n-gleand uili 'na mortimcell, co na bui accó cae nó conair no cindis ass mani cláitis in talmain fothu, no mana dictis for foluamain isin aeer uastu nó mani cindis i cend a cetcomlín do miledhuibh foa n-armgaisced co rún a marbta uili la gach n-aenfear dib.
Sochtais Curio ic faiscin in anforlaind.
Sochtait a munter uili dano.
Ba nemada ind abairt da ronsat arsin.
Nír'
urmaisedar maith nó saich do denum.
Nir' thriallsat tecedh no imbualadh nó gnimh catha do denumh re méd ba tapad & ba h-uathbas léo in comlinad & in comegur do bertsat a m-bidbaidh for in glenn do gach aird impo gan a faiscin, gan a forcloistecht co n-igi sin.
Ba deithbir dona míleduib cena cia nos-linadh in cridenbas amlaid sin, ar rosn-imbir cid iter in n-uathgrain cetna for graigibh eciallaidibh na n-echradh badar leo, cona tainic nach sonairti aignidh nó nach metughudh menman doib frisin comgair cumaisc atcualadar do nuall na stocc & d'fothrom na n-echradh & d'fogurmuirnn na miled, d'fidren na saigheat srubderg, do scretgaire na foga faebrach, do drongair na luireach lineach lancuir, da comtuaircnigh na sciath scellbolgach, do comcoicedul na claideb cruaidgér claslethan, da comgeoin na sochaidhi ic comtriall inn imairic i n-aenfecht & i n-aenfaball Ro traigset & ro truinset echrada muintire Curio ic cloistecht frisin morborbgair sin, co n-derna eocho trethi timmi triamain i seitfedca anescaidi dib, cona frecraidis a sporad nó a m-brostud.
O 'tconncadar immorro na h-Affracda for in fabairt sin iad ro comgairset in aenfecht forto.
Ro scucsat co neam-imcoimairceach cucu, eter coissidi & marcach, curo crithnaigh an talam fo cossaib a n-echradh, co n-derna luaithreadh & denngur dona maghraenaibh ro cinniseat, gur fasadar dobur-neoill dorca dubciach uasa & do impo imaltar in dendgair os analaib na n-each & na n-anrad ic dianascnam na sligeadh do saighidh a namat.
Ro timcellait na Romanaig desen & da ronad circull bodba impo d'ogbaid na h-Affraici, cona bui asrus eluda accu.
Ro gabad co comtrom do gach aird dib for in esarcain 'arsin do saighdibh a fidbaccaibh, do liagaib lam, do crunnclochaibh tabull, do slegaib slinnleathnaibh, da craiseachaib crandreamraib, do laignibh leathanlebraibh, do manasaib miled, da loirgfeirtsibh laech, do claidbibh claslethna carad, do beraib bodba birguirt rinnaithi.
Ro badar luireacha dluithi dianscailti desin, & cathbairr caema coimbristi, & sceith scoiltidi, & taeib tolla & cuirp cirrthi & oig athgaithi, & troich trascairthi & laeich londa ledarta, & milidh marbta, & colla curad i cossair cro.
Ro cuired cach i ceann araili dona Romanchaib annsen co n-dernad aenmell dibh etir na h-Affracdaibh for lar in gleanna.
Ro sonnait, ro dluthait, ro dingit, ro daingeantuairgit iad 'arsin, co na cumgadh neach dib imirt a sceith nó imluadh a claidib no sadud a sleighi nó luth a lamh.
In fer imeclach dib for a n-urailedh in t-omun immel in imairic d'fagbail ic saighidh immedon a munteri ni roichedh in conair no indsaighedh noco m-bidis cruiseacha & claidbi a munteri fein comtarsna trit, conna bui acco 'ar sin acht fulung a marbta, air ni cuimgidís imbirt a n-arm isin crobuailidh cumaing i m-badar & gen go n-imbridis a namait a n-armu forro no taethsaidis do comfuasmadh & do comtuaircnigh a n-arm & a n-uchtbruinde fein fri araili.
No bidis na h-abaigi & na cuirp cirrti, & na firecta fuathaidi ina comseasam frisna beoaib eturru, air ni bid acco conair no taetsaidis co lear ar a daingni ro dluthdingset a m-bidbaidh cach i cend araili dibh.
Bá digbail faelti immorro co mor do na h-Affraicdib na faccadar in diach do bertsat a n-airm fein for na Románchaib annsin.
Air ro badar imda srotha fola & caepa cro & cnamradhach & lamha leoiti & leithcind letarda & inni & inathraighi ic na Románchaib ic a tuindsium fo traigthibh isin gliaidh sin.
Nir digladar na h-Affracda athrigadh Annibail no indred na h-Affraici nó a n-anfalta uili riam for na Romanchaib co n-igi sin.
Dia-fris cena, is ingnad in gnim do rala andsin ed ón in t-ár do ratsat námait na Roman forto, a maissi & a foghnum sin do bith don righ Romanach ed ón do Poimp.
Ro soillsigh & ro diglae in t-aer os na sloghaibh 'arsin, air ro scuap in gaeth dib inn dobarnellgail n-dendgurda bui uasú, ó ro linsat na sritidi fola flannruaidhi & na sruthlinti cro in talmain fothu, go m-badar 'na n-aibhnibh dergruada fuirri, gonar' erig luaithredh nó dendgur i n-airdi dí.
La sodain atconnairc Curio na h-ara mora sin, & a muintir uili gan elodach innisin scel dib do bith acht comtoitim docom bais an aonfecht ina fiadhnaisi.
Nir' fulaing a aignead do bith ic a fegad & gan acmaing a foritni aigi.
Ro leicc go nertmar nemleasc docum lair é.
Ro mebaidh cromaidm da cridhi 'na cliabh, & dos-fanic bas i m-medhon a miledh.
Atrocartar a muinter do gach aird immi, conna terna aenfear innisen scel dib as sin.
Maith in fer ro tuit annsin eturru-sum ed ón Curió.
Ni ro as isin Roím riam a comaesa adbar bad ferr innas meni millead fein, & mina treigeadh in seanadh, & meni creacadh in Roim & in rígrecht re Cesair darcenn óir & indmais.
Do rala do-sum andsin a threcudh don atharda ro treic, & a corp saerclanna soceneoil co corpaib a muinteri leis do bith gan onoir cainti nó adnaicti fair i crichaib aineoil fo cossaib con & cuanart & sinnach & serríach & én & etaidi ingnathae na h-Affraici.
Conid remscel do remscelaib catha moir na Tesaili co n-igi sin.
Aidead Curio ainm in sceoil.
Aideadh Aip.
Ro comét in toictiu co cudruma na da tuiseach sin ed ón Poimp & Cesair, eter sonmighi & donmigi frisin re sin.
Tainic la Kalni Enair fuisin, & tossach bliadne nui.
Is ed on aimsir i n-denta atharruch consul & maer & airrigh & ordaighthi cogaidh & sloghaidh la Romanu dogrés.
Ro battar dá consul togaidi la Romana antansin dano ed ón Lentulus & Agellus a n-anmand.
Is ed bui re a consulachta co n-igi sin in la sin, arai sin is iad da roine tinol in t-sloig & caingni in t-seanaidh & ordaighthi in rigrechta in la sin beos.
I S ann ro tinoileadh in mor-coinni sin isinn Eipir i c-crichaibh na Greicci Mori, ar nir' lamsat tadall na Roma la h-imeccla Cesair.
Do ronait tra ordaigthe móra isin coinne sin la Romanu.
Ro cinnsett in n-airdrige do Poimp airett bad beo.
Ro ordaigsett mair & airrig fria lamae for cendadachaibh in domain do tobach a cisa & do tinol a slog docom an mor-catae doneoch batar fo a mamus som dibh cettus ed ón ilcinélu na h-Affraici & sluaigh imda na h-Aisia & inn airthir uile. arro gab Cesair fortamlus in domain o Roim siar.
Ro scailed iarum an coinne sin na h-Epiri leo & ro cotar uile d'oenlaim i l-lenmain Poimp docum an mórcatha acht oeinfer namma ed ón Apius airrig do muinntir Poimp.
I S i comairli ro smuain Apius, techt da fiarfaigid d'faidib et d'fissidib cia dona rígaib da m-biad maith no saith in coccaid moir sin, co congnad som lasin fer badh ferr conach catha dibh.
I S i conair ro coid da fiarfaigid sin, co cert medón in domuin ed ón co tempul Apaill i sléib Paruais.
I S e freccra fuair la bansaccairt Apaill, co b-fuigbed a din ar guasachtaib in catha moir sin, & co m-biad cumsanadh on coccad dó i n-glinn an t-slesa Eboecda.
I S edh rucc-som as sin co n-gebad rige i tir na h-Eboi.
Arai ni h-ed sin boi de iter, acht antan boi-sium for in muir Eboecda ic saichthin in tire, tainic ainbtine mor do, cu ro brised a longa & cur' baided e fein, gur rucc an tonn muiride a corp docom tire, & co ro h-adhnacht e i coimglind tire na h-Eboi, curo comalladh faistine Apaill amlaidh sin.
Conid remscél do remscélaib catha moir na Teasaile co n-icci sin.
Aided Aip ainm an sceoil sin.
Echtra Cessair.
C EI N bas icc gnim na mórchaingen sin in cach aird bai Cesair icc gabail na h-Espaine & iarthair in domuin, co tarnacair leis, & co ro riarsat uile e, & co tancatar i tocustal in morcatha.
Tainic reimi iarum a crichaibh na h-Espaine do breith a slog leis i n-diaid Poimp do cosnam airthir an domuin fris.
Do bertsat a milid dilsi frithbert amnus do-som annsin, ar ro triallsatt impodh fair, & do coidh doraith occo a facbail uile, ar romed les a saethair catha & ar lagat a tuarustail.
Ba foruallach a freccra na fer sin o Cesair.
Araisin ro fostait co firglic leisium iat, & o ro cindsett airisium ro dedlad friu lucht tuscairnte na comairle & auctair in deilighthi & inn impoid, & ro dicennait i fiadnaisi Cesair for lar in longphuirt.
La sodain o ro daingnigh Cesair a shluagha ro cuir Antoin reme, tuisech da muinntir & forgla a sloigh leis, & ro forcongair forra co ristais isin decmadh lo co cathair Brundais for bru in mara Adriateccda inn imel tuaiscertach tire Letha, & asbert friu guro tinoiltis cucu na h-uile longa fogebtais for sruth Idauir & for sruth Tara & for trágaib cathrach Leuca & cathrach Sip & for cuanaib in mara Adriateccda uile i comfochraib slébi Gargain, co m-betis ellma inmara urlama occo d'asccnam in marae Adriatecda estib do cosnam na Greicce & in airthir fri Poimp.
Eisim fein immorro tainic don Roim co n-uathadh da miledaib immailli fris, gur ros-oirdnestair fein é fein i n-uilib ceimennaip cadais na Roma o decan co dictatoir.
Tainic as-side co h-ardchathraigh aili na h-Etaili ed ón co h-Alba Longa, guro forbtig inte uili ada a consulacta amal ba gnáth.
Tainic as-sidhe co cathair Brundais i coinni Antoin cona muintir.
Ni tancatar side immorro in ellma sin iter co cathair Brundais.
Ba h-eimilt la Cesair a n-urnaide ann.
I S fair deisid leis iarum, tuc a coblach for in muir Adriateccda, & ro asccna cona slógaib gur' gab cuan & caladphort isin Epir i crichaib na Greicce Moire.
In Epir isin cennadhach isin Greicci.
Is di as ainm Canonia.
Is fria at-berar Molosiam.
Is inti bai in senad Romanach & Poimp antan sain.
Tainic Cesair dano i tír annsin, & do suidhigh a longphort ann oinech i n-inchaibh do longphort Poimp itir sruth n-Genais & sruth Aipi.
Is i sin cetchrich in ro comraicset a l-longphorta 'ar maidm sida ettorra, & ba h-e imfoicsi i m-batar i l-longphort co cluinedh cach dip glor araile & co faiced cach fer araile i cechtar na da longphort.
I S ed ro fairigh an cath annsin, Antoin cona miledaib gan torrachtain docom Cesair.
Ba snim & ba deinmne mor la Cesair gan na sloig sin do torachtain in a docom.
Ro faided litri & scribenna uad docom Antoin do spraic fair & da etarguide co tisedh co h-ellam cona slógaib leis docom in catha.
Ba h-ed annso tothacht na scribenn sin ed ón ‘Timmarnad bethad & imcomarc slainte o Cesair, o rig in domain, da tuisech tairisi & da muintir dilis ed ón do Antoin cona miledaib.
A Antoin,’ ol Cesair, ‘cidh imma fuirgi na Fathi & in conach? aras urlamh go maith duin acht co tisaid-si cuccainn.
Ni docair duit taidecht co h-ellam im dail.
Ni i n-Affraic no i n-Espain no i n-inadaip imciena in domain atu accut tobuch no accat tinnenus, acht is a crichaib comfoicsi na h-Etaili inn imfocraib dam can tir coccaid, gan muir n-guasachtaig ettrainn.
Tabair do th' aire nach edh asslaigmit fort, tect i n-dail cathae 'nar n-eccmais fein, acht atam acut togairm do taidecht linn docom an catha & meisi fein remut i n-dail in catha.’
‘I S ingnad an ni fil ann ed ón meisi do taidecht i crichaib mo bidbad gan eccla form & atar-linn is oman lat-su taidecht im longphort-su.
Ale, na tairmisc cid dom muintir fein tidecht im docom, ar masi an aichne fein doberim-si fortu cemad ainbthen an muirro bad lainne leo saighid m'arm-sa inas anadh im eccmais.
Ni éttum can galar & can accaine ar cride do aisneis duit.
Ni comthrom ro rainn-sium an doman iter ed ón an seanadh uile & meisi & Poimp conar sochraittib isin Epir namma & in Etail uili occut-su it oenur.
Dechasu fein at masa choir amlaidh sin.’
Aitescca Cesair fri h-Antoin co n-icci sin, & ni anadh Cesair dib sin, acht na techta druim ar druim uaidh co h-Antoin.
Aráisin ni tainic Antoin fos.
Ba brisedh aiccnid mor la Cesair sin, & iss í comairle ro scrut ed ón intan tainic in tres uair don aidhchi atracht asa leabaid & tainic a oenar reimi co tráigh in mara sis, co fuair luing m-bicc ann & tetréfed rofada esti i l-lenmain do tir, & tigerna na lungae i m-bothan cumang curcallacda for ur an trágha.
Benais Cesair beim bascraind i n-dorus in tige sin.
Frisccart tigerna mesarda in tige dó, Amiclas a ainm.
‘Cia dusces an trat-sa sinn?’
for Amiclas, ‘cia sailes nach maith uainn?
Ni fil toisc nach duine frinn mana tisedh nach combaiteach do tuinn no do carraic cuccunn.’
I Ss edh sin asbert, & atract asa leabaid & ro cuir refead lasamain fon coccladh, & ro fursainn í, & ro oslaic in dorus re Cesair can oman can imeccla fair.
I S follus maithus & nemsnimh na bethadh mesarda as sin.
Air ge ro batar longphorta slog in domain i n-athfoccus don tigh-sin, ni ro lae tigerna in tige i snimh no i n-deithitin, uair ni rabattar cruidh no innmassa occo.
Tainic Cesair isin tech 'arsin & asbert: ‘A occlaich,’ ol se, ‘as maith in turcairthe tarla cuccut da n-derna a n-abrasa frit.
Fogeba conach mor & bethaidh n-airegda occum-sa da fagbur uait a n-as ail dam.’
‘Cidh connaige form?’
for Amiclas.
‘Taidecht lim isin lunga m-bicc-si this dom imorcur i crichaib na h-Édaili,’ ol Cesair.
‘Ni sodaing anni connaigi form,’ for Amiclas: ‘air atait airdena ainbthini for in muir, & ni tarla coir na gaethi immaille frind dano.
Acht arai mata morsodethbir agut-sa bidam urlum-sa lat, amal atberat do beoil.
Ni misse nod-fuirega acht mení diultat na gaetha nó in muir tu.’
La sodain tucsat a lungu lanbic for in sal serbglas, & ro gabsat ic mallascnam in mara eocairguirm Adriatecda edir Epir & Edail.
Frith ainbthini adbul & edualang dermair de sen.
Ni frith for muir ríam etternam as guasacht bad samail don guasacht sin ed ón bith isin lunga lanbicc for in muir lanmoir.
isin ainbtini édualaing.
I S neimtim ro fuilngeadh la Cesair in guasacht mor sin cena.
I S beag ro h-ísligheadh a glor nó a aicneadh ic fulung in morgabaidh sin.
Badar for anamtaigh amlaidh sin fri re na h-aidhchi co maidin, guro cuir in tond urcur dib isin maidin muich 'arna marach ic calad na h-Eperi dorisi.
Ba samail righi can frithbert, la Cesair a cos do tadhall in tiri in uair sin.
Imsae da longphort 'arsin & Amiclas leis, & nir' scar-sen fri munterus Cesair airet ro bo béo.
Tainic raethini mor isin muir 'arsin la tosach lae.
O 'tconnairc Antoin cona slogh sin ro taithmighseat a m-barca benncaela brondfairsinga & a l-liburni luchtmura leburgorma a cuan cathrach Brundais amach, & ro gabsat ic snamhram in mara Adriatecda docom na Eperi gach n-diriuch.
Dosn-imairc in seol seach tragaib insi Lesb, gur' gabsat port i caladh na Nimpretar i crich Eperi.
O 'tcuala Poimp immorro a sloigh uili do torrachtain in áit aeninaidh docom Cesair, ba derb & ba demin leis na biadh a scarad don cur sin acht tre edergleodh catha eigin.
I S i comairli da roini iarum, in airdrighan Cornelia co righnaibh an longphuirt immaille fria do cur uadh for muir amach co h-inis Leisb fadaigh cib é diliugudh doneadh in toictiu eturru som & Cesair i l-ló in morcatha co m-beth in airdrighan & romná na rigraidhi i n-inudh inill in n-inis Leisp 'na cumsanadh.
Ro bo leasc la Poimp la Cornelia in dedail sin.
Ro bo truagh tím triamain tadiur toirseach a comhradh & a n-imagallaim in adhaigh rena scartain, gan cotlud, gan cumsanadh co m-maidin muich, gur rucsat a munter & a fiallach grada in n-airdrighan leó arna barach co h-inis Leisp, & nir' cumscaigh si asin indsi sin nogur cuireadh in cath mor.
Conid remscel do remscelaib catha móir na Tesaile co n-igi sin.
Echtra Cesair ainm in sceoil.
Aideadh Sceua.
O rancadar longphorta na righ sin i n-athfogus & i n-imfochraib d'araili, ro cuir cach dibh suil dar a sochraidi & da ronta taisbenta slogh & each & arm acco.
Ro raidseat a milidh fri Cesair teacht rompo d'argain na Greci & do gabail a mur & a caisdiall & a cathrach, & da tisadh Poimp cucu da cosnum friu no fobertais gan diceall é.
Ba nemtní la Cesair sin cena, & ro cuir seach laim gach ní acht innsaighidh Poimp, air ro-fidir da cloedh Poimp robad leis in Greic & an doman uile.
Ro ób gach comairli do berta do acht saighidh in morchuil & rochtain co fithceallacht na faithi & na toicten & gu h-oenguasacht coitcinn in domhain uili ed ón co lathair in morcatha.
Tuc iarum a catha coraighthi fon idhnaibh aigh leis re tri la diaidh a n-diaidh co saidedh a mergedha ar in ard os cinn longphuirt Poimp i n-airis catha do Poimp cona slogh.
Atberedh Poimp nach praipidi ticfadh don cath gemadh laind la Cesair é no gumbadh urlum aigi fein gnim in imairic amal bad soneirt leis.
Cesair immorro, o na fuair a frecra im cath a l-longphort Poimp, imsae cona sloghaibh do argain tiri Grec & da crothad-creachadh a dind & a cathrach & a caistiall Imsae iarum for tus docom denna Diraich, cathair sin a m-bid Pirr mac Acil i traigh in mara Ionda i n-imul na Greici.
Do landaingnib an domain uili h-i.
Aelen clochda cairrcidhe sin, & in muir Ionda do cach aird uimmi acht oen cosescrach ind namma.
Ni lama saer immorro nó saethar daenna ro daingnigh in dind sin, acht clochalla glassa gaibtheacha, & cairrci bunaidh bithbuana bennarda o tossach an domhain & o aimsir dileand do gach leith impe, gurbo annsa a togail cencombeth degslogh ica dín edir.
Ro seol Cesair a míleda tre garbacdaib doidngibh drislechaibh na Greci docom in baili sin.
O 'tcuala Poimp sin ro coid side cona sloghaibh for redib in traga laimh re muir guro coraigh a scuru & a longphorta ic dind Diraich resiu rainic Cesair ina imfochraib edir.
O ro airigh Cesair in baili do gabail do Poimp remi, ro bui ica scrutan ina menmain cissi comairli dogénad.
Rogab ic forcsi & ic fordescain in tíri uad for gach leith.
I S e smuaineadh da róni, caissel comdaingen clochda do denum leis tarrsna in tiri uile on muir co araill do gabail & d'imsuidhi for Poimp cona slogaib isinn inadh imcumung i m-bui.
Ni dumada criadh nó fót amain da ronta andsin la Cesair, acht ro tairrngit & ro teclamit cuigi clocha ocus cairrci na crich comfoccus.
Ro scailed & ro scainnred cuicci muir & morcaisléin in leithe comfocraib don Greicc uile.
Do gnither cumtach direccra dimór la Cesair dib sin ed ón artt-caisel lethan landaingen bad annsu do togail do rethedhaibh togla no don nach luithiuch scailte caislen isin domon uile.
Do ronta tuir arda & iudusu imairicc & tighe trota imda uassa tuas.
Ro claided lethanclais landomain dondara leith do on cinn co araill.
Ba h-adbul a mett in t-saethair sin.
Do gnid Poimp cona slógaib imircedha & aitherraige longphort ina medhon.
Na h-aibhne & na srotha no turcbaitis ann, boi d'fot an cumtaigh co n-dibdaitis na srotha sin & co teigtis fo talmain dorisi ina medon.
Ocus antan teiged Cesair do chuartugud in t-soethair sin ni roiced i n-oenlo on cind co araile de noco m-bidh aidce longphort i medon ind eitir a da forcend.
Ni ro cumdaighit isin domhan riemh muir bad barsamail don caisil sin.
Nir'bho menmarc itir muir na Troi no na Babiloine do cutrumugud fris.
Na bad ingnad la neach cenae in morgnim sin do rochtain la Cesair re h-edh n-athgairit, ar gerbo h-adbul an soethar robtar imda na h-oibridhe, ar boi d'imat slógh Cesair ocus do menmnaige a miled, cidh edh do berad somh monair co n-dingéntais tir shoimtechta do mhuincinn mara Torrein ota inis Seston i crich Eorpu co h-inis Abido i purt Affraici, no co tibratais in muir mór ina ruadhbuinde robartae, co n-dedladh murrusc na h-Epiri re tiribh Gregi no ciped inad isin domun bad lainn leo do chumscugud in inad bad ferr ro soised leo.
Ocus ni biadh frithbert friu imma denam.
Ro gab Cesair sosad ocus longphort i n-imfogus don daingen sin.
Ro h-ordaigit forairedha ocus lucht faircsena in cach aird don mur uathu for slógh Poimp.
Poimp, immorro, ni fitir side itir in gnim sin do denam la Cesair co tairnic a daingniugud amal bad lor.
O ro airigh immorro Poimp in m-bloigh tiri i m-boi do imsuidhe fair & do fordúnadh imbe, tucc a dirma slóigh ocus sochaide leis a h-innillib denna Diraich co n-derna srethbuidne ordaigthe ocus catha coraigthe dib laim frissin caisil, ardaig co scailte & co tanaighte slógh Cesair do gabail in caisil Ocus as e méd do ferann ro gabsatt catha Poimp 'arna corugadh uillinn fri h-uillinn re taib in caisil ed ón an meid do tir fil o imel na Roma co cathair Arictea isin Etáil, no in mét ferainn imteitt sruth Tibir o muraib na Romha co muir Torrein acht co m-badh co direch no gabadh gan filledh gan fordul ann.
I S ed a tomus coitcend sin uile ed ón da mile ar fichit do milib ceimenn, nó.

leugada ier tomus francach.
Batar muinter Cesair tra & muinnter Poimp agaid in agaid amlaid sin fri re cien, gan gnim catha no imairicc ettorra.
I S edh fotera sin, teidm galair moir ocus plaig difulaing do taidecht i l-longphort Poimp ed ón diangalar d'adhmilled a n-eachraidh for tus co n-aipiltis araill dib & a mirenna feoir ina m-beolaib & araill aile i m-medon a n-erma, co m-ba h-annsu da marcachaib a n-imdhiten forru ic tarblaing dib re h-am in tedma.
Ro lobhsatt apaighe na n-echradh isin & ro linsatt aier in tire do brentaid ocus miboladh.
Ro tuit neim an aieir truaillnide sin for uscip ocus for aibnib in tire beos, gur ro fas teidm dermair do dainib in longphuirt tre ól na n-uscedh sin ocus tre sughadh-boltnugud in aeoir.
Ba h-e dermaire in tedma co na taircedh da cairdip na mairb anapaighe d'adnacal, co m-bittis mesc ar mescc frisna beoaib i m-bothaib an longphuirt, gur' bo tormach don teidm sin beos.
Bai do teinne in tedma fo deoidh occo co m-ba h-onoir mór ocu da cairdib a cuirp do cur dar longphort immach amain.
Acht ro congain co mor leo imfoicsiu in maru doib, arro scuabsat garbgaetha in glasmara mortlaidecht ocus brentaidh inn aeoir uatha.
Ro linait na cuain doib dano do longaib cennaig 'arna linad do ilar fina ocus d'immatt gacha bidh arcenai a cennadachaiph na h-Aissia ocus ind airthir uile, cona bai terca bidh no maithiusa leo.
Slóg Cesair immorro, cen co raibe teidm galair forta, dos-fainic teidm nar'bo sodhnge d'fulang ed ón in gorta ar scithlim a l-loin uata, ocus dano ni tanccatar guirt in tire ina n-aipche fein beos doibh.
Ni ro fhétsat dano crecha no airccne do denam i ciana, acht bith ic coimet in daingin ocus icc imsuidhi for slógaib Poimp.
Ocus ba h-e met an gortai co m-bittis ic coimhithi in feoir ocus in duleabaid immaille fria a n-echradhaibh fein ocus co m-bittis ic tomailt na luibhi n-anaichintae na ranccatar miessai daennai reimi sin riem.
Arai sin ni ro fagsatt a l-longphortai no a n-inadha imsuidhi ger'bo difulaigg í doib.
Poimp immorro, o tainic suntaige ocus seitreacas da slógaib ar n-dul an tedma uathib, is i comairli do roine, an tir imchumhaing i m-boi d'faccbail ocus fobairt in caisil do ronadh da imsuidhi.
Dia fris tra is inrigh do ronadh in fobairt sin la Poimp, ar ni i taidhe folaigh no i n-dorcaib ciach no aidque do ronadh í, acht i fiadnaisi a bidbad i midmedon in laei.
Nir'bo mied leis techt for sligid ele dar in caisel, acht tre sleghaib ocus tre claidhmhibh a namat ar n-dith a curadh ocus ar cur a n-air. ara aisin ro bai occ togha in inaid bad ussu dó d'fobairt isin caisiul.
I S fair deisid occo a fobairt ic caistellaib Minuic.
Ro dírigh iarum co follus a dirma slog & sochaide leis ina cathaib cengailti cobsaidhe coraigte docom an inaidh sin don caisiul.
Ro seinnit a sturgana & a cuirn comhairc ocus a n-adurca furfoccra ocus a cuislendai cathai ind aeinfecht ocus a n-aenfabhall.
Tuccad úarduscadh namat leo for lucht coimeta ind inaid sin don caisil.
Do cotar sidhe focetoir for a n-iudusaip debtha ocus for a toraibh trota.
Ro gabsat ic fordescain in muighi uathu, co facatar cucu na meirgedha aille eitteacha ocus na h-onchonu obeli ocus na delbae aquili ocus na bratacha srollda os na slegaib ocus na muighe lanu do scellbolccaib scieth ocus do dairib slegh ocus d'feraib armtha.
Ro truinset som & ro traighsett deiside.
Ros-lin bidgad bais ocus aduath ecca conar' bo h-eiccin da m-biodbadhaib a n-airm d'imbirt forro.
Ro comfoiccsigset slóigh Poimp don caisiul, ocus tuccait caindli ocus locarna giusta for derglasadh fo cosoip fulaing na n-iudus ocus na tor troto, co m-batar for crith ocus utmailli ic tuitim fri lar, conar' h-anadh re díbhraccad no re h-imbualad intip.
Ranccattar muinter Poimp for mullach in caisil iarsin, co facattar edh a forccsi don tir moir uatha for cach leith.
Acht ata ni chena, in t-inad nar' chosnatar in mile buidhén, & ina m-boi do muintir Cesair uili ann dano ro sluag Poimp, ro cosain aen occlaech do muintir Cesair sin, ocus do roini a aenar a n-imforcraid maithisae uile. arincein boi-sium ina sesom, ocus a airm for congbail ina laim, nir' leicc duini do slog Poimp secha, & ro tairmiscc a cosccur im Poimp fein.
Sceua a ainm in occlaigh sin, ocus milid togaide do Románchaip fein in fer sin, ocus gaisccedach geslach é, ocus boi i g-coimitecht Cesair amal gach milidh isin t-sluagh nogo rainic Cesair do gabail aittrebthaide srotha Rotain i crichaib Gaillia fecht n-aill.
Doroini Sceua calma mor ic gabail na cinedh sin, & ro cinn forsna miledhaib bai ina farradh uile no gur' giallsat na cineda do Cesair.
Do ronadh iarsin tuiseach cett ic Cesair deisiom, ocus bai ina langradoip o soin immach gan dedail fris riem gusan la-su.
Deghocclaech da tigernae fein in fer sin.
Fer tairberta é do denam cacha h-uilc ocus cacha maithiusai no furailed a thigernae fair.
Ni fitir co m-badh meste do ní da n-dingenad acht co n-erbad a thigerna friss.
O 'tconnairc in fer sin a muintir ic airimbirt teichidh re slógaibh Poimp, ro gab icca cairiugud ocus ica n-gresact co mor.
‘Cia leith imaiges in t-oman sib, a occa?’ olse.
‘I S anaichnidh do muintir Cesair cusindiu ind aiste trialltai ed ón teiched.
A mogada dochraidhe ocus a ceithri doerclanda,’ ar se, ‘is granda daib teiched do denam ocus gan for cru do todail beous.
Nach nár daib gan for cuirp d'airimh etir corpaib for n-aesa comaind ocus for commiled intan bias Cesair ic denam onora adhnaicthe duin.
Cen co n-derntai maith ar grad for tigerna no for n-einigh, tabrad cid iter in fherg foraib calma do denam, ar ro imbir Poimp tarcusal mor foirn intan ro innsaigh ind inadh i m-bamar-ne sech cech inad isin caisiul uile.’
‘Dar mo breithir cenae ni ragha in la-su ass gan todail fola a muintere-sium co h-imda ina cinaid side.
Mo cen-su bas da m-beith Cesair i fiadnaisi mo gnim.
Ni fil do conach form-sa in fer sin im fiednaisi.
Atchifi Poimp immorro i n-dingen do maith, ocus molfaid mo gnimrada intan dofaethus.
Cuiridh for n-ochta fri h-armu for namat & denaidh maith air doforficfa foirithin i n-ellma, daig atchife Cesair luaithredh na m-marcslogh & atcluinfe gaire in catha.
Doraega annsin fer ar n-digailtene ocus sind fein icc faccbail bais alainn 'ar n-denam maithesa isin chath.’
Ro eirig Sceua co ferrda annsin for mullach in iudusa, ocus ro gab for denam calmo móire.
I S cumma no diubraiced crunna ocus clocha ocus curpu ind fienlaig marbtha do mullaigibh na n-iudus ocus na tor trota i g-cennaip a bidbadh, ocus do beired idhlanga mora i n-airde, ocus no tomaithed forta co minic a leiccen fein cona armaip ina cend.
Ro gab acc srainedh araill da naimtib uad do clethaib & do cuaillip ceindbiraigti na tighe trota ocus araill aile do sabaib ocus do sonnaib ocus d'fianglassaib sithremra cona n-irellaib iairn imma cennaib.
Ro gabsatt drecta móra do muintir Poimp ic dreim fri h-uachtar na n-iudus ar sin.
Atconnairc Sceua iat ocus ro noct a claideb cruaidgér claislethan asa imtiuch bodba, ocus ro gab for imscothad a crob ocus a l-lamh diph, co tuititis ina tortib tamnaigthibh i g-cendoiph a commiled fein, co combrutis a cinnu ocus a curpu ocus a scietha ic tuitim fortha, ocus co m-bitis na craisecha comtarsnae treotha som dano.
I S cuma iarum no imscothad a l-lamha da claidib ocus no comtuaircced a cinnu ocus a cnama do clochaib ocus do cairrcib tulammais.
ocus no comloisced a fultu ocus a n-ulcha & tugen a n-gruad ocus a l-lecan do locharnaibh lasamna ocus d'aithinnib giuis ocus do beraib lethloiscctibh.
O ro eirgetur tra cuirp & apaige ind oesa marbtha co m-batar 'na carnaib & 'na n-dumadaibh dermara re taeb in caisil, cona roiched Sceua imbualadh fria bidbadha sechu no tarsu, tuccustair idlaing curadh de asin inad i m-boi, ocus ro ling co neimlesc feib as doiniu no lingfedh in leoman Affracdha dar srethgaibh sealga, co tarla ina sesom e i certmedhon catha a bidbadh.
Ro gabh ica imbirt forta asa medon 'arsin, & bai ica comthuargain ara aghthib ocus ara culaib, dia deis & dia I SS edh no saigedh gach conair i faiced tairisium fris.
Gach conair no beired a aghaidh no maidedh reimhi.
Ro bernad ocus ro formaeladh a claideb 'arsin ar cnamaib curad & ar fiaclaib fer ocus ar medhibh miledh ocus ar tulaib sciath & ar slabradaib lúirech ocus ar cir-ciomsaib cathbharr, co nach gnim claidib boi leis ocus co nach tesccad no leod no lettradh do gnidh, acht comairt ocus brúdh ocus brisedh ocus basugud.

Ro daingnigsett ocus ro dluthaigsett iatt, & tuccsat in cath cruadh inaigte a n-aeinfecht fair.
Do ronadh cath nua nemhghnathach andsin ed ón na h-ilmile acc cathugud frisan n-aeinfer.
Ro laesett uili ind oenfaball a slega fair.
Ni deachaid slegh imroill dib, acht ro ansatt uili ina curcais comaird i cnes an curadh ocus i n-drolaip a luirige.
Ni ro leicced a cend do toccbail dó 'arsin, acht ro gapadh for a essorccuin as gach aird do diubraicthiuh slegh ocas saighett & d'fuasmadaib laigen a l-lamhaib laech ocus do braithbeimendaib bidbad, co n-derna bretaig m-briste da sciath for a inchaib ocus bruara mina menbaighthe da cathbarr immá cend, & simnecha rebta & scabur-tana tollscailte da luirig imma táebu, cona bai ní ic congbail a inne nó a inathraig ann, acht an clethcur sleg seimnech sithremar batar comtharsna trena cnes.
Ba dasacht mor sleg no saighett do diubragad fair o sin suas, ar ni antais ann acht toct ina rith for slechtaiph na slegh occus na saigett aile trit.
Acht is edh ba qomhnert ocus ba coimtig doib cuicci, rethi togla, no trelam scailte múr da trasccradh, daig ba múr daingen díthoglaide eisiom dar cend Cesair ic fostad Poimp.
Ro la Sceua arsin urcor da scíath uadh & ro gab ic coimgnimh inn imairicc da deis & da cli, & a clethcur fogha faebrach comtarsna trit, conach delb doenna bai leis, act amal ba bledhmhil do torathraibh in maru é.
Bai co h-attuirseach athscith iaram ic cur neith da armaib as ocus se icc toga cia dia naimtib no indsaigfedh do comtuitim immailli fris docom bais.
Ni bai a samail intansin acht amal innester ind elifaint Affracda do beith intan diubraicther isin cath í do ilar arm, & crothaidh eiste na h-armu sin gan nach crothodhail fola na n-diaidh ar aiccnedh cnamaige bis i curp na h-eliphainti im thodail fola.
Ba h-amlaid sin do Sceua dano, air gé ro threghtaisett na h-armu a chorp ocus a cholann dianechtair, araidhe ni ro thraighedh ocus ni ro tairnedh a nert no a menma no a brigae inmedonacha trit-sin, ocus gér b' imdha sleg & saighett trit ni ro imretar uile bas fair frisin re sin beos.
I S annsin ro diubhraic occlaech do luct na Creti saiget fair.

Tairrngid Sceua an t-saigett co h-opunn asa chind ocus do bert an suil iar m-brisedh a fremh leis immach for corranaibh na saigte.
Cuiridh urchur uad for lar dib ocus do beir fuirmidh dia sail ina cenn, gur ros-folaigh fon talmain maraen.
Ni bai a samail annsin acht amal indister in mathgaman feocair do beith arna guin ocus domeil a déda frisin n-gai dia g-crechtnaigter, co cuir ina m-blogaib briste ass é.

Ni recair a les fuilled crectnaighthe form, acht na slega filet acum fulang do tarraing as mo crectaiph.
Denaidh comairle maith form ed ón taid cucum & beirid me i m-bethaidh libh i l-longphort Poimp, gurbo deismirecht im impod for Cesair la cach impodh damh-sa fair & riarugud Poimp dam re n-ecc.’
Ro creit ócláech maith do sainmuintir Poimp sin, bái for a inchaibh isin cath.
Aulus a ainm in occlaigh sin.
Tainic Aulus cuicci da breith cona armaibh leis.
Tucc-somh fuasmad da claidib fair, co tarla i m-bun a thengadh, gur' gabh a chuilfeite trít.

‘Gach aen shailis mo tigerna do treccad dam-su,’ ar se, ‘ticced i l-le co tuccur in diach-su fair.
Madh ail do Poimp sidh d'faghbhail on claidib-su, leiccedh a mergeda fri lar ocus slectad do Cesair.
As deimin na fuigbhe mo sid-sae fris-sin adiu.
Inne for n-aiccned fein ro sailsiupair ocum-su, a muinter Poimp?’ arse.
