La sodain atconncutar muinter Poimp tromnellgal mor & luaithred ceo dermair os cennaiph slogh darsan mag ina n-docom.
Atar-leo ba h-e Cesair cona buidnib tainic ann.
Ro maeladh forra-sumh a h-inadh inn imairicc desidhe, & ro faccsat ait na scainnre do Sceua.
Atrochair Sceua 'arsin o ro tairinn a ferg ar scuchadh a bidbad uadha, & ro scar a ainim fria corp, ocus nir'bo bas ar midlachus sin, acht ba bas ar gnimaib gaile ocus laechdhachtae, damad d'escairdibh cetamus no berad cosccur ocus manbadh ic gnim imairicc in catha cathurda fogabad bas.
Ruccad a chorp la a muintir 'arsin, ocus ro bensat armu a bidbad asa thaebaib, & ro idhbrattar a arm-somh fein do Mairt ed ón do dea in cathae.
Ge ro maeladh tra for slógh Poimp don leith sin ni moiti ro tairis don cathugud beos, amal na scithaighter in muir mor cidh formaelad do bertar for ni da tonnoip o beinn cairrcci no o slis alla no airdshleibe, ar ni tairis in muir do grés ica tuarccain da tromtonnaib cidh cian connicce.
Ba h-amlaid sin dano do Poimp icc togail in caisil sin, ar tainic roime docom an daingin boi i forba in caisil i fochair in mara ic muintir Cesair.
Ro ordaigh slógh lanmor i l-longaib icca togail, & a coisidhi ocus a marcslog for tir, & ni ro an de noco n-derna cathbernadha comlaithre mora and, & co rucc a sloga uile tar-su isin mag mor.
Rob anmesardha ro scailitt na slóigh sin fon magh ar n-dul dar in caisil immach amail as deiniu, & as anmesardha scailis tuile srotha Paid dar a bruachaibh co lethann dar na crichaib comfaicsib.
Cesair immorro ni fitir side in n-imairecc sin do denamh itir noco tairnic a gnim & co tuc aichne for in teine caismberta ro h-arladh icc lucht in coimeta ar n-dul do Poimp cona slogaib dar in caisil immach.
Tainic-sium reimi fo cetoir co h-airm ar'harlad in teine ocus atconnairc na clíathbernadhae mora oslaicte ocus slichtlorg na slóg ocus na muir 'arna muradh.
Ocus atconnairc dano longphorta Poimp co subhach sidamail for reidibh in maige ina fiadnaise.
Ba brisedh mor menman ocus aiccenta do-som in cumsanadh sin do beith for Poimp.
Nir' léicc a ferg do ernaidhe re a slogha gan fobairt longphuirt Poimp, ar ba fo laiss cidh ár no láthe for a muintir acht combuaidredh na failtedha ara batar isna longphortaib.
Imsae ieram cusin uathad sloigh tarrusair maraen fris i m-mulluch longphuirt Torquait bai i comfoccus do focetoir, tuisech maith do muintir Poimp eside.
Tinoilis Torquait a muintir i n-aeininadh fo cetoir la h-airiugud Cesair cuige amal as deiniu ocus as neimleiscce no tinoilfitis n-aeireada seolbrata a long ic airiugud guasachta muiride ina comfoccus nó icc soadh gaithe forru.
Ni mo innás dar muraiph longphuirt Torquait innunn ráinic Cesair intan ro rathaigset luct mórlongphuirt Poimp e.
Ocus ro eirig Poimp 'arsin & ro doirt na catha cengailte coirigthe druim ar druim d'foiritin Torquait.
O ro airigh Cesair sin ro impo co h-opunn a l-longphort Torquait immach, ocus ic sodh dó is edh dos-rala cusin uathadh bai ina farradh i g-cend na cath i m-boi Poimp.
Ro lin omhun ocus imoccla ocus cridenbás mór a muintir-sum desidhe icc aisgin in anforlainn ocus inn étualaing adbuil ed ón ilcatha Poimp ina n-agaid chuca ocus luct longphuirt Torquait ina cathais coirigthi for a I S i comairli do ronsatt iarum, gan fobairt in anforlainn iter, acht tanccatar ina reimim & ina techtae eissiumail laim frisna cathaib imach.
Ocus robtar lanbuidhig do rochtain a n-anmann leo in drong nar' mudaigedh diph.
Ba deithbhir doib-siumh on cena, ar da leicced Poimp da miledhaib slan a claideb d'imbirt forra somh no biadh scur for in cath catharda tre bithu ocus ar na h-uile olcaibh ro asatar isin Roim trit on lo sin amach.
Ocus amae nir dichait esbaid muintire Cesair iter ge ro coiccled dhoiph, ar ro tuitsett ed ón ar mili laech & da cenntuir ar fhichit dhibh isin fobairt sin o tus co deredh.
I S ed tuc for Poimp in coiccill sin do tabairt doibh, ar ba dimbag leis na cinedha comaighthe d'faicsin ic básugud na Roman ina fiadhnaisi, ocus nir b' ail leiss dano a catha do scailedh co dicra for in m-becc slóig sin, o nar shail Cesair ettarra, ar ba deimin leis na tiucfad Cesair la h-uathad miledh da fobairt-sium dogrés.
Tainic Poimp iarum reime da longphort co subhach somenmnach ar m-breith do an coscuir sin do Cesair.
Conadh remscel do remscélaib cathae móir na Tesaili co n-icce sin.
Imairecc na h-Epiri & Aided Sceva ainm in scceoil sin.
Tuaruscbail na Tesaili.
Cesair immorro, o ro airigh in n-anfen mór ocus in duaibsighe do ralae do ocus da shlógaib isna muigib sin na h-Epiri & denna Diraich, is i comairle do roine, in tir sin uile d'fagváil ocus tir aile d'innsaigid dus in badh ferr a chonach catha indte.
Imsae iaram cona slógaibh leis guro ordaigh a scuru ocus a longphortae for clarmaigib tire na Tesaile allanair.
Ó 'tcuala Poimp sin ro tinoilit a righ ocus airrigh ocus maithe a slóigh cuicce do denam comairle cinnus do genad.
Is i comairle do bertsatt dho, o ro tubastar Cesair, techt d'innsaigidh na Roma ocus na h-Ettaile, uair na raibe sluagh bidbad ic a gabail fris.
‘Acae om,’ ol Poimp, ‘ni dingén-sa in comairle sin iter.
Ni rag-sa dogréss docom na Roma amail do coidh Cesair.
Ni faicfither mo dul-sa di tre bithu acht ar lecon mo shlóigh da tiribh ocus ar cor cestu an morcatha dim.
Damad ail dam-su cathugud ar lar na Roma ni tiucfainn eiste amal tanac.
Ni ceist lim-su cena mo dul fein gusin Scitia tuaiscertaigh no cusin teintidhe fo deas, acht co m-badh adhbhar cumsanta ocus sídha don Roim.
Inn edh ba coimtig dam-su ann side in tan isam coscrach toct do denam coccaid isin Roimh & me do teichedh eiste fecht aile ar daigh na beith eccumsanadh coccaidh innti.’
O tairnic do inn aisneis sin ro seol a mergedha rena slógaib dar sleibtib na Candavi sair gach n-direch, gar' gab sosadh ocus longphort isin Tesail i n-aeintir fria Cesair.
Ba h-adbor ugra ocus ba damna margliad sin, ar as annsin ro cinnset na faithi in cath mor do tabairt.
Ni do tuarusccbail ina tire sin na Tesaili do bertar sisana colleicc.
Tri h-anmanna atat 'ca sloinded fon domun furre Emathia ainm di, o Emathas, ri maith ro gab fuirri fecht n-aill.
Parsalia ainm aili dhi, o Parsalos, sencathair uasal fil innti.
I N Tesail immorro a h-ainm bunaidh, tír daingen dodaing olc ainmin accarb imdorcha innill in tir sin, ocus carracbenna sliaph n-urard n-imaimreidh impi da gach leith ed ón sliab Peil ettorra ocus in turccbail samrata.
Sliabh Oiss allanair ettorra ocus in turcbail geimretta, co nach taitnit ruithne greine innte i tosach nach lae isin bliadain.
Sliab Exrim allaness di ettarra ocus tes n-greine.
Sliabh Point allaniar di etorra ocus in fuinedh, cona taitnit ruithne greine innte i n-deredh nacha laithe tre bithu.
Sliab Olimp don leith atuaidh ettorru & in t-uarda.
In lucht aittrebait fo taibh deiscertach in t-sleibe sin, ni benand in gaeth atuaidh friu, & ni faicet in seachtarréte tre bithu.
As becc réa don lo taitnes in grian innti sech na slebte aile atrubartmur.
Tír arar' digbait renna in lae & na h-aidci amlaid sin, ba cubaid in cath mor do gnimh indte.
Atát cathrachae imdha isin tír cétna sin ed ón cathair Parsalos i m-bai Aicil mac Peil, ocus cathair Philcce, as innti side ro cumtacht in Airg ed ón an long i n-deachaid Iason mac Essóin arceann in crocainn orda co h-inis na Colach.
I S innte atá cathair Teleos & cathair Dorion & cathair Tracci & cathair Pretio--da cathraigh Hercuil maic Ampitrionis sin--& cathair Melibeus--is inte-sede ro foilgitt saigde Hercuil 'arna ecc--& cathair Larissa & cathair Argos--is innte sede ro ben Agaue a chend da aenmac fein ed ón do Peint.
Tir i n-dingénta olc mar sin, ba cubaidh in cath mor do gnim innte.
Atat srotha imdha & aibhni adhuathmara isin tir-si fos.
As dib-side sruth Eas, & sruth Inaich & sruth Achiloin forsatat insi Eichnidh, sruth Maill & sruth Speirch, sruth Amprissos & sruth Anauir, sruth Aspidain & sruth Eniph, sruth Asoip & sruth Pheula, sruth Melax, sruth Tituros & sruth Péin.
I S edh innisit senchaidhe na Tesaili conadh a sruth Stig i n-ifern theprines bunadh an t-srotha sin.
Tir i snighfedh an sruth sin ba cubaid an cath mar do gnim innte.
Atait popail indha anaichenta dano isin tir sin ed ón popul na m-Bebricda & popul na Lelegitam, popul na n-Eolda & popul na n-Dolopecda, popul na Magnecdha & popul na Mineta, popul torathardha na Centauri & na n-Ech-cumusccda ed ón each & duine a cummascc aenpersainne inntip.
Ba dib sidhe dano na h-Each-cumasccda airdirce ed ón Monica eningnech & Retheas rocalma.
I S eside no tairngedh na crunna fa h-airde isna cailltip cona fremaibh a talmain ocus no telgedh urcar a riara dhibh.
Ba dib Neis centauir dano.
Is esside ro triall comrac ar eiccin re mnaei Hercuil, ocus abhand etturra & Ercuil, cur ro marb Hercuil do urcur shaighti é dar abainn innund.
Ba dib dano Ciron centauir, aide Aichill maic Peil.
I S amaid fuathaighit na h-asdrolacdha a deilb-somh isin firmimint nemda & boga co saigitt innilte fair ina laim for comhair renna Scoirpi immach amail no beith ica guin.
Tir i n-geinfitis na torathair sin ba cubaid an cath mor do gnim innti.
Isin tir sin na Tesaili ro artraigset dano sila & adbair in catha & in coccaid for tús riemh.
Is innti amh ro riadad ech for tus, & tuccad srianglomur ina beolu, & ro coidh marcach fair.
Is innte do ronadh long ocus lestur in mara for tus riamh do sirthain in domain ocus na crich n-ectrann n-anaichnidh estibh.
Itonas dano, ri Tesaile aicce ro bervadhlegad mein oir ocus argait for tus i tinnib, ocus as leis ro h-ordaighedh monadh peinginne re creic ocus re cundradh for tus riem.
Is innti dano ro taiscced & ro cistigeadh ór & indmas for tus.
Isin Tesaili cetna dano ro genair in nathair neimnech airdirc ed ón Pithon, curro folmaigh & curro diláithrigh rempi an doman no curo marbh Apaill mac Ioib Is innte ro tusmit clannmaicne Aloe torathair ed ón Zethus ocus Epialtes cona m-braithrib.
Tri bassa a bisech som fein ar gach lo.
Cubat lamha immorro & bas forbairt cach maic da macaiv re gach mís, curro lin dimus ocus ardmenma iat, conadh í comairle ro lúaidsett sleipte in domain do corugud os cinn araile, ocus toct d'innsaigid nime ocus a ríghi do gabail, co ro mudaigit do saignenaibh teintidib iett ic triall in morsaethair sin.
Tír i n-geinfittis na moruilc sin ba cubaid an cath mór do gnim innti.
Conadh remscel do remscelaib catha moir na Tesaile co n-icci sin.
Tuarusccbail na Tesaile ainm in sceoil.
Faistine ind arrachta a h-ifern.
O ro ordaighset na dá airdrígh sin ed ón Poimp ocus Cesair, cechtar a da mórlongphort for lar aentire na Tesaili, ba cinnte & ba deimin la slógu in domuin uile batar ina farrad na dedeltais asind imforrain gan cath, & tucsat uile da n-uidh & da n-aire gorbo comfochraibh comfocus doib uair na h-etrana & in deiligthe, & trath scuir saegail na sochaide & aimser in guasachta romoir ed ón la in morcatha.
Ro ardaigit & ro tennait & ro daingen-toccbait aiccentae saerclann, & menmanna miled occo som de sin i fúr in catha Ro trasccrait immorro & ro truinit & ro tairnit, ro crithnaighit & ro utmallaigit menmandae muadhlaech & midlach & daesccursloig docineoil re cridhenbas in catha & re h-uathgrain inn imbualta & ar eccla an bais.
Morthúr & scrutain & smuained snimach sodeithbir & comairle ciulanach ro túrsit menmanna na slog sin isna h-aidhchibh resin cath.
Mac ro bai icon airdrig, ic Poimp, isin longphort, Poimp Sext a ainm in maic.
Is i comairli ro greis in t-oman fair, toct da iarfaigid d'fathib & d'fisidib cinnus no bhiadh digleodh in catha moir, ocus cia dona airdríghaibh forsmbadh raen é.
Ni do tempul Ioib no Apaill no dei aile no bandei ro cuaid Poimp Sext d'fiarfaigidh na scél sin.
Ni do taisceltaib rend no retlann no reatha saighnen no gotha én ro iarfaigh iat, ar ro sail a fhis cinnte d'fogbail o bandruidib in tire i m-boi ed ón o ammaitib na Tesaili. arba comfochraib comhfocus do morlongphort ro battar a cathracha & a caisteoil.
Ba h-adamra ingnathach immorro a cerd & a n-elada na m-bandruad Tesaltai.
Ni bidh isin domun ni torathardha na faillsightis a n-demna doib & gach ni ba h-ingantae ocus ba dícreidmiche ina cele is edh ba h-ealada doib. arbatar linmaire lossae neimnecha & luibe denma draidechta isin tir sin na Tesaili ina i tiribh in domuin o sin ammach. arintan táinic in bandrai airderc Medea ingen Eta rí na Colach la h-Iassón mac Essóin isin Greicc, & prímammait in domain isidhe, ar ai fuair a h-imarcraid ammaitechta & tincetla druadh & luibe neime i tir na Tesaile.
Na h-inadha isin cruinde dano in ba gnaitchiu elada draidechta do denamh ed ón cathair Mempis, & tir Egipte, in Babiloin & cricha na Callacda, do gnithe an imforcraidh sin uile acc na h-ammaitib Tesaltaibh, ar no imbritis a m-brechta druadh forna duilibh domunda cona leicctis a richta fein forra.
No fotaightis in aidce & nó cumbrigtis an la amal no rictis a les.
Ni leicctis in n-aer no in firmimint ara cummus fein, ar no fostatis an firmimint da rith domunda antan ba toil doib.
Do bertis torne & ainbtine isin aer & neolla braenachu & fordorcha dar grein isin aimsir ba soilsi a saighnenrad & ba reli a ruithne.
No scailtis na niullu & na tola tromfertana intan ba h-aidbli iat.
Do bertis tonngail & ainuthen aran occian ar lar na feithciuine.
No tairmmiscctis na tonna dano & no isligtis in ainbhthen intan ba gairvi in gaeth for in muir.
Do bertis na longa for lainseoladh i certagaidh na gáithe for in muir.
Do gnitís marbhucht tairismech dona buinnibh garba folcmara fograchaib & dona srothaib rotrenaibh riathordaibh.
Do gnitis clarmhuige coimreidhe dona slebtibh ro-ardaib.
No íslightis sliav Olimp co n-artraightis na neoill uasa.
Ingnad mor esidhe, ar ata do airde slebe Olimp co fil a uactar & a forcleithi osin aeor fuasnaidhe suas & conid foi taitnit na neoill tre bithu.
In fer teit oentadall ina mullach ni cluinenn ni iter ina diaidh 'ar m-buaidredh a eistecta la blosctorman retha na n-airdrennach & la fogarmuirn na firmimint ic impodh.
Do gnítis na h-ammaite cetna snechta na Scitia do scailedlegadh i n-uacht in geimrid gan tes greine no teinedh do beim friss.
Do gnittis in lan-mara d'impodh for culu i n-agaid neirt inn occiain & inn éscai.
Do gnitis moil nemcumsccaicthe in talman do cumscugud co faicthe 'na rith ima cuairt Do bertis fordorchu for dreich éscai co n-urailtis co h-eiccnech fair comfaicsiugud do talam co faisctis a druct & a uanfadh tremit for feraibh nemhidibh in tire do dhenamh a n-ilcerd n-draidhechta diph.
Cidh fil ann tra acht cach anmanna isin domun uile doneoch ercoitiges do duine, eter leoman & mathgaman & loiscenn & tigir & viper & colubir & nathir neimide arcena, no bidh eccla na n-ammaite sin & na n-urtrach forra, & ni fognadh ni doib todail a n-neimhi ina n-agaid, ar ba feochra & ba demhnacdha neime na Tesalta inas neimhe cach anmanna dibh.
Gerba h-imda tra ammait aingidh ica h-adradh isin ealadhain sin i tir na Tesaile, ro bai aen ammait ann ro derrscaigh dibh & da tabratis uile aitite & uaisle.
Scairb caillighi fesguirmi forgrainne isidhe, Erictó a h-ainm, sai ammaitechta Do gnítis airci druadh & brechta nua uaith fein ar cach lo.
No teghedh-si a n-iffern & i m-bruigibh srotha Stig & i teghdaisib Pluton rí iffirn gach tan ba tol dhi.
Is ann no bid a h-aite & a h-aittrebh & a leabaidh lighe, i scailpibh carrac & inn uaim-tollaibh talman & ina adhnaicthibh marbhhh.
Ni tathaigedh-si airecht no cathraigh nó aitedha daenda eistibh sin, acht mana thisadh in dorcha ciach no fertana nó aidhce.
Do teglaim & do thinol a l-luibe neimneach & a trelamh n-druadh fona crichaibh batar comfoicsi dhi, & in gort airthe for a saltradh-si intan sin, nó in t-achad can ar, ni ásadh a fer no a n-arbar fri re cian ina dhiaidh.
Ni cuingedh ni d'faistine tre bithiu acht o demnaib iffirn.
Do gnitis sidhe a frecra lasin cétbricht fochetoir, & ni lamtais urnaide in aithbrechta uaitho iter.
Mor n-gnimh n-adéittigh do gnidh an t-arracht sin isin tir i m-boi.
Intan no bitho icc losccud na marbh i comfoccus di, ticced-si cucu co tinoiledh cnamha a n-apaige & luaithredh na corp & sméróiti tuthmura in tellaigh le, & no tairrnghedh na h-aithinne a lamaib na tustighthe no bittis icc losccudh cuirp in mairbh beos.
In fail i fagbadh dano na curpu rena losccud inn eturbaegul fora fuataib no tairrngedh da meraib a suile a cloiccnib, & no tesccadh-scomadh da fiaclaibh a n-ingne dibh, & no beredh utlach-brossnada mora do slisnib na fuat le.
No gabad corpu na crochairedh asa crochaib isin aidhche, no tesccadh da fiaclaib snadmann na n-gad & na n-goistedh no bitis ica fostadh ina crochaibh.
No bhidh si ic creim & icc scripadh na croch leo da h-ingnibh & da fiaclaibh.
Fecht ann no bid-si ar banganaigh a cuirp in crochaire & a fiacla i l-lenmain ina feithib & i cenglaib a cuirp, & in corp no bidh can onoir adnaicte fair isin crich as tuscu ro soicedh-si cucce inat allta & ethaitte in tire.
Araidhe ni imred-si lamha fair no co reptais na maic tire & na h-allta é, & co tinoiledh-si a m-mirenda lethcoccantae asa m-braightibh le.
Intan ba h-adhailc di fuil daine m-beo dochom na draidechta, teged-si isna cathaib & isna h-ergalaibh co m-bidh ic frithailimh na fola a crectaib na fer re síu no siled a cru for lar.
No tairrngedh dano a naidhena becca beoa tre bronntaeba na m-ban torrach immach.
Intan dano na fagbadh apaige urlamha fria less no mharbadh fein daine di.
Ni h-immirthe for duine earnail bais na h-imred-si fortha.
No spelad i fultu & i n-ulcu cona laim clí dib intan bitis na daine ic éc.
Intan téighed cara di bas ticcedh-si docom a cuirp co m-bidh acc poccad a bhall.
No foslaiccedh craes in mairb 'arsin, & no bidh ic coccnamh a thengadh, & no canadh a bricht druadh ina brágait, co n-dernadh tectuirecht ettarru & demna iffirn.
Mor dho gnimradaib doidngibh duaibseachaibh aili nach airmither sund do roine in uathammait & in t-arracht Tesalta sin ed ón Ericto, isna tirib examlaib i m-bid.
O 'tcuala mac in airdrig ed ón Poimp Sext, in caillich n-duaibsigh sin do beith i c-comfoccus do, tainic trath medoin oidce asin longphort immach da h-iarraid, & uathadh do tairisib a muintire immaille friss.
Ro gabsat 'ca túr & 'ca h-iarraidh i n-uamtollaib talman & i r-relgib idhol in tire, co cualatar a garbdordan i scailp cairrci i n-ucht slebi Eimh os cinn cathrach na Parsali suas, & si ic denam tairmisc annsin na ructais na dei adarta in cath mor ocus immargal na da n-airdrigh ed ón Poimp & Cesair, dochom tire aili uaithi-si immach, ar nir' sáil a daethain do corpaib rig & d'apaighib saerchlann d'fagbail co brath acht mana fagbad isin oengliaidh sin coar' tinoilit ilcinela in talman.
Arai tra ro lin a menmain & a h-aiccned uile saint fogbala cuirp Poimp & cuirp Cesair co tuccad in diach & inn imlot bad laind le fein fortha.
Tainic iarum mac in airdrig cona muintir da saigid, & atconncattar ina h-arracht áightige aduathmar i n-ucht na cairrci.
Ba granna in turcairthi atconncas annsin, in ammait aingidh Ericto Tesalta, edón Caillech dhochraidh doidelbda dicoll, os i cael corr cruaidrengach.
Aghaid glasban etlaide inalcaille le, co cuirri gruaide, co tuilli oile, co luimi lecon.
Glennshuili locliatha linnaca ina cinn.
Sron cuasach, cicar, croimremur, tulgorm, tanaidhe, urchrom, urgranna aice.
Blaescbheol duvglass duaibhsech firuathmar fodrecda le.
Garbeccur grainemail do birfiaclaibh barrglassa bunodra i cechtar a da drant.
Mong roliath roinnidi na scuaip aimreidh forscailte imma cend.
Lama lacremra litarrda aice.
Cruib garbae glaissfethacha leo.
Meoir cromma ceindremra for a garbglacaip.
Ingne aithgéra odurbhuidhi in seabaic fortha.
Medon crapach cuislennach aici.
Sliasta accaelae ibraide, & da glun garba glicurda le.
Da coiss colpthae fiarcamma finnfadacha fotha.
Da lethansluasait delecha forméracha ica fulang.
Grainniu delbaibh domuin a taidbred.
Mesu isí fein inas a forcsi.
‘Rot-bennachat do dei adurtha,’ for mac inn airdrígh.
Tincais in caillech co forniata fair & ni freccart iter é.
‘Dot accallaim tancammair-ne, a deigben út, ar atcualamur conadh molad ocus conad maissi do mnaib na Tesaili uile do geineamain-siu dib, & atcualamur dano co ticc dit remhaisneis cach neith ticfa isin domun; ocus cach ni as ail let do thairmisc dano, ni leicci a torractain immonair tre bithiu.
Bennacht fort, aisneid duinn scur in catha moir-si trialltar sunn.
Bidh a fis occot, ni drochhduine sires fort anni-sin, acht mac airdrigh in domuin ed ón Poimp Sext mac Poimp Maige.’
‘Bídham tigerna fer an domain da ternar & m'athair co cosccrach asin cath. ann do faeth-sum dano; bid am croaidh-si for a uile fhorb da eis, & as maith do neoch mo command amlaid sin.
Is mór traethus mo menmain cenae gan scur deimin in catha d'fis damh, & amae as maith a fulang occom cidh drochcelmaine atcluinim asa loss.
Acht is ed aenni ierrmait fortsu, na tí duin olc na h-innessa dun rena torrachtain.
Furail for na deib nemdha a n-innisin duin, nó coiccill doib side & asslaigh for demnaib ifrinn inn aisneis dun.
Furail for in Écc fein tidhact a h-ifern da foillsiugud deit cia slogh uainn as imforcraide beras leis docom ifirn don cur-sa, uair atacumang-sa sein uile.
Cidh mor saethor sin dano as dingmala do degmhnai mar tusa a snim do tabairt fris.’ tra acht ro taitin co mór fri h-Ericto cloistecht a cluaighthe & a h-airrderccaighthe amlaidh sin, & ro gab coir comraid frisin n-gilla, co n-ebert:
‘I S fir, a occlaig,’ for Ericto, ‘in dara ni ro tomaithissi duinn ed ón co fil remfis na todocaide do leire linn.
As doigh da m-bdais mincaingne foilli fodhalta doberta-sa cuccainn do genainn-si a tairmesc re h-ed eiccin.
In caingen lasa tancais immorro ed ón etergleod in morchatha-sa Poimp & Cesair, ro cinnset na faithi & na dei adartha & in toictiu sein cian mór uadh, & as daingen dicumsgaighthe ata etergleod in morcatha-sa oca arna ordughud co cobsaidh cinteach o tosach domuin ocus o cruthughad denmae na n-dul.
Uair do reir rechta na toicten ata tinnremh in cinedha daenna uile ocus leiccmitne fen forn co fiadnach conadh treisi don toictiu inas duin.
Acht cenae damadh lor lat-sai uaim-si tochmi na mórgnim-sa do rem-innisin duit, ni fuicciub-sa ernail nach faistine i tír nó i muir nó i muigh no i g-caill nó i g-carraic nó inn aer nó inn ifirn nach cuairteoch uili noco m-beri-siu fis fire lat.’
‘I S lor lim-sa uait-siu omh,’ bar in gilla, ‘scur & etergleodh na mórchaingni-si d'faisneis dam.’
‘Bidh gar uair dait-siu on,’ ar in caillech, ‘uair toduiscfet-sae duit-si corp mairb eiccin it fiadhnaise innossae fen ocus do bér anmain ind a h-ifern co n-innisi fein duit-si cach ni iarfocha de.’
‘I S maith lem-su sin,’ ol seisium.
La sodain ro delb-si duibnell dorcha draidhechta impi & imsaé uathaidh d'iarraid apaigh mairb eiccin & a cuathan este, & is edh atberedh: ‘a deu nó,’ ol si, ‘as gairit co m-ba h-imda cuirp saerclann & abaige airdríg fo esonoir isin tir-si ce túsa innocht icc iarraid abaigh innti.’
Ráinic iaram inadh cinnte ar' cuiredh ár isin tir & cuirp imda can adhnacal ann.
O rainic isin armach fo cetóir ro teichset ass na h-uile fael & allta & ethaide bator ann re mét a h-aduaith & a h-urgraine na h-ammaite ráinic ann ina n-docom.
Batar mor n-anmann inn iffern ina freiscisi in uair-sin, uair ni fetatar cia dhibh do bertai d'aisneis scél in morcathu dissi, uair da tuccad si immonair anmanna in locta ro marbhait isind ármuigh uile do todusccadh tria tincetlaib druadh, ro soisedh le, & ni biadh frithtairisiumh fria imbi.
I S annsin ro tog-si araile aenabach fencbel fuataighe urcrechtach agedbán mór asind armaigh sin, & delligh a menmain fair.
Ro coirigh delan immo brághaitt & ráe imgairit as, & corran-bac cruaidhrigin for a cinn.
Ro gab-sí an corrán sin ina laim ocus ro tarraing in n-apach ina diaidh le dar cairrcib cruaide cendgarba, & dar cnoefoitibh corraca, & dar bernadaib brisde belshalchu na sliged, no co rainic le é cusin inad i n-gnathaigedh a h-ammaitecht & a draidhecht do denamh ed ón uaimscailp urgranna aduathmur inn accomul cairrci slébhe Eimh.
Fualascaige imda & fidhneimedha firdorcha & craebchaill comdigainn & doisiubair dluthbarracha im dorusbel na h-uamha sin, conar' thaitin ruithen greine no nach solsi ele riamh inte, acht solsi do gentae do tincetlaib druad no tre brechtaib ammaitechta.
Coiccrich coitcenn tire na m-beo & thire na marb ed ón nadh pianta na n-anmann inn-ifern in uaim sin.
Ro coirig ina faenlighe inn iarthur na h-uamae í, & Poimp Sext cona muintir ina fiadnaisi.
Ro gab a h-errad imtechtae & ammaitechta impi in uair sin ed ón lend fuataige ilbreac co taitnem cacha datha treimpi.
Tuc a da glaic immo moing n-glais n-garbleith, co ro scail a scuapfolt roinnidi rogarb dara slinnenaibh siar sechtair.
Ro coirigh craebcoroin cummaide do nathrachaiph neimide do timorgain in fuilt sin immo cend, & da nathraigh derscaigtecha for leimnigh & for banganaigh a forcipul a bairr.
Ro lin oman mor ocus imecclae Poimp Sext cona muintir i ca faicsin for in abairt sin, & o ro airig sisi sin ro impo a h-agaid co gruamda ortha & asbert friu: ‘Cret in gne omain taitnes foraiph, a óccu?’ ol sí.
‘Cuiridh bar m-bidgadh.
bar n-imecla uaib.
Do bértar ainim inbar fiadnaisi isin marb-sae, co m-bia fein ic imacallaim fribh & ic aisneis firinne duibh, & dano cid iat alcailli ifirn fein cona ilpianaib no taspentais daib nir'bo coir daib-si a n-adhuath no a n-urgrain, nó a n-imeccla forib & meisi immaraen frib.’
Ro impo frisin abach iarsin, & ro gab occ imbirt a h-ammaitechta fair ed ón ro doirt linn fola fichtighe imma ucht & imma urbruinne for tús, & ro chomail neime escaidhe co h-imda foi 'arsin, súgha foreiccnecha no faisctis a brechta druad-si fen asind escca.
Ro tuill-si frissin dono cach aidhmilledh aile & cach airicc urcoiteach ro bai for lesugud le.
Uair cach gein torathardha & gach súgh neimnech & cach duil duaibsech & gach udhim aidhmillti aili o tossach dhomuin riem ni bidh uiresbaidh na urchra neith dib fuirri-si in tansin.
Ni testa fuirri amh cuvur uanfadhach na con confadh.
Ni testa fuirri innedha na linche, edhon ceneli nathrach sein, & intan aipgiges a sotha ina bruinn tescaid a cuilena a bruinn da n-ingnip co teccait fein & inde a mathar leo triana broinn imach.
Ni teastatar fuirri dano na h-ifne snadmacha, ceneli nathrach sin fasait a smeraib na m-marb, & a n-aittreabh inn adhnaicibh na m-marb dogrés.
I S e met a neime co m-mudaighit na daine do tinfedh a n-anala.
Ni testa fuirri in t-eiccne ercoitech ed ón ceneli bratan sin commet traiged ann, & fostaid in luing fo lainseolad for lar in mara.
Ni testatar fuirri dano suile na n-draicce, & na clocha biti in netaibh na n-aquili & na g-corr n-grian, ar bíd do tesaidecht na n-en sin co lasfatis a nit fotha mana tucctais clocha fúaraighthe inntib do mesrugud a tesaidechta.
Ni testa fuirri dano nathracha eiteacha tire Arabia & trágha Mara Ruaid.
Ni testa fuirri trusca na nathrach adharcach a crichaib na h-Affraici.
Ni testa fuirri dano luaithredh na fenici a h-airther in domuin.
En ingnathach sin & da bliadain fot a saeguil.
Do gni fein teine di i forcend na rea sin, & lengidh isin teine co loisccther ann, co n-ásann en nua asa luaithredh doridisi.
Ro commaiscc tra Ericto ina h-uile trealmha neimide sin for in apach, & ro tuilli friu dano na h-uile luibe neimneacha batar isin Tesail fein & na lossa forar' laisi fen brict ic a n-geinemain asin talmain fo cetoir.
Tuargaib garb dordán mór & fogurmonguran eccubaid esaentadach fuirri 'arsin do ail & do etarguide na n-demna ifernaide do tabhairt anma di isind apach bai ina fiadnaisi.
I S mórfogur tra isa cosmailes ro taitne isin nuallan draidhechta sin Ericto.
Ro taitnetar amh ann amastracha na con & donala na fael & gerana na m-bufa & grechach na n-echtach & beicedach na n-alta & fetguire na nathrach & torman na tonn & fogurdresachtach na caillted & bresmadmanna na n-gaeth & torman na nell.
Ro ainmnigh-si co suaicnidh isin eturguide n-draidechta sin anmanna locta cadhais & cumachta ifirn & tuseach a pian.
Ba dib-side in Bas fein & Pluton mac Satuirn ri na n-dorcha & Ecates agedhbhan a rigan, & Cerbir craesfoslaicte dano doirseoir na n-dorcha, & Caran cnesodur immurcurthidh srotha Stig i n-ifirn, & tri dasactaide ifirn, edon, Alecto & Dissipone & Megaera, & na tri Parci ifernaide bite icc snim saeguil gach aen duinne isin domun ed ón Clothae & Lacessis & Atrapos a n-anmanna.
O tairnic de tra in eturguide mór sin ro taidbreastar for in apach & si icc seitfedhaigh & ic analfadaig & ic uchfadaigh dermáir, & cuvur mor & uanfad imdha imma bel & imma sroin & imma gnuis uile, atconnairc fosccad na h-anma for foluamain os cinn an cuirp, ar nir' lamh a fagbhail ar eccla na cailligi, & ba lesc le tocht i carcair cengalta & i cuibrigibh imcumcaib in chuirp mairb & se co h-inarmaighe ina fiadnaise ed ón aenda secdha sithrighte, & a ruiscc obela, & a bel cocuasta craesfoslaicte, & crechta letarta fata fiartarsna mora tairis.
Ba h-ingnad lasin caillig ind adhleiscci sin do lamachtain eter innagaid a cumacht no a draidechta.
Ro lin ferg & lonnas í iarsin, & ro ghabh nathraigh m-bí ar bolgán ina glaic, & tucc tri forguma di for in corp, & ro gab icc bagor co mor for demnaib ifirn & icc imcainedhh Táinic tesaidecht isin corp 'arsin, ocus ro reth in fhuil ara cuislennaib, & ro crithnaigsett a feithi, & ro boccsat a baill; & tucc clisedh fair co tuarcaibh ind aeinfecht o talmain é gan crapad coisi friss, gan fuirmedh uille no lama fri lar, can imresain eirge, noco tarrasair na colamain coimhdirigh ina cert-sesam i fiadnaisi Poimp Sext cona muintir.
Arai sin ba gné bhais beus bai fair, ar ro mair caite & baine inn ecca ina ballaiph.
Tucc buille ar a abra 'arsin, & ro tenc for na Ni ro saigh immorro comradh forra, & ni ro labair guth friu, ar ni tuccad do do glor, acht freccra gach neith no fiafraigte de amain.
Isbert an caillech Tesalda friss: ‘Do ber-sa logh maith duit,’ ol si, ‘dia n-apra firinne frim don cur-sa, ar madham buidech-sae dhit do ber d'onoir adnaicthe fort, conach lemat ammaite nó urtracha isin domun do thodusccud doridisi d'aisneis nó d'innisin scél doib co deredh in betha.
I S menic bis forscath mor & conntabairt for aisneis na faithe aile,’ ol si.
‘Na dena-sa amlaidh sin iter, acht tabair anmanna suaichenta forsna neithibh atbera, & innis co cinntech na h-inadha & na h-aimsera i n-dingentar iat.’
Ro scuch inn athfoccus do 'arsin, & ro can brict druadh ina beola.
Ro maidh a cai for in n-apach trúagh tursech ieram, gor' muid a déra dar a gruadaibh, & ro tinnscain labra friu, co n-ebert: ‘A dhaine maithe,’ ol se, ‘ni ranac-sa inn imdoimhnibh ifirn iter dar sruth Stig innunn, airm i finntar feib & reimes cach duine & airm i tát na Parci ifernaidhe ic snim na saegal. arintan ro basa ac triall tairis innunn as ann rom-gairmedh cuccaibh-si o bruach in t-srotha, co nach fil lim-sa de sin a fhis cia fot no cia gairde saeguil neich isin bith.
In ni atconnarc immorro & isa fis fil occom innesat daib-si co leir.’
‘Atconncas amh esaentaidh adbail & deabaid dermair eter allcaillibh na Roman uile inn ifern.
Atconnarc cumscaigte móra léo i fúr in cathasa Poimp & Cesair ed ón na maithe icc faccbail na n-deghinadh don luct as ferr indát marbtar isin cath-sa & na h-uilc icc faccbáil a n-drochinad don lucht as mesa indáit marbtar isin cath cetna.
Atconnarc faircsi broin moir for maithib na Roman inn ifern ara doilghe leo in cath-sa do chur.
Atconnarc faircsi failti moire for a n-olcaibh ar a febus leo in cath-sa do chur, ar sailit éttromugud a pian & comrainn a ciulan friu do rochtain cucu na cintach roimda marbtar isin cath.’
‘Atconnarc dobron mór for Silla inn ifern & geran adbal aici frisin toictin ar daigin a maic ed ón Silla a ainm side, & marbtar e don cur-sa isin cath.
Atconnarc dobron mór for Scip Affracain i n-ifirn ardaig a úa ed ón Scip esidhe, & dano do faet side isin Affraic tre bithin an catha-sa fos.
Atconnarc anfailte mór for an fellsamh, for Cait, ardaigh a úi ed ón Cato Iudicensis do faeth tria bithin in catha-sa.
Atconnarc failte mor & subaige n-dermair for Brútus inn ifern.
Ba h-e adbar na fáilte moire sin, ar as eisiumh fessin ro cuir Tarquin diumsach a flaithes na Roma, & as e a ua ed ón Brutus aile, mairbfis Cesair isin Roim.’
‘Cid fil ann tra acht atconncas co dobronach anfailid inn ifern cach aen isa mac & isa ua marbtar inn imairicc in catha moir-si.
Attconnarc co subach somenmnach cach aen da fil laghad occus éttromugud pian do rochtain na cintach Atconnarc Pluton mac Satuirn ri na n-dorca occus tire na m-marb ic tinol a riaghaired & a piantori & a drong n-dirmmand n-deamnach da saigid, & atbert friu im fiadnaisi-siu:
‘Daingnigter for slabraidh & for n-glais & bar n-geibenna lib, ol se.
Géraigter bar m-beara & var g-corrána & bar faebair.
Glinnigter bhar slegha & bar tuaga occus bar n-uird esoircne anmann.
Arlaidhter bar teinte londa loiscctecha.
Aithighter bar clocha & bar cairrci cendgarba.
Oslaicter bar n-uamdoirsi pianta & riagta, & na h-inadha pianta na ro h-oslaicit riam occoib oslaiccter don cur-sa, ar ni tancattar a h-aencath isin domun riam cuccuib, & ni targa a h-oencath isin domun doridisi, coimlin a targa in bar n-dail a h-immairecc in morcatha-sa Poimp & Cesair.’’
‘Atconnarcus muinter Plutoin co subach somenmnach de sin, & siat uile co h-urlamh i frestal esairgne & imlesta ina ria do cintachaiph cucu assan cath mor-su.
I S adbar dubaighe dermaire duit-si sin amae, a maic ind airdrígh, & ber in coimdhidhnad m-becc-sa let arai ed ón atconnarc-sa Plutón fein ic ordugud inait pianta fo ercomhair Cesair inn ifern.
Atconnarc-sa inad cumsanta immorro fo ircomair Poimp & a da mac i tulaigh na trocaire i n-grienbrugib ifirn. arcen co fagbat na h-airdrigha a n-airlech isin cath mor-sa, mo nuaran as gar uair co roiset maraen a n-inadha urdaltae inn iffern.’
‘I S mór bar n-onoir-si ann cena as denta daibh saint da saigidh.
I S e deiliugudh in coccaid moir-si dona rígaib, indara fer dib do marbhad isind Egipt & a adhnacal i sruth Nil a n-Eigipt, & in fer aile do marbad isin Etail & a adhnacal i sruth Tibir isin Roim.
Tusa fein immorro, a maic an airdrígh, na sir form-sa faistíne do denam duit, ar fogeba faith bus tairisiu lat innússa do innisin do tinnriuma duit ed ón an t-airdri t'athair fein do ragha do t'accallam 'arna marbad.
Acht acc-so aeinni atberim-si fribh, na denaidh tairisi don Eoraip nó don Affraic nó don Aissia, ar ni fagbaim-si isin domun uile rann is innillium duib inas in Tesail.’
Ba santaigi-te la mac in airdrígh in cath do tabairt isin Tesail sin.
Ba fir don faith ind ebairt cena, ar ger'bo h-eisinnill doib in Tesail, ba h-eisinnilliu dhoibh ranna aile in domuin innas. arro marbad Poimp fein isin Aisia, & mac da maccaib inn Affraic & in mac aile inn Eoraip.
O tairnic tra don apach na scéla sin d'aisneis doib ro bai co tostach taethenach attruagh atturseach ina sesam ina fiadnaisi, & se icc urnaidhe bais on cailligh, ar nir' lam a ainimm deiliugud fris noco comarleicced an caillech dhi.
Tainic in caillech Ericto rempu iarsin darsin uama immach, & doroine tor teinedh dermaire indorus na h-uama, & ro cuir an apach da loscudh fair.
Ro fáccaib annside e, & tanic fein maraen re Poimp Sext docum loggphuirt Poimp Maige a athar, co rancatar in longphort & na scuru i crepuscul na maitne muiche trath etarscartha lae & aidque.
Conidh remscél do remscélaib catha móir na Tesaili co n-icci sin.
Echtra Poimp Sext, & taircetla Ericto Tesalta, & faistine inn arrachta ifernaidhe ainm in scéoil sin.
I S é sin dano reimscél deidinach catha na Tesáili.
Conidh comairem remscél co n-icci sin.
Scéla immorro & turtechta & eitirdeilighthi in catha móir fein, & tinnriumu na laechraide inn ellach inn imairicc moir i m-muigh na Tesaili fein, is iat atfiadur sisana fodhesta.
Cath mor muighe na Tesaili innso.

sin ro raidhiustar Ericto aingidh imarsaidh iffernaide, nirbo soinmeach airerda immorro ruccadh ass in adaigh sin resin morcath i l-longphortaibh fer n-domuin.
Ina m-battor d'uamdoirsib iffirn i tir na Tesaile ro h-osslaicit in adaigh sin iat.
Do berad a tlachta folaig & a n-dicleithe druadh do uilib aittib demnacdaib in tire inn adaig cetna.
Tanccatar foil & foluaimnigh & anmanna feochra fuirechra & daescarsluagh demnacda in tire uile, co m-batar i n-dithrebaib na Tesaile inn adaig sin ic urnaidhe in morcatha arna barach.
Ro tuitsett sceith & slegha na cruinne uile da n-aidlennaib isin aidche cetna.
Atcesa ann saignena roimdhae & caera teintidhe ic tuitim a fraigtibh na firmaminte nemda, co n-imtacmaictis in talamh i mórtimcill na dá mórlongphort.
Ro comdoirtset tri ruadbuinne robarta in betha fon domun inn aidche sin ed ón muir Caisp & muir Ruad & muir Torrein, co ro comtuairgset a morthonna ina m-ba coimnesa doib do murruscaib cairrcide & do bennaib all & airdsliap in talman, co closs fona crichaib batar comfoicsiu doib mongar in mórmara & escal inn occiain & garbconghair na m-bledhmil & na muc mara & na ron & na rinnach, na tollcenn & na corrcenn, na milmór & na libedhan & ilpiast anaichnidh inn occiain arcena.
Ro blosccnuallsat ceithre primgaetha in betha fon domhan in adaigh cetna ed ón an Stefir iniar, in Voir atuaidh, inn Euir anair, inn Auster andes.
comma rainic comtuargon & imlessadh doib for lar tire na Tesaili gor' fas teintech & toirneach & ainbtine imforcradach isind aer desin, cur' fas crith & talamchumscugud i fotaib & i slutraigibh in talman, cur ro fogluaisset inn uile coimtinol demnachdha bai isin Tesail a h-uamtollaib i talmuin, a dithrebaibh a cailltedh, a scailpib a carrac, a glacaib a tulach, a fanglenntoip a cnoc, a mamannaib a sliab, curro comhgairsit i n-aeinfecht & i n-oenfaball im dib mórlongphortaip na da airdrig sin ed ón Poimp & Cesair, gor bo lor d'adhuath & d'urgrain & do cridenbas dona slóghaibh a n-eistecht.
Re siangail & re sibsanaigh na m-bufa & na loisccend.
Re donalaibh & re h-amustraig na fael ocus na con ocus na cuanart ocus na mac tire.
Re coimhcnedaigh ocus re barann beicedhaigh na n-os ocus na n-alma ocus na n-allta n-eccennais.
Re h-ardglaedaig ocus re h-ardgairmnibh na parti ocus na l-leoman ocus na mathgaman.
Re gothgail graccallaigh na n-en ocus na n-etaide ocus na foluaimnech arcena.
Ra garbhgortgholgrechaig na n-gelt ocus na n-gribh n-ingnech, na n-ammaite ocus na n-urtrach ocus na m-badb m-bélderg & na fantaisi foltscailte ocus na n-drong n-dirmann n-demnacdha ocus diabhaliasccaigh inn aeoir arcena os a cinn, nir' leicced lochad no tatham no tinnabrad d'oenduine i cechtar na da mórloggport airet batar na h-ammaiti for an abairt sin ina timcell.
Intan immorro atractatar luathghoetha adhuarae imluatha ocus glasneoill utmalla etarbhuasacha na maitne, ro ansat na h-urtracha da n-aidhmilltib, ro tairinnset a trethan ocus ro coisccset a congair ar uaman & ar ureccla solsi na maittne da t-tarractain.
Ro tuilset na slóigh iarumh lasin tai moir sin, ocus atrocair a suantairtim cotalta for in airdrigh, for Poimp.
Tarfas fis ocus amra ocus aislingte do-som isin cotlud sin ed ón indar leis a beith fein co maithibh na Roma imbe ina suide rigdha i n-oenach na m-buad for lar na Roma, ocus slógh tire Letha uile ocus luct na Roma uile, eter occ ocus sen, do beith isin oenach imbe, ocus siat uile co fogurgairibh moraibh ocus co nuall ocus co éiselbi adbail ac denamh a buad-som ocus ic toccbail a clua ocus a urdarcais os rigflathaib in talman & os degferaib derscaigtechaib in domuin, feib as glormaire ro batar imme isin oenach mor do ronadh do i l-laithib a rígtha isin Roimh ar clod do na murthaidhe & na meritrighi rígh na Pointi ocus locta na h-Espaine treuillige iar n-iarthar.
Bhess is edh ro bai annsin menma snimach urecclach in airdrigh do cúartugud na maithis mor fuair fecht aili & in toictiu do taisbenad na Roma inn aislingi do, ar nir' leigset na faithe do a faicsin innas aile.
Nó dano is ac taircetul tromgaire n-doinmeach in morcatha arna barach ro taisbenait na gairiu subacha soinmecha sin do Poimp ina cotludh, ar isedh is gnath anfoilti do taircetal tria failte na h-aislinge & na fisi aidhcidhe co menic.
Tainic mochneoill na maittne foisin, & ro gabh solsi ind lae ic fortamlugud for bansolsi na retlann & na renn aidhchide.
Da festais fir an domain cena rob adbar dubha occus dobroin dermair doib maitin in laithi sin d'faicsin, daig ni ro tairic oenla riem tareis na Dilenn don cinidh doennae samail in ro tairicc in la sin doib ed ón an dith ocus a mudugud inn ellach in mórcathae eiter Poimp & Cesair for muigh na Tésali re h-ed an lae sin namma.
I S techt tar aicned immorro, ocus is feidm os nirt, ocus as onfaisi occiain, ocus as iarraidh fhorais i fudomain ocus is decsin radhairc i r-reodoirce, ocus as gabail re muir lain icc linadh, ocus as triall eiccne for airdrigh, ocus as techt i cath gan congaibh airm, ocus as seoladh ind agaidh gaeithe, ocus as cuindgidh freabta i fritagaidh ecca, ocus as airem ar immatt eccintech d'oenduine isin domun fobairt aithrisi no aissneisin for cathugud in lai sin, ar is ed is gnaithciu ann aisneis imforcrach do tabairt for gnimradaib na cath aile icca n-innisin.
I S deimin immorro na fagaibtear isin bith oentenga oenduine da tised a taithmet nó a tuarusccbail gach a n-dernadh do morgnimaib ann, ar nir' furail no imforcraidh staraide cacha cineda isin cruinne do cumma & d'ordugud gnimscélradh in oencatha ina m-batar ilcinela an talman o or co h-or.
A suim immorro, & a n-aird & a n-airdirc triallfaidter sunn a tecclaim co cert & co commair doreir amal frith iat i fis & i foglaim & i finnfoclaibh filedh & inn ealadhnaibh augdarda na n-augdar Romanach buddein.
La sodain tra táinic lansolsi na matni da saigid, & arai ní ro artraigh in grian doib beus biucc, uair leiscce & admailli & ainesccaide atract in grian os tonnaib inn oicciain do taitnem dar colair turcbála suas isin maitin-sin innas in cach maitin reime riem, ar bai da neimdeini ro taitin grian frisin talam an la sin.
Atar la cach curbo seachna solsi, & curbo h-ercra greini rob ail ann, ar ro suigh & ro tarraing in grien da saigid isin maitin sin uile tromnellgala dluithi doburda duibciach deridh na h-aidhchi & fraisnella fannscailti fuasnadacha na firmaminte uile, & dano ni d'furtacht na d'altrom a l-lassar no a teintidechta no a tesaltactu sin, amal atberat na fisecda, acht as da m-beith ina clarcolbadaibh gorma glasgarba & 'na m-bratachaib duba doscailte ettarra & tir na Tesaili. arnirbo lainn lasin grein a ruithne sirglana solusta do taitnem frisin tir sin, ar aidbli in moruilc ro ba cinnte do denamh innte ed ón dith & dilgend in cinedha doenna iter Poimp & Cesair.
Araisin tra gerbo lesc ainesccaid inmall an eirghe sin atract fo deoidh in grian ina h-ubullmhioll cró & ina crunnpupall teintidhe os dreich in talman, curro fortamlaigh a solsi for bansolsi na rend & na retlann, co ro lin glennta & cnuca & caillte & tuaithtemracha in talman.
O ro airigset slogbuidne mor-longphuirt Poimp in t-eitirdeiliugud sin in lai & na h-aidce atrachtatar eirge athlamh aeinfir la mochdedol na maitne muiche.
Ro eirig geoin mor ocus fogarmuirn & fothromh & fogluasact & fodord adbal isna longportoibh desin.
Do dheochatar na slóig co m-batar ina m-buidhnib & ina sesib ic geran ocus icc uchbadaigh ar fot na faithchi & na n-urdhom & na n-imdhorsi im puplib inn airdrigh.
Ba sedh a n-aenguth & a n-aenradh uile, cudhnodh & tinnenus in morcatha can fuirech gan esnadhadh co brath dar in lasin amach.
Do gapsat ic aisc & ic tobeim co mor for in n-airdrigh, for Poimp, ar imfuireach in catha do.
Atberte frisium a beith lesc & a beith meta ocus a beith imecclach & a beith ic fulang tarcaisne co mor o cliamain ed ón o Cesair, & conidh aire no fuirged in cath ar eccla socraite imar sud do dedail fris & a scarad fein re rigflaithius na Roma 'arsin.
Dia fris tra as truag inn abairt ro ba for slógud in longpuirt annsin amh ed ón a m-beith ic saint & ic ailges im tabairt an catha an lucht ac nach raibe do saegul acht madh co h-am tabarta in catha nama. iat ríghfhlaithe rathmara & popul in airther dano nirsat luga a n-acaine inas gach drong aile ann im tinnenas & im cudnodh in catha ara foti leo beith inn ecmais socrachta i tire ocus a n-atharda budéin.
O 'tcuala airrigh & uaisle, flaithe & fuilngidh, consuil & comairlidi in t-senaid Romhanaig in gearan mor sin ic rígaibh & ic rodhainibh in longpuirt im fuireach in catha moir sin is i comairle do ronsat, techt i pupaill Poimp dia asslach fair accaine na n-airdrig do coscc & in cath do tabairt in la sin fen.
Maith co n-icci in la sin ceana in t-airecht ro coid isin pupaill sin ed ón rigflaite na Roman.
It e annso anmanna na n-ardflaithe & na n-airech ro cotar isin pupaill sin ed ón Cata mor Iudicensis & Brutas in primconsul & Sill mac Sill, & Scip mac Scip maic Scip Affracain, a cathraig Lucinae, & Tuil Cicer, in primretoridh aentenga ón na sulbuiri latianda can samail gan baramail ina h-aimsir fríae.
Tainic ann Decius consul & Curio consul & Cetegas consul & Drusus consul & Grachas consul & Camill consul & Marcellus consul & Torquatus consul & Lucius consul & Lucilius consul & Lentulus consul a cathraig na h-Esculi isin Etail, & Agellus consul & Domitius consul a cathraigh Corpin isin Etail, & Libon consul tusech na n-Eotrastacda & Tarnius consul tusech na n-Umbreta & Fabius consul & Varus consul o dinn Auximon, & Antonius consul & Octavius consul & Marcellinus consul & Iunius consul & Quintus consul & Scevola consul & Marius consul & Lelitus consul & Aruns consul & Altus consul & Agellinus consul & Affranius consul.
Gneus Pompeus & Sextus Pompeus da mac an airdrigh, & maithe na Romhan arcena, & drong-dirmanna mora do degrígaib an domain immailli O 'tconnaic in t-airdri Poimp iat isin pupaill is edh ro raidh friu: ‘Cidh ro fogluais na maiti-si i tradh-sa a mucha-sa do lo o puplib & o leabtaib & o n-dergadaibh,’ ol se.
Gerbo h-imda fer frestail gotha & urlabra dó isin pupaill, araidhe sin tra ro togsat & ro ordaighset co h-oentadach aoinfer da freccra & da accallaim & d'asslach in catha fair & do frestul gotha & urlabra daracenn uile ed ón an t-shai forcti & in t-ollam uasal oirdnidhe & an cainnell airechta & in abis fesa & an fisid foglama & in indeoin forais & an forus breth & an dromcla gacha dana & inn eochair foslaicthe gacha h-ealadna, in primretorca on.
Tul Cicer, in aen tenga as ferr glor & aslach & innsci & urlabra ro bai in aenaimsir fria gan fodurd, can format, can imresain fria imbe.
Beo ocus tend, trén ocus toccbalta cach cuis ocus cach caingen lasa congnadh ce madh etrom anbfann anarrachta a adbar.
Marb immorro & tlaith & tuitmeach ocus trascairte gach dail no daeradh ocus gach caingen no cairigedh, cemad scel firen fiadhnach fasaigte forglithe no beith ica furail fair.
Inbaidh immorro ba iudic breithe eisium fein in gleod do genadh ni ticfad do bretheamnaip in betha uile a tollad no a tathair dar a eisiu.
Consul ro-uasal e on, ocus ro coiscc mor do coccad & d'imresnaibh na Roman beus airet ro ba beo tria gaeis a gloir & a labra ocus a urlabra & a nirt a lama & a claidim & a cruas a cridhe, ocus ar imat a miled ocus a socraide disli budhdein, conarb ingnad ocus nar' decair fer a maithiusa in fhir-sin do freccra righ ocus d'asslach comairle caich fair ocus d'aisneis ocus d'innisin ruin na socaidhe do.
Ba saint ocus ba duthract lais ar da adbar aslach in catha for Poimp ed ón ar na maithi do cur in dala ina leth im furail in catha, & dano ba lan-lainn leis fein rochtain na Roma i traiti ar mett ocus ar aidble a édala 'na h-aenaigib ocus 'na margadaibh ocus 'na dalaibh.
I S edh inso asbert ieram: ‘A uasail ocus a oirdnide ocus a oenri,’ ol se, ‘da festa-su eim ni suaill sodhethbiri ro fogluais na maiti-si i trath-su it dochom, ocus madh cet let atfiadu-sa duit in toiscc imo tancatar.’
‘Abair uait biucc co cloamar,’ for Poimp.
‘Do fetaraisi fein, a airdri, conidh cian ocus conidh fota atát na maithi-si isin coccad-sa immailli frit-su inn ingnais a muintire ocus a ferann, a cathrach ocus a castiall ic fulang docra ocus merten mara ocus tire as gach crich im-araili i freastal in morcatha sa fil ettrat-sa ocus Cesair.
I S ed rob ail leo, crich & scur ocus foircenn da beith for na docraibh sin doib, ocus ni faicet scur aili forro acht tre etergleod in catha moir eiccin.
Inni as scor do cra ocus do bethadh dibh ann, is edh as tol doib-sium a gnim can cairde, can fuireach, can failliugud isin laithi-si indiu fein.
As e a n-aenglor uile--ocus atat acat atach imme, iter riga & airecha ocus amsu ocus anrada ocus occbad ocus dóescursluag--leicc eturra ocus Cesair do clodh, ocus fulaing doib a clodh it fiadnaisi.
Atberatt fos contat mora ocus condat maithi cummaine na toictin fort-su cusindiu.
Ni becc leo uait-si daracenn sin uile airbert dit uaitib namma ocus tocht i cenn catha co Cesair.
Atberat fos conidh romor in lucht fuirigh ocus foslongphuirt as ail lat-su it farradh ed ón an cinedh doenna uile, ar ni cien fuilengus Cesair doip can clodh da leicci-siu da shaigidh iatt.
Ata ar aill aile ann dano mana coir dait-siu tinnenus in imaireicc do clodh Cesair. ara mett as nar ocus as mebul lasna cinedhaib ro cloaisi can fuirech gan fosugud occo acht a clodh icc tocht tairsibh namma, beith duit co fata ocus co h-adhmall ic clodh Cesair can srainedh catha focettoir fair.
Atait righa imdha it tinol-sa no fobartais fein freccra Cesair im cath cen co betha-su i cinn-comair friss eitir.
Ale cia leith ro cuaidh in clu mor-sin ocus an borrfad ocus an brígh dermair ocus an danatus adbul ro bai occat-sa eitir masina queist fil fort cuisi & caingne in t-senaidh Románaigh do lecon i l-leith na n-dea ocus na toictin.
Ni cumtig duit-si on cena.
Arbertait-sium a n-arma leo docom in catha & a mergeadha mana aentaighi-siu friu, ocus nach ba nar lat-su andsidhe gan a furail ar eiccin forra Cesair do clodh ocus gan h'aentaidh fein d'fagbail docom an catha remi?
Ocus dano mas ar ar n-daigne ocus gurab duinn-e gnisi in t-imfuireach sin, occus d'ar les, leicc ocus cetaig duinn saigid Cesair isin aimsir ocus isind inadh bus lainni linn fen, ocus bidh aran maig-si na Tésaili ón isin lo-sa inniu.
Ale cidh imma tairmiscci-si claidhmhi in domuin itir o telccadh fola Cesair, ar as urlamh iat uili friss.
Itat in slóg uili icc gabáil a n-arm ocus ic bertnugud a n-urcor.
Ocus as inbectain leo fuirech re a mergadhaibh gan imtecht rempo docom in chatha.
Dena tinnenus, iarum, a degduine, ocus geib t'arma, ocus coirig fein do shloghu na ro scuchat uait do socraite ocus na rot-facbaiter inn uathad muintire for lar in longphuirt.’
‘Ar n-glor-ni aile sud,’ for Cato mor Iudicensis.
‘I S e cidh aenglor na sochaide,’ for Brutus ocus for na maithe archena.
Ro lae socht mor ocus snimh adbal for in airdrigh desin, ocus ro cuir fair co mor, ar nír' lainn leis an cath do cur ocus nir' sodaing do taidhecht inagaid in primretorca ocus a innscni ocus a asslaig co n-aentaidh na maithe uile immaraen fris.
Ocus ro airigh-sium na faithe ocus an toictiu ocus in conach d'impodh fair trit-sin, conidh edh ro raidh fo deoidh: ‘Cidh fil ann tra,’ ol se, ‘acht madh edh sin bus lainn la cach uile, mana reccat a les formar misi do shetugudh comairle rompa. fil ann tra cidh da m-biu-sa im aenar ic fuirech na faithe, acht tíagat as biucc co fesarata conach catha isin laithi-si indiu eiccin.
Forclim-si immorro comba esin in la oirrderc i m-bia scur saeguil na sochaidhe, acht damad í mo comairli-si dano no fiasta ann ro clofinn-si Cesair gan ar gan airlech.
Do-berainn co fomamaighté d'athnuadhugudh in t-sidha ro mill.
Dia friss, as dall an t-aiccnedh don lucht lasar' ferr fuil do thodhail ic gnimh in catha catharda inas Cesair do clodh can ar, can airlech gan telccud fola itir.
Ro forbthighsium-ni urmor ar cotach don cath ocus don coccad cusindiu.
Ro bensam amh na tire ocus na muire for Cesair.
Ro aslaigh-sium dano gorta for a muintir co filet ic slait na n-gort n-anabaidh sechnón tire na Tesaili cach lai.
Ro furail-sium fortha conidh mó as mian ocus is toghu ocus is duthracht leo taidecht da marbad fein cucuinn-e innas i fuireach mar tat.
Araisin masa lainne la cach cathugud inas clodh gan cath, ocus mas ferr leo a conach do cur i n-uct na toicthin ocus i fidhcellacht na Faite ina congmáil ime, cidh dambiu-sa m'oenar na n-agaid uile imme.
Acht mad óenní do-rat in toictiu dam-sa chena, in rigrecht Romanach do stiuradh ocus d'follamnughadh cusin laithi-si indiu.
Atci fein dono conidh mo ocus conidh ferr indíu innas in la tuccad im laim-si é.
Ditned fein festa é, ar ni bia a soladh no a doladh damh-sa o sund imach, ocus dano cipe fasus do chathugudh in lai-si fos fuacraim-si ocus atcuirim cona bia a moladh no a tathair damh, ar ni gabaim a maisi nó a domaisi im leith o sunn amach.
Deitber dam-sa on, ar ro fetar-sa co cinnte cona bia maith eitir de, acht madh olc Ar inti clofes ann bidh miscnighthe la cach, ocus bidh tathairthe o feraib in talman inti clofiter ann: as fis ocus is follus conidh messam cach main.’
‘I S aire sin bad lainn & bad saint ocus badh rogu carthanach lim-sa co tegmad in cétga no diubraicte isind imairecc-sa triam cenn-sa comtarsna acht comad soer mo muinter tar m'eisi gan a mudughadh.’
I S ed sin tra ro aisneid Poimp, ocus o tairnic dhó a faisneis ro cetaig do cach a n-arma do gabáil ocus eirge docom in catha, amal bis stiurusmann lunga luchtmuri lanmoire cusa teccaim gaeth rothren a n-aghaid a h-imtechta, ocus bidh ic seitriugud ocus ic fulang co fata inn agaidh na gaithe noco furailenn ocus noco n-aslaigenn treisecht na trengaithi fair fo deoidh in long do lecon co laindirech la nert na gaithe in conair gabas 'ar n-dith a neirt ocus a chalmatais.
Ba h-amlaid sin do Poimp ic fosadh-congmhail stiuire an flaithiusa ocus in ríghrechta Romanaigh in agaid aiccenta an-b-fosaig ur-etruim fuasnadaig a muintire airet co tainic de, ocus o nar' cumaing a n-imfostadh ro cetaigh doib a n-arma do gabail, amal leiccius marcach a srian la h-ech rott.
Cidh tra acht is neimimcomaircech ro freccradh in forcongra sin la h-anradha in domain isin uair-sin.
Ro scailit inn oenfecht & inn oenfabhall docom a m-both & a caprach & a pupall.
I S garb an crith & an comboccad ro bai isin longphurt annsin.
Ro gabsat for tuarccuin a n-ochta & a n-urbhruinne.
Ro soiset a n-aiccenta & a n-derbha do sochaidi moir dibh.
Ro bansat a n-aighthe & a n-gnúisi.
Ro dubhglassatar a m-beoil lasin tuairgnigh & lasin uctbualadh & lasin n-geoin moir & lasin n-grithghair adhbal ro bai ic slogad in longpuirt, ic gabáil a n-echradh, ic eitiudh a n-arm, ic seinm a stoc, ic comgairm a comarc, ic sleman-cainnligh a sciath, ic slipadh a claidem, ic limad a lorcfertas catha, ic trothadh a tuagh, ic melbleith a craisech, ic athinnsmadh a slegh ocus a l-laighen, ic tarraing thennadh a suainem, ic stuaghboccadh a m-bogadh, ic sinedh a sreng, ic linadh a saigetbolg do raignibh a saiget, ic daingniugudh a n-dillat, ic áithiugudh a spor, ic glinniugudh a srian, icc tairrnged ocus ic fosughud a crua imdhaingen iarnaidhe fo cosaib a n-echradh, ic innell ocus ic imluadh a n-adhelge arcena ocus a n-arm catha o sin amach.
Is annsin dana ro gabsat righ ocus ruirigh ocus rodaine an longpuirt for eitiudh a n-arm.
Nirbo deidbliu in geoin sin ed ón drongair na luirech lineach lancuir ic a slislecon im cneschorpaib na curadh, ocus figair sibsanach a m-bil-chimhas inichtarach ica n-imcomailt frisna h-asanaibh iarnaidhib, ocus masladach na claidem claislethan coilgdírech ar shlesaibh na laech, globeimnech na minn righda ro-etroct ic a cengult osna cathbarraib cumhtaightibh, sreangal na luireach ocus na sciath & na sciathrach ica suidiugudh for muinel-braightibh na miledh ocus for rightaibh na righ rodiumsach, crithnugud & boccadh-bertnugudh na slegh slinnlethan & na laigen lethangorm ocus na craisech crandremar crofairsing ica n-gabail re gelguaillibh na n-gasradh n-gaisccedhach inn airius in morcatha.
Ro gab iaram in t-airdri fein ocus in flaith forglide ed ón Poimp Maige, a catharm catha & a erred imaricc imme ed ón ro gab da braici breaca buailtecha do sinsnath uretrom uainegda im dibh coscolptaib dho, co n-gabtais o innaib a traiged co remhar a sliasat.
Ro gabh dá assan a certcomhat do breacsrol blathetrocht tarsu i muigh anechtair.
Ro gab dá asan coema corcurda do croicnib leoman arna lansuathadh tarsu sin fos.
Ro gab dá asan imthroma imdluithi iarainn tarsu sin fos.
Ro gabh dá scaburassan ailli uretroma do electair ed ón do thinni commascda airgit ocus credhuma, tarsu sin uile anechtair.
Ro gab tonaigh seim sreabnaide snathcháil siretroct do sita oeingel i custal a gelcnis dó.
Ro gab tairsi sin inar imetrom orcimsach do srol rígda a tirib Siria, cona stuaghlubaibh airgdidib, cona cnaipip oir deircc fri h-iadad & fria h-oslaccad ann.
Ro gab inar suairc suata sofilltech sreabnaidhe do croicnib ferb tairsib sin.
Ro gabh dá breclamainn boccmine biannaide immo dib gelglacaib ocus im innaibh a lamh.
Ro gab tarsu sin uili luiriuch dluith drolach dualach degfigthe derscaigthi d'uriarann do glaisiarann cruaidh cotat-rigin arna legad ocus ar na h-athleagad fecht for a sé.
Ro gab sciamhluirig n-imetruim n-electarda do commusc oir & airgitt óengil tarsu imuich anechtair do somaisi a erridh ríghdachta inn airdrig.
Ro gab cathcris comdluta immo taebu cona bordaibh ordha fris, cona dunadh do licc logmuir, cona tuaghmilibh rinnta d'or & d'airgett on ur co araile de, co n-gabad in caithchris sin do o fanaib a arann co h-ard a formna.
Ro gab a armlama flatha i forcipul in cresa sin eter a uillinn cli & a taeb ed ón claidem cruaidh coilgdírech aithger ailtnide blaith-slipta bricht-faebrach stuagmar sithrigin sohfillteach cona eltaib snaidtib slemonsoilsib do raighnib na lecc lógmar, cona mindruimnib mineccair do snath óir or-loiscti imma urdorn, cona inntech coemcumtaighe do cnaimh aoingel elifinte, cona dib caelspeltib blathmaetha biannaide ettarra-sein & a eo, cona mintruaill edrochtglain forordhai tarsu amuigh anechtair.
Ro gabh a corrchathbarr cirach clarda cruanchumtaigthi dar maelat drolach, linech a luirige imma cenn, cona dib remartinnib imcoimsib iernaidib, co forbrechtradh airgit aeingil forra dar a muinél siar sechtair ass, cona sronlainn imdaingein iarnaidhe, co forbrechtradh oir deirg fuirri, dar aghaid in airdrígh ass, conarbo sogonta ocus narbo soidercctai oenball dia curp nó da cendagaid acht mana dirged in toictiu soigett no beran dar trealmaib timtirechtai a anala no a feghtha Ro gabh a inncomarta a imperechta ed ón a minn ríg, uasa sin uili imma cenn.
Minn oir buide eisside, & bil-cimsu oir deirg fris co sreith cristail & gem coem carrmoccail ina mórtimcill ann.
Coimhrinnadh comcoitcenn do dhelbaib en & ethaiti & anmann n-anaichentae n-ingantach fair osin amach, co n-dib benncobraib blathsnaidthibh do leccaib togaidib tire na h-Innia airtheraige uasu co n-deilb uvuill Affracda, cona cairchi ciuil ann for inn cacha benncobair dib, co m-ba binnither teta mendcrot binufhoghroghudh na n-ubullcairchi-sin ic a fogluasacht la cach ceim no cinged in t-airdri fein & la h-ardluth a eich.
Aeingem socarchain solusta do derscnaig do gemcumtachaib an domain inn airenach a aigthe an innchomurta sin, co m-ba comsolus la ocus adaigh in gach inad conuargaibthe e.
Tuccait cuicci a dá shleigh ailli innelta órcrai cona n-dib cael-crannoip comfata coimdirge do cedir neimhcrin inntu, cona n-airiallaibh airgdidhe fothu, cona semmannaip creduma trena m-braigtibh.
Ro h-erbait da righmilid d'imurcur na sleg sin la taebu inn airdrigh gach conair imma cingfad isin cath.
Tuccad a comla catha for a inchaip ed ón a scieth croderg aelenda orcobradhach.
Ba ditiun dá coicc cathmhiled i cró catha.
Brechtar-breacad do bolg semannaib finndruine etir ecclanna oir Slat chotat condualach ina h-imtacmung cona loss imcael imthrom iarnaide fuithe, cona taulimlinn tailc tuinigthe d'or derg daigerda, cona cobradaib coimeccuir d'airget oeingel, co forbrecad oir buide fair, cona sciathrach linidi lanurlam eli.
Stuagdruimne rinnta roimda do ilcinel cach tinne isin bith, arna coimecur tre indtlechtaibh ollamhan & tre aiccentaib suadh for leirg droma in sceith sin.
Ro h-erbait ochtar ríghmhiled re cotut-congmail in sceith sin ar incaip Poimp inn imforran & inn imargail in catha moir.
Tuccadh cuicci iarsin each midhach merdana moraiccintech, lonn luath luthmur leimnech leabarmongach, tenn, tailc taiblebar torannclesach, airdcond allata eterbuasach uchtletan, gobcael cosremhar, bolccsroin baisletain bolccshuilech, cona cetair crua iarnaide foi, cona srianglomur airgdide friss, cona suidedillait ordha for a muin.
Ro cing Poimp indorus a pupaill for in each-sin d'ordughadh aslogh ocus do córugud a cath.
Ba feidm adbal d'oeinfer isin domun triall cosnama na cruinne frisin uair-sin, ara righdacht fein & ar airde a aiccnid ocus ar febus a tidnacuil & ar aidbliu a innmais & ar imat-linmuirecht a h-socraiti & a tinoil. arbatar uile ilcinela in talman o Sléibh Elpa sair co n-icci inn Innia airtheraigh acht na Pairteccda nama, & ilcinela na h-Affraici o Roim budhdhes co crichaib in tentige, ar aenachadh ina farrad in uair-sin.
Neach atcifed iat annsin ni sailfedh nech n-uresbaidh for in cined doennu can a m-beith isin t-socraiti moir sin immaraen re Poimp.
Ro ba doca leis gan aeinfer socraiti i farrad Cesair inas acmaing frestail in tinoil moir sin aicci.
O do deisidh Poimp for a ech iaram, ro tenc, & ro mid, & ro mor-dech uadh for slógad an longphuirt ic tinol a mergedh & ic comgairm a comarc.
Ro leicc a fuatan foerma don eoch allata airdermach allmurda bai foi docom rigbuidean na Roman airm i m-batar ina m-broin badba & ina cipi comdluta & ina coroin dluith dithoghlaide inn aironach in morlongphuirt.
Ro leicced sraitslige lethan lanfairsing do, gor' gab a inadh imtechta eitir na ceithri senatoraib for larmedon catha na Roman.
Ro bai ica comairle friu cinnus no ordaighfedh a sloga.
Tanccatar a túsigh conaire & a eolaigh sligedh cuicci, ocus asbertsatt fris: ‘A ardflaith & a aenri,’ for siett, ‘atait sligthe salcha dochra do-imtechta ocus conara cumcca ettrat ocus inn imreidh ed ón mamtulca sleibi Ois & fanmothair glenna Bebis.
I S lor deit-si, a deigri, do catha do cengal & do corugud iar riachtain deit for maigreidib maige moir na Tesaili allamuig da imreided in glenna.’
‘Dentar amlaid,’ for Poimp, ‘treoraiged in t-sliged co seitreach remainn iarum.’
Ro gapsat rempu la sodain dar leithcenn sleibi Ois & dar lar glenna Bebis immach docom maige na Tesaili gach n-direch.
Tancatar miturusa móra & airrdhe aighthidhe aduathmura doib ic tabairt a n-aighthi for an Tésail.
Tuccait tromcetha móra teinedh & toirnighe doibh ina n-agaid, co m-bitis na saignena tentide for foluamain os a cendaib fo delbaib columan mor & sparti & troisti n-adbal, cona leicctis a rusca d'osluccud doib, & conat comgeontais in conair for a cingtis.
No láetis na saignenasin a círa do cathbarraib na curad & a cobradha da sciathaib & a n-elta da claidhmibh & a slenna da slegaib.
Atcitis delba na m-biast & na nathrach neimide for foluamain os a cennoip.
Atcitis na saithedha beach & foichedh for foluamain imma mergedhaib uasa & is invechtain no toccbatis na mergedha sin o talmain, acht siett 'na m-bratachaib marbda merbhlighthi re crannaip na sleg sin, co fortuightis cinna na laech, & a m-braengal dhér & ciamaire ic siled eistip noco rancatar in Tésail.
Ro triall Poimp 'arsin idbairt dona deibh, ocus tuccad tarbh torav tiughfhormnach taeipslemain da shaigidh, ocus intan rob ail a bualadh imsae for dasacht fo maigib na Tesaili & ni thoraig for cúlaibh doridhisi, conach frith nach n-idbairt occo dona deiph 'arsin.
Nirbo h-amlaidh sin do Cesair, immorro, acht rainic leis fobail gach idhbairt fo tarat laim isin lo sin.
Tuccait taidhbhsina imda doibh isin lo cetna.
Tadbas amh do droim dibh, sliabh Pind & sliab n-Olimp do beith ic coimrith docom araile comma rainic comrac a n-aein-inad doib.
Tadbas do dreim ele dib dano sliab Eim do sluccadh-badudh isin talmain sis co m-bai i comharda frissna glendaibh batar imme.
Tadbas do dreim dib dono srotha cro & fola do beith ic snige dar lar glenna Bebis.
Tancatar dorchatae dermarae doib isin glinn cetna conat coimgeonadh nech dibh agaidh araile.
No artraigtis foiscte & fantaisi na carat batar marba reimi-sin doib isna dorchoib sin.
Ba faelid iet-som dona h-airrdibh sin, ar indar-leo is edh ro tircansat doib co m-beitis i traiti ic airleach na carat m-beo batar i farrad Cesair.
Becc a ingnadh cena buaidred cetfaide for in droing sin ed ón an lucht ic nach raibe do saegul acht edh risi roistis i comfocraib longphuirt Cesair nammá.
Ba soideithbir do miledaib in catha sein aichni for a airrdibh, ar gach aird isin doman i m-boi duine do lucht na Roma do rat aichni for a airrdibh & no bidh co toirsech dubhach dobronach, ar ni fitir cia linmairecht da cairdib do faetsad i cath mor maigi na Tesaile isin lo sin.
Masat fira na forcetla dano do reir cumni na senori, do rala in la sin fisid firamnus i tulaig Eugan eiter sruth Appoin & sruth Timaip i crichaib na Veneti.
Ro gab ic taidbred inn aeoir uasa cred do foillsigedh dó in saignen nó in rith renn nó in dath greini, acht is edh asbert:
‘Dia friss cidh innso?’ olse.
‘Ni tartamar-ni barsamail in lai-si riam.
Atathar icc denam mórgnimha éiccin ann.
Ni fuil a samail acht amal bidh isin uair-si fen no beitis buidne Poimp & Cesair i comrac.’ fil ann tra acht as derb-deimin nar, delb in t-aicnedh riemh oenla ica m-beitis airrdena in lai-si.
Deithbir on, ar ni tainic deis na Dilenn oenla no cutrumaighedh frisin laithi-si im dith & im dilghenn, im marbadh & im mudhughadh in cinedha doenna, & da m-beitis fiside & fireolaig ica feccadh in gach aird imeachtraigh secnon an domuin, ni raibe ann aird no inad asna bad forreli na h-airrdhe aigthidhe adhuathmarae ro batar isin aer os cinn na Tesaile in la sin.
Dia friss tra roba derscaightech na daine sin & ro bu ainmesarda a nert & a smacht & a cennacht & a cumachta.
Ro bo fortren fata fairsing forlethan, a flaithius & a forlamhas, a nert & a recht & a rigi, intan ro linadh cruinne in talman fotha & an muir ina timcill & in nem & an t-aer uaistib do sighnibh & do derbairrdibh a cath & a cosccar, a n-olc & a n-aidedh, ocus antan as urgairdiugud menman ocus airpeitiud aiccnid la h-uile dainib in domain co coitcend beith icc innisin a scel ocus a cosccur ocus a n-aided in locta sin doib ina fiadnaisi o sin cusinniu, ocus as doig ni ba luga bus airpeitiud fos & bus urgairdiugud co bruinne m-bratha ocus co forcend in betha.
La sodain rancatar na sloig dar glend Bebis immach, & ro gabsat a m-belgip belsalchaiph ocus i m-belataib imcumcaib in glenna co forscailti for fairsingiugud fo cetoir for tetib & for tulcaib, & for tuaitemrachaib in talman, & for rennaib reidip roglanaibh, ocus for cnocdruimnibh comardaib clair maighe moir na Tesaili.
Ro thatni grían-taitnem na greine i tuile a delraidh ocus a ruithne friu, curbo milled da forcsin & da radharc.
Ro curit annsin bollsairedha & callairedha & ardmair & armainn & aes furocra o Poimp for tossachaib na sliged d'imfostadh & d'imfuireach na sluag re taisbenad a socraiti ocus re corugud a cath ocus re h-airem a m-buiden ocus re h-ordugud a n-imtechtae.
Ro bai imfuireach mór forru-som annsin ic rim a miled ocus a mergedh, ocus ic taispenadh a tuath & a tinol, & ic glinniugudh a comairle im corugud a cath.
Ro coidh an t-áirdri Poimp fein, & drong adbal da ardmaithib immi d'ordugud a slogh ocus do corugadh na cath annsin.
Ro ba deiglin taburta catha immorro do ríg aili in lucht ordaigti ro boi immailli ro Poimp annsin.
I S e so amh ordughadh do ronsat ed ón ro h-airmedh leo for tus a socraide n-dilis buddein & tinol an t-senaid Románaig & teglach Poimp cona maithib, ocus ro h-ordaighit occae ceitre catha & ceitre cath do gleiri miled & curadh cengailte fo n-armgaisged & dá mili traighthech i fosugud na h-irgaili ocus a n-uct inn imbualta & a tuinigti an catha.
Tuccad Lentulus in consul & ceitre legiona lanmora do raignib laech lanchatut immaille fris i m-beind cli an cata.
Tuccad Doimit tuseach cathrach Corpin isin Etail cusin lin cetna immi i m-beind deis in catha.
Tuccad Scip mac Scip Affracain & mórthinol na Cilecda immi i n-airenach a etermedoin in cathae cetna.
I S e an Scip sin bar Affraici dar eis Poimp iertain.
Tuccadh scellbolcc dluth doscailte do sciathaib gacha dathae isin m-bith, co m-bidh corranbac in sceith for araile im mórtimchill in cathae.
Tuccait a eitedhae catha imme arsin ed ón dc.
marcach isindara h-eiti dibh
dc.
isin eiti araill.
Poimp fein immorro cona senatoraib & cona consulaip ocus cona centuribh & cona thuseachaibh & cona trebannaibh ocus co n-ardmaithib in t-senaid arcena immaraen friss ina m-broin moir marcsluaig inmalla forustu for cert-druim in catha moir sin.
Rígh immorro & tuisig, flaithi & forlamhaidhe, cuingid & coraid in domain batar maraen re Poimp nir' cumcetar rimh no airem a socraiti re n-imatt & re a línmairecht.
Nir fetad catha do denamh dibh, acht gach dirim imo flaith, & cach curi immo coraidh, & gach tuath immo tuiseach, ocus gach buiden immo ruirigh & gach roslogh i morig fein for leith amal ro gabsat in mag, acht ro boi oensmacht forra o Poimp ed ón na remtiastais in morcath ro h-ordaigedh inn airis imbuailte in catha moir.
Tancatar iaram dronga aidble dib im slógadh na Capatoci & im marcshlógaib insi Point don dara leith dona Romanchaibh ettarra, & sligti uisccemla in tire ocus locsrota Eniph.
Tanccatar immorro don leith aili dib for reidib in maigi moir na h-uili ri ocus tuseach tancatar i toiritin Poimp cona mórsochraidib leo ed ón lucht in airthir uile ota in Innia sair, ocus occbadh na h-Aisia & slog na h-Affraicce ocus fir na n-innsedh do muir Torrien.
Ro asccnatar rempu iarom fon samail sin ina ceim cobsaid & ina reimim forusta inmalla imtechta for certammus longphuirt Cesair cach n-direach.
Nirbo h-obadh augra immorro in ceim sin.
Mairg rig & sluag cena ro innsaigh da deoin in net n-gribi-sin & in lasair teinedh ocus in neim nathrach ocus in fochla leoman & in saebhchoiri icc sluccad ocus in teidm dígla & in damna áigh & an t-ágh urlamh ro h-innsaiged annsin ed ón longphort Cesair, & anraid na h-Eorpa & iartair in domain maraen fris ann.
I S edh do eccaim do Cesair dano in la sin, beith tria tecmang & tre turcora conaigh airechtus mór do beith aicci co maithib a muintiri imme forsan faithchi forreid bai for lar an longphuirt. aris ed ba gnaithbes gabala longphuirt la Romana dogrés ed ón múr do claidhe ina thimcell & faithchi urfolam fo ercomhair airechtais for larmedhón in longphuirt.
Bai in la-sin dano airechtus for larmedón a longphuirt ic Cesair, uair rob ail lais drechta mora da muintir do cur do buain arbann cuicci fo glasgortaib in tire, ar nir'bo saidbir loin lucht a longphuirt-siumh intansin.
Batar a n-eich & a n-echradha urlama in imtechta occo, & a mergedha toccbalta forra fo comair na sligedh & inn imtechta docom glasgort an tire.
A m-batar ann ic forcsi & ic midemhain for lergaibh lebra lainreidhe in maigi moir for a n-agaid, con-facatur in magh fata forfairsing barclan do slogaib ocus siat ic mall-asccnam ina n-dochum gach n-direch.
A m-batar ann dano ic fordescain in maigi cetnae confacatar na h-eltadha aighthidhe adhuathmara os na slógaib, ocus na h-onchona craebhacha cróderga craesforlaiccti, ocus na h-aquili imluatha ilbreca eitecha etarbuasacha, ocus na mergedha ailli allata inncaela eirblecha iarlepra, & na bratacha snathcaine sreabanncaela sroil, & na fannbreiti fata fannscailti do shítta & do siric ocus do sinsnath, co n-delbaib mathgaman & leoman & nathrach ocus ilpiast anaichnid inntibh uili, co m-brechtradh druadh & idhal & aincreidmech ina n-uamannaib do métugud a n-adhuatha ocus a n-urgraine.
A m-batar ann iarom ic forcsin in maige cetna co facatar na dairedha dluithi digainne dergruada cona lasraibh tenedh os a cennaibh ic dirged da saiged ed ón ruadcrandgal finnfota inneldirech na sleg semneach slindgerglan, ocus na n-gonfainne niadh, & na laigen lethangorm, & na craisech crainnremar crofhairsing ic a cruadhcongmáil re gealguaillib na curadh, cona cennoip solsib saignenta forru, co l-lasair taitnem teinedh os na cendaib sin.
A m-batar ic forcsin in maigi cetna confacatar na h-amdabcha adhuathmura aighrete gacha datha, & na crobuailte bodba fo aendeilbh timcill ic snamasccnam darsin mag da saigidh ed ón buailte cengal & ocus cath-caraiti curadh do sciathaibh aillib aengelaibh, ocus do sciathaib engachaib uaineccdaib, & do sciathaib dubhdorcaib deilgnechaib, & do sciethaib imelchaini aladbreacca, & do cromsciathaib odraib aighthidhibh, ocus do sciathaibh breacbuidhi buaballdaib, ocus do crannsciathuip corcurdaib, ocus do sciathaiph breachtnaighte cacha datha isin doman osin amach.
A m-batar ann ic forcsi in maige cetna confacatar na cetha ana imtroma & na casracha ana imluat ha & na cethae dluithe degtroma i fritseoladh na sluag ina n-agaid amal silti snéidhi snechtaide, nó amal clumha coilctech re gaeith ed ón in cuvur-uanfadh anal-utmall etarbuasach ic tepersain cun anadh gan urespaidh a gingobaiph & a h-eocurbelaibh na n-ech n-allmarda n-airdermach, & na serrach sulchruinn sronfairsing seitfedach, & na midach mórmongach nertmar n-diumsach ic meilbleith a fiacal ocus ic fosheinm a n-glomar ocus a srianmirenn ara luinne leo a fuirech nó a n-imfostadh gan a lecon doreir a menman ocus a móraigentae isan magh.
A m-batar ann ic forcsin in muighi cetna co facatar edh a forcsi & a radairc don muig mor barclan do shlógaib & do grinnib ocus do leigionaibh, do buidnib, do drongaib, do dhirmannaib, do miledaibh, do cathaib, do cuirib, do cetaib ed ón sloig na n-insi & na h-Affraici & na h-Aisia & inn airthir 'na poiplib deilighthi & 'na cinedaibh scailti scamhanta.
Gach ri cona socraiti, ocus gach córaidh cona curi, ocus gach toisiuch cona tuaith fein ime, can rimh gan airem gan airdmes forru, acht amal ba barclan in mag uili dip.
A m-batar ann ic forcsi in maigi cetna co facatar da saigidin lebarbroin lanmoir lethanfota d'óccaib fon armgaisgedh ocus a n-ucht uili friu i fairsingi achaid, ocus a n-dlus fidbaidhe, ocus a met cathrach no caisteoil ed ón an senadh righdha Romanach arna n-ordugud & arna corugud ed ón na h-ocht catha ocus na ceithri fichit cath do curadaibh cengailte ocus na da mile traigthech 'na tri lorgaibh, druim ar druim, co m-beradh gach lorg fri araile dib ina m-buaili bodba ocus ina cro catha & ina n-innellaigh, cona tuighi do clethcoilltibh aigh, ocus d'fidbadaib neime, & do slegaib crainnleabraib snasta slinnsolsi uastib, cona sonncaistel cotat comdaingen do cuarsciethaib cetraimteachaib ocus do chlarsciathaibh aladaib uachtarfairsingaibh moraib ina timchioll, comba lor d'urgairdiugudh a n-aisgin indara fecht re h-imat dath n-examail a n-arm & a n-ecradh & a n-otgadh, re gristaitnem & re gleordealradh na greini ina certagaid friu, re somaisi na mergodh & na minn rigda roietroct, & na cathbharr cruan-cumhtaighthi, & re geildergi gruadh na miled amal cnaim oeingel elifainti iar na tumma i corcur, & re solusruidedh na saerchlann soicineoil os bilib na sciath ar n-ergi na ruaidgrisi romoiri sin in aigtibh na n-anradh n-astarach re h-annaime a n-imtechta & re cumga na crobuailedh cathae i m-batar ic mallascnam in maigi fonnglais foruaine darar' cingset.
In fecht n-aill immorro ba lor d'uathbas & cridenbas a forccsi re h-aduath na n-arm & re h-uathgrain na sochaidhe ocus re fostacht a ceime ocus re treisecht a tocimme ocus re h-admaire a n-innill; re n-aidble ocus re n-imatlinmuirecht fodein ocus re met ro gapsat fotha don muigh reidh rofairsing forsa rabatar, ocus dano risna h-ammaitip aerdaip ocus risna h-eltadaib adhuathmuraib do duibenoip dorchaidhib batar ina n-urlenmain ic urnaidhe a fola ocus a n-apaige n-escoman d'fagbail gan uiresbaid in-ellach in morcatha ocus inn otharligib na n-anradh isin armaig 'ar trioll.
La sodain tra doeccaim menma slóig Cesair forra, ocus gabait co feithmech fuireacur, & co sanntach sodeithbhirech ica sirdecsain.
Ro airigh Cesair fein sin dano, ocus tucc a agaidh forsin magh, ocus ro dech uadh in morsocraitisin Poimp, ocus tucc da uidh annsin co tucsat na dei do inní ic a m-bai siriarraid reime sin ed ón a daethain catha ocus irgaile d'fogbail.
Ocus o 'tconnaic asrus a fogbala aicci ge rancus a les anad re comairli ocus re h-imradhadh mor do denam re h-ucht in turcairti tarla ann.
Araisin ro gab-som for neimhsnim do denam de ocus ic a cur for dail m-bicc & for neimfni.
Acht cena o ro airigh ina menmain in guasacht romor i n-imfoccus dó ed ón a dith fein nó dith Poimp i traiti isin lo sin fein co cinnte, & nachfitir a deimin cia dib diar'bo foicsi maith no saich, ro la socht mor fair, ocus as suaill narbo nar leis a n-derna do dánacht gloir ocus do boccacht urlabra asa conach cathae co n-icci sin. arro lae a menmu i cumtabairt dermair ocus inn imresain adbail ic tur brethnaigthi ettorra fein ocus Poimp, ar intan do beired da aire mét soinmigi ocus soconaigh Poimp ros-linadh oman ocus imeccla in catha do srainedh fair fein.
Intan do beired da oidh, immorro, a degtoictin fein ocus a conach catha ni leicced nach snimh no nach n-ureccla fair.
Nirbo cian do Cesair for in abairt sin antan ro ling a detlacht ocus a danatus fein ann, gur' baidh ocus gur' dibustar inn uamun ocus in cumtabairt ro bai ina menmain.
Ocus ro éirigh i medon in airechtae ocus ro spraic a laim forsna slogaib do thai ocus d'urestecht friss, ocus is edh asbert friu:
‘A degmuinter,’ ol se, ‘as sip ro tairbir in doman fum-sa cusindiu.
As sib mo toicthi ocus mo conach ocus mo dei adartha.
I S frib berim a buide gacha maithiusa fuarus riem.
Do riacht anois cuccaib inní ic a fuilti iarraidh ocus togha co fata ocus co menic anallana ed ón in cath mor, ni h-e riccthí a les d'iarraid festu acht an conach do cosnam a l-loss bur lamh & bur n-arm, ar is in nertaib bur riged ocus i cruas bur cridedh & i m-bonnaibh bur n-guailled?
ata mo conach-sa no mo dochonach, ocus mo métugud no mo lagdugud co brath isin laithi-si in morcatha.’
‘I S essidhe an la ro gellsapair dam-sa icc tonnaib srotha Rubicon intan ro atcurius a sidh for in senadh Romanach ocus for Poimp.
I S e an la cetna-sa dano isa sailecta inar' gabsam ar n-armae ocus ima tuarccaib-sium ar coccad ocus ar n-eissidh o tosach uile.
I S e in la cetna-sa dano in la frisi n-urnaigsium-ni do tabairt duin na m-buadh ocus na somiad forfemid Poimp & an senadh do denam duinn ar n-ar torrachtain don Roim o gabail na Gaillia ocus in iarthair uile.
I S e in la cetna-sa dano do bera tighi ocus crodh & clanna, mna ocus muinteri daib, ocus denaidh calma ann.
I S e in la cetna dano do bera feranna forfairsiunga daib fri fulang bur senndatadh ocus bur senordhachta, & denaidh calma ann.
I S e an la cetna dano do bera scur ocus crich ocus forcend ar bhar soethraip ocus ar bar sloighedaib, ocus denaidh calma ann.
I S e an la cetna dano do bera lucht an domain fuib tria bithiu, na lemhtar athcath no aitdeabaid daib in cein mharthai, & denaidh calma ann.
I S é an la cetna dano do bera cach fuibh ocus sibh os cach, & denaidh calma ann.
I S e an la cetna bus fiadhu forgill & bus íudic breithi etram-su & Poimp dus cia uainn bus firencha tuarccaib in coccaid-seo, & bidh follus do cach sin as inti clofitir ann, & bennacht uaim-si foraibh-si narab misi sin.’
‘Masa dam-sa dano ro soichsiubair in Roim fechtus aili co n-armaibh ocus co teintib, ocus masa dam do ronsaidh gach maith riamh sechnoin an domain, denaid inndiu cathugud seitriuch duthractach damh, ocus dedhlaidh sib féin, ocus meis frisin cair & frisin míclu liít in senadh forain ed ón co m-badh sinn badh cintach ann cusindiu.
Ocus dano cenco n-derntai calma ar mo daighin-si, denaidh cid eiter ar bur n-daigh fein, co m-be bar sairi ocus bar commus féin agaibh, ocus rige for cach.
Ocus cidh amhus, no oicctigern, no cathardha becc dinnim dereoil do gnethe dim-su, no cipe ni fodalta eili isin bith, dar mo breithir, i fiadhnaisi m'arm, ni fil a obadh occom-sa acht co b-fagbaithi-si deigbethaid namma.’
‘Ata araill aile ann dano.
