Na loccadh ocus na forlaighed foraib-si itir an t-imat adbal & in t-socraiti di-airmidhe ut atcithe chuccaibh, ar is uathad dib-sin as luct gaisccid nó engnama acht sgolaide Greccacha & lucht foglama leaburda ocus saerealadhan a n-urmhor, ocus as ing mas eol doib a n-airm d'imurcur.
Madh a n-imluadh immorro i n-agaid miled ni combtig co m-badh eol daib.
Ni aile da lot dano ed ón ni lucht oenbérla iat, ocus ni tabair cinedh dibh aichne for glor araile, ocus teichfit a n-urmor lasna cétgairibh i cétuair, ar ni duthract leo anadh fri calma do denamh is incath.
Bidh uathadh accaibh-si immorro ro sia cathughad cathurda do gnim, acht beith ic díthiugud na cinedh n-echtrand sin, & ni cath cathardha eissidhe, ar as namait & as bidhbaidh bunaidh do Romanchaibh iat.
Ocus o ro fetabhair a m-beith amal atbeirim-si frib, tabraidh bur n-agaidh for tus for in morsocraiti sin locta in domain, & narab d'anadh occo cena, ocus na damaidh cathugudh no comlann doib, acht eirgid trempu gan fuireach ocus trascraidh remaibh iat, ocus denaidh fodhail ocus brígh m-bicc dibh. arteichfit remaib fo cetoir, gorrabh a fiadhnaisi la cach 'arsin conadh becc m-buada nó m-buadhnaisi badh denta do Poimp de, cidh menic tisadh don Roimh 'ar clod cinedha dib sein.’
‘Ni h-inann ocus tisaidh 'ar clod na Gaillia ocus lochta Lochlainne ocuus insi Bretan.’
‘In sailti-si fein dano in mor a brígh la lucht airrthir Assia atat annsud cipe uainn-i bes i cennus na Romha nó i r-righi in domuin, ocus ni mor itir ón ar, dar mo breithir-si, is lainbecc da fuil bad dutracht lasin occlach do lucht na h-Armmeni do thodail ass ic cosnamh ríghi na h-Etaili do Poimp secham-sa, ar as becc nach coimhmisccais leo sinn uili 'nar Romanchaib.’
‘Acht cena is bes coitcenn fon doman uili conidh misgaisiu lasna tuathaibh na tigerna clechtait forru innat na tigernada aili, conadh airisin sáilim-si nach diliu leo sút Poimp itussa fadhein.’
‘Mad misi immorro tuc mo conach damh mo teccmáil alt in lai-si eter lamaib tairisi mo muintire dichra duthrachtaige fadein, ocus deghaichne caich ic arailiu uainn, ocus fis a n-deglamaigh-sium accum-sa isna cathaib crodha ro cuirsit maraen rim ic gabáil na Gaillia & iarthair in domain.’
‘Ni fhil uaib milidh nach tabair mo cluassa aichne for builli a claidim nó for fidren a fogha ic a diubraccudh cen co taidhli mo roscc a taidhbred fein.’
‘Atcimsi foraib dano na comarthadha ocus na h-airrdena na tardsat breicc immum riam, & as follus dam & as cinnti lem co clofidhe for m-bidhbada tresna h-airrdhenaibh atcither damh foraib ed ón atcim gruamdacht in for n-gnusib, & urspraic in for n-aigtibh, & tomaithemh romor in for rosccaibh.’
‘Atcither dam innossa fein im menmain na srotha cro & fola ic snighi im fiadnaisi, & mededha maelderga na saerclann ic saltarnaigh forru, & maithi an t-senaidh for anamtaigh & for ochursnam ina cru fein ocus ina fulradh.’
‘Amae atúsa innossa ic lainmilled noith immum fein comor ed ón sib-si for dasacht icc iarraid bar leicctiu don cath & misi ica for fostadh.
Cidheadh ar ai mataidh-si ocus logaidh dam-su in fuirech sin, ar ni ar for misccais fostaim-si sib, acht ara mett as uraibnius menman dam bith ica for n-accallaimh re febus na sailechtan fil lim.’
‘Nach faicthi me ar crith & ar comboccadh re mét mo degsailechtan, ar ni tartsut na dei riamh maithius mar so i faicsi duinn intan na fil etrainn & cach maith duthraicmit fein d'fagbail acht inn rae-machaire becc-sae nammá.’
‘Biad-su fein innossa co l-langairit ic scailed ocus ic tidnacul daip-si ina fil do chrodh i l-longphortaibh na righ ocus na tuseach ocus na tuath n-echtrand atat annsud.’
‘I S cinnti iarum loighidhecht in coccaid-moir si d'fagbáil indíu nó a pian dano, & dia m-bad í a pian badh urlam, tabraid-si ar bur menmain a fuilengmais-ne do cenglaibh, do cuibrigibh, do crochaib, do cestoip.’
‘Décidh lib amal no bretfatis mo baill-si ocus no berta mo cenn-su for cathairib in oenaig isin Roimh.
Napadh ingnadh lib-si sin, ar dalta do Sill Poimp, & ni ro coiccill side do duine riam, ocus ni mo no cocceladh Poimp.’
‘I S e for snim-sa fil form-sa desin cena, ar, dar mo bréithir, i fiadnaisi na cath i comrac imberaid an lam-sa fein bas form-sa, manip me cloes in n-irgail-si, ocus, a dei adurthae, cena inte bhus uille tarbha do chach gurab é cloes ann, & inti na digéla ara comchathardhaib arna clodh a teccmail i cinn catha ris reime.’
‘Ni h-ed sin do róine Poimp frib antan tarraidh imcumhang na Eperi foraib, acht ro mudaigh can díthcel i tarraidh da bur muintir ann.’
‘Madh misi immorro, bennacht uaim foraib-si, a occa, na h-imridh neach uaib a lama for an lucht teichfius remaibh, acht gurab é gabthai amal comcatharda dhaib inti teichfius remhaib ann.’
‘Na tabraid coicill d'athair nó do brathair, nó do carait no do comfhuilidhi airet beiti a n-aighthi foraib, acht buaidridh iatt, & geibid na claidhmi dar a n-aigthib doip, & gach oen airisfes frib gabaidh amhail dergnamait é, & cidh cara fire bes ann clanntar an claidemn ina loing m-bronn amail bidh namha uathanaichnidh no teccmadh frib.’
‘Denaidh eirge do ghabháil bar n-arm festu,’ ol Cesair, ‘ocus étid co h-oponn siph & innsaigid bar n-inadha catha & comlainn, ar ni riccim-si a les bar n-ordugud.
Ni h-aichenta damh for n-inadha catha ina daib fein.
I S menic ro coraigsiubair sibh isna h-inadaib sin docom catha docair maraen frim-sa cusindiu, ocus intan ro sia agaib co dul asin longphort immach innossa na saigidh docom a dorus itir ardaigh na scailter & na tanaighter for coirighthi catha ic techt tar doirsib imcumcaib an longphuirt & dano na teccat for m-bidbhaidh co h-opann o bur cúl chuccaibh, ar ni da saigid atát dorsi an longphuirt.
Trasccraidh fuibh iaram fal na leiti-si as nesa doib-siomh don longphort, & denaidh cessaigdroicet comdaingen fo for cosaib de, & linaid clasacha in longphuirt do múraibh ocus do criaidh na clodh filet impo, cor-risat na sloigh ina coirighthibh catha inn oeinfecht for reid in maighi dar in longphort immach.
Na dechaidh a bhecc d'iarmairt don longphort-sa, acht cosnaid co cruaid & co seitrech in longphort lansaidbir co lain-imat cacha maithesa ann asa teccatt in slógh troch ut da bar saighidh.’
Aitiuscca Cesair co n-icce sin, & is inbechtain ma tairnic leis deredh a imacollma intan ro eirgetar in slogh uile eirge n-aeinfir inn aeinfecht dochom a m-both & a caprach & a pupall, d'étiudh a l-luirech & do gabail a n-gaisccedh & d'airitin a n-arm, & do thochaithemh a prainne laithidhi re techt i cenn mórgnim & mórsaethair inn imbualta & erghaile in catha moir.
Ba maith leo-som in celmaine do rala doib annsin ed ón a n-armu & a m-biada do teccmail co coimhirlam da saighid.
Gabait iarum na slóig ic tocaithem a prainne laithidhe co h-enda etarbuasach an-b-forusta annsin: araill dib ina suide, ocus araill aile co h-urchrom eccobsaidh os a m-bordaib, ocus a n-urmor uile ina sirsesam ar dorsibh a pupall ocus ar belaibh a m-both.
Cesair féin immorro ni ro fogluais asin maigin i tarrustair e, acht tuccad prainn mesardha do, & ro tomail re h-ed n-athghairit í ed ón a teora laechmírenna d'feoil geisechtaige la teora deogha fina Falernecda immaille Tuccsatt a fianlach frithalma a arm timcell catha co Cesair gurrus-etestair é forsin tulaig i m-medhon in mórlongphuirt.
Ro gap iaram da assan aeingela iarnaidhe imma dib sliastcolpthaibh.
Siat glanta gleorda glainidhe.
Siat niamdha nemmergidhe cona m-bondbaigib dilsi degfuaighthe druimlethair fotha, cona cassnaithchib caiti cruaidhsnithib coimtenna columdai ic imfostadh a n-uruachtar & ic cassadcengal a cuarbel im certmedon da sliasat inn airdrigh.
Tuccad a comgha cnis & a corpditin catha imme ed ón cathluirech dluith drolach dualach degfigte derscaighte d'úriarann.
Ba din doiti, ba coimet cinn, ba comga cuirp, ba h-anacal anma, ar ni cumgad rind no faebhur a tolladh no a tesccadh.
Deithbir disi on ar fuair a h-urgnamh co h-ollomhda augdurdha, & a fobairt co frichnamhach firglic a l-lendaib inmara olarda itharda ola indara fecht ann do boccadh & do righniugadh, do suntugadh ocus do sofilltiugud a adbair.
In fecht aile immorro no foibrigti do crúadugadh & do chaitiugud a drol a grethaib gleorda glanusci & a sruthlintibh lindglanaip linduaraibh & a h-aibhnibh aillib ochurglassa firtuaiscirt Lochlann i coicrichaib ammritib etoirtechaib ind uarda adhuair aigreta bathuaidh.
gurbo menmarc la Cesair nach boi i m-mórsocraiti Poimp oenarm catha no coemsadh aendrol da drolaib do tesccad.
Tuccad a caithchris cathae & comlainn im Cesair dano.
Clarchris columdha glaeta glolethair sin do druimlethar teora n-daimseicheth n-dartada arna n-acomal & arna n-daingendluthachadh do glaed & do sechim & do bitumin.
Clarland cummaide credhumha i comfhata & i coimlethan in creasa sin 'arna comdluthachad friss.
Clar airgit oeinghil co n-aireccur oir forloisccthi fair da somaisi iar n-imechtair.
Fiartarstnana orda & airgidhe, & cach treas tarstnan de iarann aithlegta oeingel 'arna coimeccur on burd co araile de.
Fiacalcorrana croma creduma isin dara cind de.
Stuagluba umhaidhe dar braigdibh na corrán sin isin cinn araill re h-iadhadh ocus ro h-oslaccadh im cnes ind airdrig, co n-gabadh in caithcris sin dó ó filltibh a occsall co l-lethan a les.
Ro cuir Cesair a claidem orduirn inóenaigh uadh annsin, & ro congladh a cruadhclaidem comlainn for a cliu i forciupul an cressa sin ed ón claidem cruaidh corr-cotut claislethan colgdha coilgdírech cona croseltaibh comdaingni comtairisi de iarann secda sithrigin sechtlegta fair, co cetheora traigedh toimside trenmiled o ta a urdorn co a ind.
Teora basae laoich ina lethet.
Do raighnibh & do togaidib & d'firdingnaibh na lann laingér lanchruaidh lainrigin lancotut Lochlannach in claidem on frisna geibed iarn na cruaidh do cruaidhiph na cruinne, na tinne do tinnib in talman, na crann, na cnaim, na carrac, na daingen do daingnibh an domain No stuaglubadh Cesair in claidem sin inn aimsir ainesa, co tibead a inn re a urdurnd.
No sceinnedh-lingedh in claidem ina coilgdírgi cetna doridisi re brafad sula no re luas menman duine, acht cena ba iar cein máir no tairised don cressnughadh ocus don crithnugudh no gabad fair ic asccnam ina dirghi fadein.
Ba cosmail & ruitne greini fri h-usce a taitnem ocus a taidhbredh airet no bid for a crith.
Mairid in claidem sin fos i n-aigrecht athri & senathri ina set maic & úi & innúi, ic sil Iuil Cesair inn inniumthigh na Roma.
Cach imairecc catha cusa tocaibther é ni congabur fris.
Ro gabad immo cend dano dar maelat a luirighe seachtar corrchathbharr círach crúandathach serigh sronach sogabaltae do iarann aithleghtha orchumtaighthi, cona sronlainn imlethain iarnaidhe, co cumtach credumha fuirri dar agaidh an airdrigh ass, co n-ditned a srona ocus a beolu, co n-gabad i comarda fria a smeich.
Ceithre remurbuinne iarnaide ass dar a culu sectair, co cethra uvullmellaibh cruinni cruaidhiarainn for a cennaibh co n-gaptais na clobuinnedha sin o brud in cathbharra co bil an cresa boi immo do dhín ocus do dhitin a muineoil ocus a formna ar beimennaib na claidem ocus na loirgfhertus catha inn imtruastadh ocus a n-imforran an catha moir.
Da clobuinne caiti cethardruimnecha do iarann aithlegta cona n-inneoin-traigthibh tanaidib tuinighthi fothu i coimlenmain na luirighe for cechtar a da gualann, co cennaibh dlochtanacha dedhailti forta fri h-ocharchimsaibh an cathbairr cona tortromadh a troma for cond ind airdrígh ocus co n-ditned a bragait ar beimennaib na claidem da gach leth.
Caelchorrana cruaide cnes-tsaidthe & minslabraidh segda seimi seic-rigne ic fuaigel ocus ic imfostad in cathbairr sin i n-drolaibh na luirighe for cach leth, cona bai cumang a n-dedhailti no co n-deiligti do reir a aiccenta & a ailgesa iat.
Ro gabad a inncomurtha impirechta imma cenn iar n-uruachtar ed ón a minn righ.
Minn airgit oingil essidhe co mineccur oir deirg fair.
Sreth-linedha certa coiri comarda ina mórtimcill and do mairgreit & do cristaill ocus do carrmoccul & do lecaib togaidhib tiri na h-Innia airtheraigi arna tairmimurcur-sen i cropaiph en & ethaiti dar in sliab teintidhi a Partus Adaim co tir na h-Innia, cona cathairib credhumae fothu, cona snatheccur oir forloiscti ic a n-imfostadh.
Ceithri bennchobair aeingela findruine uasu.
Drumlorga don tinni corintecdai eatarru, tinni cumuscda sin do choimhlegad na n-uile tinne, eter iarann & stan & luaidhi & uma & or & airget, co n-deilb nathrach neimidhi for in drumluirg sin.
Bai do beachte & do bertnaigti & d'urspraicemlacht ocus do beoamlacht a innill atar la gach fer no teccmadh ar agaid Cesair as cuicci no lingfedh la gach ceim no cingfedh an t-airdri, gur vo métugud urgraine do-som sin.
Tuccait ina docom dano da craisech cennglassa ceinnlethna croremra co n-ocht slightib seimi slemanrignibh do brichtbuinnib neimhi arna sádudh i slesaib a slend, co slipadhcainnledh socarchain solusta saignentae fortae, co taitnem-taidhlig etroicht glain aigreta innta, co r-rinnaithi eoa for a n-innaibh, co n-aithgeri altan for a n-uillib, cona n-dib sabcrannaibh comfata coimreide coimdirgi coimremra inntu, co na n-dib n-iriellaib imdaingnib iarnaidhib fotha.
Balclan gelglaici Cesair i tacmaisi crainn gacha craisigi dibh.
Sect semann-clui uriarainn co remet medoinmeoir miledh in cach seim arna sadudh co cert comard tre cro-innsma gacha craisigi dib.
Tuccad a guaileiri catha co Cesair annsin ed ón cuarsciath amlach aladhbreac engach-bommanach uammannach uainecdha imelchruaidh ochtcobradach, cona sciathrach imcoimsi ecclannach imlethan do croicnib leoman 'arna lansuathad le, cona h-imelbord imdaingen iarnaidhe ina h-imtacmac, cona lethanloss inncael uiriarainn fuithi, cona socht focobradaibh cuasta corpchruinne cenncorra ina crobuailidh comaird comeccair immon fossadh-cobraidh moirmedonaigh, amail mintighi im rightheach, no amail tulcha urisle im ardchnoc.
Slatbuindedha coimremra coimthenna coimdirghi credumha co n-urcbalaibh allmurdha inta 'arna lecon co laindiles re lergaib droma in scéith, co n-gabtais co forscailti fiartarstna o cathairibh na cobradh for cach leth, co luptais a n-enna dar in m-bordbil iarnaidhe sin isin leth araill.
Delba loiscenn & leoman & draicci & grib n-ingnech & nathrach neimidi & anmanna n-ercoitech 'arna rinnadh co h-adhuathmur ind etarfasaighibh na crosbhuinnedh cengail sin ro batar tairis.
Brichtscribhenna briste catha 'arna scribadhrinnadh ind do lamaibh druad & idhal & arracht & ammaiti & ancraitmech, cu m-ba lor d'uathbhas do bidbadhaib timcaisin fair i r-rae catha no imairicc.
Mad cathcliath comhlainn immorro do congmail ina agaid, ni bai i n-aenaimsir fris fer folilsadh.
Étiudh cathae Cesair conicci sin. iat sloig Cesair dano, nirbo erisi in abairt an airet sin, ar in cein boi-siomh fein ic airitin a arm ro eitsiut in slog uile iat frisin re sin ed ón ro gabhait assana uaigti imdluithi iarnaidhi im cois-sliastoib curad occo ocus luirecha dluithi drolacha deghfhighthi d'uriarann im cnesaib, & corrcathbarrae coema cruan-cumhtaighthi im cennaibh, & caithcreasa clardhae columda brecrinnta bolgacha tenna tailci tairismecha im taebu.
Ro cengailti lannclaidme aithgéra ailtnidhi i truaillib togaidhib for a Ro toccbait dairedha digainne derg-ruadha do slegaibh slipta slemonchruaidibh & do chraisecaib ceindlethnaib & do mhanaisib dirgaibh druimnechaibh re gelguaillip curadh os a cennaib.
Ro coirgit leibenna dluithi daingne dithoghlaidhi do sciathaib caemae corcurderga a timcell gacha tuinti sloig diph.
Tanccatar fon tochim-sin & fon tuaruscbáil docum Cesair airm i m-bai for in faichthe forfairsingg i m-medon in mórlongphuirt.
Cach tuath & cach tinól ocus gach tocustal dib ina cathbuidhein dluith degcoirigthe for leith, ar nirbo miadh no maisi nó menmanradh la morslogh dib a sochraidi curadh do cummusc for slogh aile cenco taidhbred Cesair co suaichnidh iat & co n-ordaighedh fein gach degairecht dib ic a inad catha.
Ba mor in t-adbur metaigti menman do Cesair, anraidh na h-Eorpa d'ascin fon samail sin chuicci as gach aird da longphort, ar robtar imda aghmura na degslóigh do dechatar ann ed ón airecht indrigh allmurda argdha ardmenmnach allata innsaigtech Almaine.
Fianna ferrdha fuilecha fergacha forusta forrancha firduilge forniata Franc. mera muirnecha merdana mormenmnachae Morian.
Sluag serig seitrech subhach sommata so sochineoil soerclanda Saxan.
Buidhne bailci beoda briscci brigacha bunata bagacha baranda Bretan.
Anraidh occa fureacra aistreacha antronta aduathmura na h-Espaine.
Gaillmilid garga guinecha gaiscedhcha grenn-fholtacha na Gaillia.
Laechraidh lonn létmech luthmur lista lainmer leaburmongach Lochlann.
Oclaich ailli innelta escaidhe uretroma utmalla airdgnimacha na n-insi & airir inn occiain fuineta & iarthar-tuaiscirt an talman.
Cenmotha dano inn ail nemcumscaighthe & an t-uchtcnoc airdshlébhe & in t-all gaibthech glasmara & in murtonn móranfaidh, & an breisim bratha, & an buinne dilenn, & an diliu ic tuili, & in linn lacha icc linadh, & an ruadbuinni robartae ic rith, in crobuaile catha sin, in sithmuine sluagharmach, in damrad dichell dur-dhoiligh dasachtach ed ón trenfir tenna tairisi tatlaighti an talman & cruaidhmhilid cuartaighte na cruinni re cois Cesair, óccbaidh ainnsercc ainmin anacardach na h-Etaili sein, ocus righamsach romer rotren rodiumsach na Romanach fein ro batar do certleth re morsocraiti Cesair for faighthi in mórlongphuirt i muigh na Tesaili in uair-sin.
Atracht Cesair & drong mor da mhaithibh imme d'ordugud na slog sin & da n-airemh & do corugud a cath.
Nirbho h-adbal itir imat a sloig-siumh a n-agaidh na socraiti di-airmidhe ro bai icc Poimp da innsaigid, ar ni raibe siumh uile do socraiti coimlin ina m-boi do Románcaib amain i farradh Poimp. arrob í so nuimir sloig Cesair & airemh a socraiti in la sin ed ón ceitre cath do curadaibh cengailti & do miledhaib foglama gaiscidh & tricha míle traigtheach acht becc, & deich cét in cach mile dip-side, & aeinmili marcach.
Do-roine Cesair techta óencatha dibh-sin uile ina tri lorgaib druim ar druim, dluithi, daingne, doscailti.
Ro coirig a n-etedha catha impo ed ón marcach isin dara h-aircend dib & an coimlin cetna isin aircenn araill.
Tainic fein cusin tuinti trenfer tarrusair immailli fris ic ordugudh na slogh, gur gab a inadh catha & comlainn itir raignibh a righmhiled inn airenach a etarmhedhoin in catha moir-sin. arger'bo corp óenchatha uili iat-somh, araaisin is amlaid ro bai gach rí & gach roduine ocus gach tuisiuch togaidhi & gach flaith forglidhi dib co maithib a miled & a degmuintire dilsi & a trenfer tairisi ina crobhuailidh timcill immi budein da imdegail ar a escairdip & fri h-ursclighi inn agaid a bidbad daracend inn imforrain in catha moir.
'Arsin tra ro forcongairt Cesair fein forru o guth mhor fogluasacht fon samail sin a n-agaid a m-bidbad dar slisbord in longphuirt immach.
I S nemlesc ro freccradh in forcongra sin la h-anradha Eorpu in uair-sin.
I S mer, is dian, is discir.
is dasachtach, is dicell, is dicuinn, is deinmnetach, is tren, tenn, tulborp, tinnesnach in tulscan trenrethae tuccsat asinn inad sin immach do saigid a namat.
Cemadh Cesair gach aenduine dib, no cemad ic iarraidh airdcennassa na Roma no imperechta in domain do fodein no beith gach aeinfer aca, ni sanntaige & ni dichra & ni duthrachtaige no raghdais docom innas amal rocotor annsin, gur rucsat 'na n-urgluinib leo ina m-boi do gharrdhaib & do puiplib ocus do bothaib bronnfhairsiunga beloslaicti etarrae ocus slis an longphuirt, co n-dernsat cesaig-droichet fo a cosaib d'faltaibh in longphuirt & do muraib a clod, gur rancatar ina n-oenbroin aentadaig oen catha can dedhail, gan scailed, gan scainredh forta noco riachtatar dar clarmagh na Tesaili dar longphort immach, co ro dirighset uile co h-oponn inn oenuair & a n-aenfhabhull i frithagaid Poimp cona socraidi gach n-direch.
Poimp immorro, o duruacht side edh forcsena for longphort Cesair, ni ro impo a agaid & ni ro tairinn a righrosg, acht beith ic midhemain & ic mórdecsain for in longphort.
Nirvó cian in forcsiu do-somh cena intan atconnairc in sruthleccad sloigh lanmoir dar lethbord in longpuirt imach da saigid ed ón lucht an iarthair & occbadh na h-Eorpa, & na h-eltadha ilbreca imluatha uasta ed ón na mergeda iairlepra erplecha eiteacha, & na h-onchona corpchaela craesderga & na bratacha lethna lebra lanscailti, & siatt for meirbliugud, & for fiarlubgail & for foluamain lasna aithechaibh aerdaib, & la sithlaicc & la fidren na fanngaithi dus-fainic.
Atconnairc dano na dairedha dluithi digainni dergruada do slegaibh fota faebracha os a cennaibh, & a n-englumma aigh ocus a n-innech urbadha & a tinfas bodbae re bonaibh na sleg sin do tuagaib tana togadaibh & do biailib imlethnaib oenfoebrachaibh, & do bogadaibh bircennaip benncrommaibh & d'fogadaib feta fogablaigi & do beraip bodba birguirt-rinnaithe.
Atconnairc dano taitnem & taidhligh & taiblenaigh na circhathbharr cumtaighte ocus na minn righroedroct ocus na n-glasluirech n-gleordatha, & na n-inar n-orchimsach, & lainnrech na lethansciath lanmor ic a n-imurcur for uillennaib na n-anradh, occus ar rightib na rigmiledh, & ar guaillib na n-galgat n-gaisccedhach, & ar cle-corpaib na curadh comnart Atconnairc dano solustaitnem na saigetbolg socarchain arna suidiugudh for slesaip na soerclann cona fothaib clardaib fotae, cona forclib finnargait forta, cona m-belbordaibh credumha fríu, cona cruinnchimsaib coimfighthi do ilcenelaibh gacha partainge isin bith arna coimeccur co frichnamach firglic firamnas inn ochurdruimnib a n-uamann da cach leith, cona toimsib, techtaide do raignibh na saiget sainighthi arna n-ordugud inntu & do neoch na tailledh isna saigetbolgaibh dib batar ina topnasgoib cengailti for a caithcreasaibh na curad cona cennaibh corranda cruaidrinnaigthe forna saigtibh sin ar na foibredh aruilibh dracon ocus leoman & a neimib nathrach 'arna fothraccad a l-lennaib legtae in oir forloisccti, cona fethcrannaibh snasta slemnaigti inntib, cona fidradaibh brecrinnta forta, cona snathcenglaib seimrighnib sitaidhi leo, co lasfadh in t-aer i n-aimsir a n-diubraicte dib.
Ba h-i toimtiu Poimp for tus ica tencaisin fon toichim sin, co m-ba do buain glassgort na Tesaili no ragdais amal ba gnath leo gach dia reimi.
O 'tconnairc immorro na buidne niatae naimdide & na dirmanna aigh, & na h-ogo armtae & na caithcliatha cengailti coirigthe can fuireach, gan essnadadh, ic dirgad ina certagaid cuicci, tainic socht ocus imuamon aiccenta & cumsccughadh menman do, & ba celmaine móruilc do-sumh sin, ar ni tarla do turcairthi catha nó imairicc riam cuicci ni no cloechlodh a menmain no a aiccned, no do beradh nach n-urecclai fair.
Arai sin ni ro leicc-sium co forcsinach fair in uruamon mórsin, acht ros-folaig ocus ros-diamlaig in meiti ro cumaing.
Tanic iarum for in foghurcosta ard-aibinn allata aird-ermach tarrustair fai i timcill a slogh & a muinntire, & ro gab for a n-accallaim & for urail degaiccnid forta & calma do denamh, co n-ebairt friu:
‘A degmuinter,’ ol se, ‘is e so an la ic a fuilti iarraidh co fata.
I S e so an scur ro sirsiubair ar in cath cathardha.
Na bidh dicell occaibh festa, ar ni fil ni aili ann do gnether act dul i muinighin na n-arm ocus an iarainn.
Cach fer accaibh iarrus rochtoin co a crodh ocus co a muintir sired a l-loss imberta a claidim i trat-sa rochtain dia saigid, ocus gabaidh occaibh for n-uile maithiusa do bith i m-medon etraibh & bur namaitt for lar in maigi-si na Tesaile i trat-sa fein, & in dream occoinn as seitrige coisenas iat a l-los na n-arm as leo ragtait asin maig-si anos-sa.’
‘& as coraite duinn-e a cosnam co seitrech, ar issind ata for fir, & as linn coingenat na dei adarta. ardamad edh bad ail leo-sidhe mo flaithius do bein dim-su & righi an domain do tabairt do Cesair, do bertais bas dam-sa, ar asam senoir cena, ocus dano ni fil d'feirg na n-dei frisin Roim ocus fri poiplib an domain co coimetfatis meisi doibh damad form badh raen.’
‘Dar lim-sai dano tuccus lim accmaing maith tochair docum in maigi-siu indíu.
Tuccus lim amh maithi an t-senaidh Románaigh uile doneoch as béo dibh, ocus ina n-deachatar bas dib dano da mairtis indiu is lem-su no cuingéntais, ar is me ata for Tuccus lim dano cineda dí-airmhidhe airthir an domain ocus lucht a cathrach & a caistiall, conar' tinoil oenri ar amus oencatha riemh tinol a barsamla. aratat airm an domain uili, ota in poil deiscertaigh cusin poil tuaiscertaigh, immailli frim-su i trat-su cenmotha dano drecta uaiti ocus sceolanna terca filet do lucht iarthair an domain i f-farradh Cesair annsud, & nach faictisi fein nach filet side lin for fobarta-sa, & dar lim-su as edh as denta friu, a lecon cuccainn inar n-ucht & benna an catha do diabladh ina timchill cona raibe asrus eluda occo, & bidh lor uathad uainn-e d'imbirt lamh forthu 'arsin, ar ni fil la Cesair slógh folartnaighes dar n-armaib’
‘Biaid drong mor linn immorro ic na bia feidm aili isan cath acht a n-gaire catha do tabairt namma i cumma chaich.
Ata araill aile ann imman coir daib calmae do denamh ed ón tabraidh ar for n-aire & cretidh co daingen co fil an senadh Románach uili i trath-su, etir mnai & fer & occ & sen, ica for nertadh & ica for n-etarguide im calma do denam do coimhét a saire doib, & da n-etrain for cumachta Cesair.’
‘Ocus da m-beith accam dano asrus etarguide foraibh ina n-diaid-sin, nirbo ró nó furail lim me fein com' clainn & com commaim do luigi foen fo for cossaibh da for nertadh ar ammus maithiusa do denamh.’
‘Araill aile ann dano 'man cóir daib calma do denam, ar mana cloiti-si in n-imairecc-sa remum-sa indiu, biad-su im deoradh & im loingsiuch ó sunn immach.
Bidh ascaid cluichi la Cesair sin, & bid nairi dermair daib-si.
I NNí aile bad doigh ann immorro gorab túsca bas i m-belaibh-si innas mo bheth indíu im senoir ic foglaim foghnamha do duine aili, & me i n-airdrige an domain cusindiu.’
Ro toccbatar na h-aithescca-sin Poimp tra menmanna na miledh & aiccenta na n-occlaech atcualatar iat, & atract nert & fergluinne na righflaithi Roman ic a n-eistecht, goro linait uile iatt do saint ind imbualta & d'faelscudh imberta na n-arm, & rob ferr leo n-aeinfecht do dail ina m-belaib innas an ní bad oman no bad uireccla re n-airdrígh d'foghbáil co brath.
'Arsin ro gapsat na catha cechtarda co coimdichra comduthrachtach ic gressacht a muinteri do saigid araile, ar ro bai an ferg & omun a n-delighthi re a conach ic gresacht muinteri Poimp docom in catha.
Ro boi immorro sailechta na ríghe & ailgius fogbala in conaigh ic gresacht muintere Cesair ina n-dail, cona boi dichell na ailsecht ic slógh dibh ic saigid araili, & ni ro ansat don reimim roretha sin ro gabsat forru nogor' comfoiccsigset for aenre machaire, cona bai acht edh inurchuir eaturra.
O ro comfoiccsig iaram dona slógaib cechtarda cona bai acht edh athgairit a n-imdiubraicthi etarra, ro reccratar a lama da saighetbolgaib finndruinighthi.
Ro innletar a saighti snasta sruibgérai for srengsnáithib ciarthaib cotatrighnib a fidbac.
Ro coirighsit a coirrmera coilgdirgi i l-lathrib a taball tul-amais & i suaineamnaiph siti soidiubraicthi a fogad feig faebharglan, & a m-bir m-bodba, & a sleg snaidti slinngergorm.
Ro tennsat a traighthi re tulpartaib an talman.
Ro boccbertnaighset a trealma diubraicthi asa n-guaillibh.
Ro dhirighset radarca a roscc rinnger rinnsholus rena n-urchuraib do saighin a m-bidbad.
Tuccsat aichne for aighthib na n-aichenta fo a n-ercomair isin cath.
Ro aichensat amh a n-aithri & a senaithri, a m-braithri, & a macu, a clemnu & a coicceliu for a n-inchaibh ann.
O ro aithgensat immorro a cairdiu & a coicceliu & a comfuilidhe i cinncomair friu, ro shocht forta, & tainic caer chonnailbhe doibh ic faiscin na fircarat ar agaidh na n-urcor i n-airenach in catha.
Ro congbattar iarum a l-lama sinti fon dhiubhracad.
Ni ro cuirset cor dibh, acht amail tarraidh in tultapadh íett, ar nir' leicc in nairi doib impodh o a n-inadhaibh catha, & ni ro leicci in baidh doib dano gnimh inn imairicc i n-agaid na n-aichenta.
Ro batar fri re cian icon imdecsain sin for lathair in catha, & ni ro diubraic neach araile dib, acht a fogadha fuirighthi urlamha for a meraib, & a l-lama sinti oc irnaidhi na h-imgona, ar ni ro cumaing nech dib a arm do dibracad ria n-araili.
Fota badh coir na lama sin cenae d'fostadh & d'irfuirech can a l-lecon lasna gnima do ronta ar trill dibh. aras garuair gur' cuirset na lama sin docum bais in coimlin na fetfadh in cined doenna d'foccbail i n-oenaimsir co brath doridhisi cidh co sidamail no beitis o sin ammach, can cath, can coccadh, gan marbadh duine ettorru. ariss edh innisit auctair na Roman féin, conidh maithiss ro bai, & conidh aithisscel aisnesen flaitiusa na Roman riem dareis an catha sin, ar ni raibe less no cathair no caislen isinn Ettail nar'bo lan don occbaidh Romanaig co n-icci an la sin.
Batar fása immorro a n-urmhor o sin amach, & ni ro linait riam.
Cach cath & gach coccad, gach ár & gach airlech ocus gach easbaid dano do ratad isin doman riem, as co cath in lai sin no cuirthe ar bharamail.
As friss no samhlaighthe gach olc, & ni ro samladh sumh fri h-olc aile riamh.
Nir'bo h-ingnadh iarumh cemadh ainesccaidh la neach imlúadh a lam ann docom in catha sin.
Araisin tra frith neach no imluaided a lama re cach ann.
Dia friss cena, ro ba mór in mire, ocus rob adbal in miciall, & ro ba dana in dasacht don oenduini ro derlaic a arm & a lama d'imluadh & d'imbeirt re cach isinn uair sin, ocus Cesair fein cidh iter can a armu d'imbeirt ann.
Crastinus a ainm an fir sin, occlaech derrscaigthech do sainmuintir Cesair eside.
I S annsin iarum ro dírigh Crastinus a geilmer gaiscid i suainem in lethga letartaigh ro bai ina laim, conus-tuarccaib i comarda fria cluais, gurros-bocc ocas coros-bertnaigh, gorros-croith ocus coros crithnaigh, curros-cass ocus curros-certaig, go ro la rot rourcuir di ocus a fidren bodba ocus a siangaran aigh eiste, co tarla 'na seol neime ocus 'na h-innell urbadha í sech bil in sceith, dar brollach na luirighe, i m-mullach a ochta don fir bai for a inchaib isin cath araill, co n-deachaidh fot ferlama da crund cruaidh cethardruimnech for slicht a glaisiarainn trena druim siar sechtair ar tregdad a cridhi ina certmedon.
Cidh seitrioch foruair as can anmain foraccaib.
Nocurb athair gan clainn, immorro, ocus nocar cenn cen chuiri, ocus nocur túisiuch gan a buidin, ocus nocurb urfoccra fogla for fann in t-urcur sin tarlaic Crastinus, ar ni boi for ti diubraicthe do shluag Poimp no Cesair aenduine nar' aithris in urchor sin.
I S annsin iarum ro sinnitt a n-organa aigh, & a cuirn comairc & a caismberta catha leo ed ón a stuic ocus a sturgana ocus a n-adurca furfhoccra, ocus a cuislenna catha, gur ro buaidredh an t-aer leo do glaeidhbeicedhaigh na stoc slescam slemonsholus, d'ardgairmnigh & d'fogurnuall na n-adurc, do buiredhaigh ocus do comghair na corn & na cuslennach.
Ro eirgettar tra aiccentai na n-anradh & menmanna in morsluaigh leosin, ocus tuargaibset gaire móra os aird.
Ni ro toccbait reimi-sin no ina n-deghuidh isin doman gairi a m-barsamla sin.
Deithvir on, ocus sloig na cruinni domanda uili ic eighmigh inn aenfecht ar in aenmuig-sin.
Ro lin mac-alla na gairi sin mothra ocus caillti, fedha occus fidhneimhedha, tulchae ocus sleivti, aibni ocus essu, allu ocus inberai in tire Ro siacht a m-bresmaidm ocus a fuamannai ocus a freccurtai co fircleithi sleibi Olimp in conair on cusna rancatar goethu no toirni na nell uretrom etorbuasach inn aeoir fuasnadhuigh riamh.
Ro freccrait na gairi-sin & na nualleigmhi cetna i comhglendaibh slebhi Heim, & inn uamhannaip imdorcaibh shlebhe Peil, & i m-bendaib bitharda sleibi Pinn, ocus i caircibh cenngarbae sleibi Paing, & in all-cnocoip agadlethnaibh slebhi Oeta, ocus in n-uiliph diamraibh ocus ditrebaibh na Tesaili arcenae.
Ocus ba h-adbur urecclai dano dona slógaib con-uargaibhsett na gairi sin fein eistecht re a freccurtaibh doridhisi asna h-inadaip sin ina n-docomm, ina m-bui do graigibh & d'almaib ech ocus indili, ocus do tretaib torc ocus mucrad, & d'ailbinibh oss ocus alltu eccennais, ocus do damraidh diceill dásachtuigh i foithrib na Tesali.
Tanccattar inn aeinfecht lasna gairib sin co m-batar for dobur ocus for dasacht i timcill na cath for lar in muighe, co n-derna fot crithach don muigh fo a cossaibh, ettar daini & alma ocus innili, cona bui a samail acht mad talamcumsccughadh tisedh ann, co ro rainset ratha ocus cathracha & caisteoil & tempaill dea & relci idal ocus cumtaighthe cloch & claradh in tire lasin toranncrith mor sin, gor'bo moiti ba difulaing doibh cloistecht re fogurmuirn in muighe fos, cona búi a barsamail acht amail bad bann don brath do berta isin uair sin ind.
La soduin ro cotar na slúaig for a trealmaib diubraicthi, & ro gabsat ica n-imluad do cechtar in da leithi.
Batar di-airmidhe re n-airdmes iat-sen.
Robtar imda amh ic a n-imluadh etarrai fogadha faebracha & bera bodhbha biraighthi & cuailleda cendloisccthe ocus saighti foibrighthi fororda occus mulclocha glac & liacca lamh & uvuill-mill iarnaidhe & pluicmill luaide & crundchlocha taball.
Ba h-e tricci & imluas inn imdiubraicthi leo conach bui nach tairisimh for a n-urcoraib occo, no nach n-uiresbaid, acht a m-bith ina n-dluithneoll dubdorcha isin aer uassaibh can tolladh, can tanughadh airet batar na sloig for a trealmaibh diubraicti, co ro dicleithset solsi ind láei forru ind airett batar na dorchata dermara sin dar na cathaibh & dar maigib na Tesali uile fothu, amail niullu fleochuidh, no amail dobur n-dubciach, nó amail dall-fedha i foghamhar, co tuititis iarom 'na frasaibh neimhi & 'na tolaib tromfertana i cobradhaiph na scieth, ocus i tulaib na starga ocus na m-boccoiti, & i n-drolaib na luirech & i corraib na n-dillat, i cennaip ocus i corpaib na fer & na n-each, comtar ile fuile forta & crechta & cnedha & letarta dileighis.
Nir b'inann duthracht la lucht na n-diubraicte-sin cena, ar ba se duthracht dreime dib cona dibhraictis urcor n-imroill isin cath, can guin carat no esccarat de.
Dream aili ba se a n-duthracht guin a n-escarat nama.
Drem aile ba ferr leo co taethsad a n-airm dimain asa lamhaibh isin talamh gan guin carat no escarat dibh.
Acht cena ni boi a cummus-sin leo-som, ar ni fer d'airithe no aimsed neach and, acht a n-airm do diubraccadh isin aer os na cathaib co tuititis for na slogaib amail ro ordaigedh an toicthiu no an t-urcor iat.
Acht cena as mo ro fairrgit sluagh Poimp desin ina sluagh Cesair, ar as dluithe ro batar & as lugha ro soichtis na h-airm an talam treotha.
In crobhuailidh bodba dano ro ordaigh Poimp, co m-maithibh in t-senaidh immi in n-airisin ind imbualta & i tuinighthe in catha moir ro tairisetar a n-inadaib a coss for lar in cathae, ocus ro dluithigsit co daingen iet.
Do ronsat amdabaigh n-doscailti dib & scellbolg do sciathaib ina timcell & uasaibh, co m-benadh bili in sceith ria araile dib.
Indar-lat cona bai ní badh eislinn doib acht a n-airm fen dia crechtnugad ar a rodlus ro innletar iat, ocus as inuectain dia coemsaitis a lama do luth no a n-armu d'imirt i n-agaid a m-bidhbadh isin rodlus i r-rabhatar fos co reithfitis carpait ceithirreidh foraib.
Morsocraite in domain immorro do dechatar i toirithin Poimp ed ón ciniuda na h-Aissia & na h-Affraice, & lucht na n-innsedh do muir Torrein.
Ni ro dluithighset re socraite in t-senaidh Romanaig, acht batar co h-edluith esraiti uathu for leith.
Araidhi ni ro saigset ind imairicc fos biucc, ar bói tincoscc o Poimp forru cona remtiastais in crobuailidh moir i m-batar na Románaig i frestal na h-ergaile.
I S annsin ro innsaigsett eitedha catha Cesair & a marcsluagh ocus a mergeda & tosach a shloigh co sanntach in lathair i n-ucht muintere Poimp.
Ro leicced marcslog muinteri Poimp ina n-agaidh side dia fubtad & ro fosaigset imairecc n-ugra forru.
O 'tconcatar dano socraiti Poimp sin ni ro cumhgadh a n-imfostadh, acht ro meabaid sruithleccadh da saigdeoraib & da n-occmiledhaiph etromaib & da n-oes occbaid & da n-glaslaith, cois ar cois frisin marcsluagh, cur' gabsat a n-inadh imairicc fir ar fir i l-lathair in catha Ro feradh an cath co ferrda annsin iaram, & atrochratar sochaide re h-edh n-athgairit annsidhe.
Ro airig Cesair airsidhecht muintire Poimp 'arsin, & rob omhan lais sodh da marcsluagh & da mergedhaib & do thossach a sloigh rempu ara deiniu ocus ara dighaire & ara edlús ro innsaighset a muinter an cath, & ara rodhlus tangatar muinter Poimp.
I S edh do roine iaromh, ro coirigh co obann a cathai coisidhe ina stuaigh bodhbha i timcill a marcsluagh ocus a mergedh & lochta in tosaigh, conach soiti asa n-inadhaib iat.
Ro cothaig iaram in n-imairecc ina h-inad amlaidh sin, & ro dedhail Cesar brotlom sloig romoir for leith uadh, ocus ro chuir co tinnisnuch uadh iat i timcioll in catha, co tancatar da lethtaibh dochom slúaigh Poimp in conair na ro shailset a taidhecht etir ina n-docom & in t-imairecc for congbail ina inadh fein fos.
Ro scuchsat co seitreach da saigidh & ro doirtset co dana forta iat, cona rainic o marcshluagh Poimp impodh da frestal intan ro clannsat muinter Cesair a craiseacha crannremru i m-bruinnib & i n-ochtaib & a n-aiblenaib a n-each, co l-lingtis in arda na h-eich, co tecmaitis na marcaigh foena fothaibh & fo a cossaib.
Ni h-aitheirghi no leiccti doiph, acht no scartitis muinter Cesair a cinnu da claidhbibh dib.
Ni ro gabadh nach n-eisimul o muintir Poimp ed ón o na coisidhibh batar ettarra, acht ro comtuaircit uili, ar ni ro leiccit a córugud no a n-ordugud doib don leith dia tancus Bai immorro da deini & da tricci ro tuairgit intan no bid an fer dibh acc triall a aighthi d'impodh for a bidbaidh d'ferthain comlainn fris ni roichedh leth-impodh lais antan no chlandadh in fer do muintir Cesair in craisigh ina cnes no do beired rucaill don claidem dar a muinel co n-eiscced a cend da cuil-meidhe.
Nirbo fota ro bai an cath can dul do lethleth annsin, ar ni bhói ic socraiti Poimp acht fulang a marbtha, & muinter Cesair a n-aenar ic gnim inn imairicc, ar rainic coimdilsi ann etir longaib bronn na sochaidhe ocus claidhme muintire Cesair.
Ro treiccsett na cineda barbarda & in t-socraite a naire annsin, & ni tucsat da n-oidh, ocus ni ro cuimnighset a n-inadha catha do congmail, acht ro impodh a marcsluagh i cend a coissidhi, ocus tuccsat uile a n-aigthe for aenleith 'arsin, etir coissidhi ocus marcach, ocus ro coimdilsighset na dromanna do muintir Cesair.
Nírbtar feich obtha la muintir Cesair sin, ar ro ghabsat co sanntach dian-dichra dluith-denmnetach ic a tuargain ina n-diaidh ic clandadh a craisiuch ina corpaib, ic sadhadh a slegh ina slesaib ocus ina n-airnip ocus i fasaib a taeb, ic coimgerradh a cos ocus a caeldromann, a méidedh ocus a múinel da tuagaib & da claidhbip, ic brud a formnadh ocus a cloiccend da n-gunfainnip niadh ocus da loirgfertsibh catha.
Rob ainmesardha in t-ar tuccadh annsin.
Ni raibe modh no mesair forar' marbad ann.
Nir'bo h-ingnad sin cena, ar gérbo linmar lúthmur data deglamaigh in lucht marbta ro bai ina n-diaidh-siumh ni tainic dhibh airlech in neich do fetfaidthe do marbad ann don th-slúag ro teich dibh ar a n-imat ocus as a n-dlus ocus ar reidhe in muighi.
Acht cena ni h-asslach fuaratar, ocus ni maithom n-anacail ocus ni trocaire ro dechad forra, acht lor a n-aiccnidh ocus a menman do tuitim dib lasin slógh ro bai ina n-diaidh.
I S amlaid sin ro taipnedh socraite Poimp don muigh.
Ranccus iarsin cusna buidnib medonchoib ocus cusanu tenn ocus cusan tairisi ocus cusin laim ar culu ro bui ic Poimp ed ón in brainech bodba ocus an t-innell aigh ro h-ordaighedh n-airis inn imbualta ocus i tuinighthi an chatha moir, airm i r-rabatar treoin ocus tigernadha, treabaind ocus tusigh ocus commiti ocus cennturi, conssuil ocus comairlidh & cuingidhi na Roma & lucht gaiscid an t-senaid Romhanaigh, ocus teglach Poimp impo.
Ocht catha & ceithri fichit cath do mhiledaib armtha & dá mile traigthech & cét in cach mile dhibh-side ina corugad oencatha, & Lentulus consul co ceithriph leigionaibh lain-imdhaibh imaille friss i m-beind cli in catha, & Domit tuseach cathrach Corpin cusin lin cetna ina beind aile, & Scip mac Scip maic Scip Affracain co moirthinol na Cilecdha immi i n-airenach a etermedoin in catha cetna.
O ranccatar muinter Cesair in cathfhal neimhi sin, ro coirighset co dlúth-daingen immo tigerna iat ina n-aenbroin oencatha.
Ro gabh cach a inad imbuailti ann, amal ro coirigit iat o thosach, ocus ro h-ordaigit, ocus tuccsat a n-aighthi uile a n-óinfhecht ar an cath mor sin muintire Poimp.
Ba gairbiu ina gaeth, ba deiniu ina seitedh teinedh, ba troma ina tuile, ba treisi ina ruadbuinne roburta, ba merburba ina tot murtonn in mormara ro h-ucht alla no airdsleibe, in tolg & in tulscan & in ruathar roimher roithren roborb roidhiumsach ruccsat i cenn na caithetarnaidhe sin ro bai ic muintir Poimp.
Nirbo luth re letredh doib-sium on cena, & nirbo turrac gan tubha, & nirbo reim gan freassabra, ar ba cruaide ina carrac, & ba daingni ina dair, & ba tairismighi ina tulach & ba fostu ina sliabh in fothughadh & in cothughadh ocus in fossughadh & an fairisiumh do ronsat muinter Poimp for a cinn.
Ro fuirgeadh conach catha Cesair annsin, & ro tairis an t-ag ann.
Ro fosaighedh an ergal & an t-imairecc ann.
Ro congbadh an cath ina inadh.
Ro timairgset impo & ro ansat occa for a scath ina m-boi do slógaib co h-anbail enda easraiti for scailed ocus for scainnredh fo maigib na Tesaili da gach aird dibh. arni socraiti eachtrand nó ciniudha comaighthe no buidne barbardha ro gniset an cathugud annsin etir, acht firmuinter diles & senáes gradha Poimp ocus Cesair ed ón milidh merdana mormenmnacha & gasraid gaisccedhach an t-senaidh Romanaigh adiu & anall, na h-aithri & na maccu, na braithri & na clemhnu, na carait & na coiceili, ucht re h-ucht & a n-agaid araili.
Rancatar na catha cenn i cenn annsin cona raibi dlug diubraicthi no edh urchuir ettarru.
O immarainic doib iarum ro lupsat na latha gaile, & ro cromsatt na catha cechtarda annsin ic slaigedh a sciath & i fochlithar a starga ocus a m-bocoiti.
Ocus ro cuas leo dano i n-urdornaib a claidhemh claislethan coilgdíriuch & i rúadhbholgánaibh a sleg snasta & i m-muinighin a manaisi & a l-laigen lethanchenn, & a craisiuch crófairsing crainnremar, cu ro coirighset co comard a r-renna bodba biraighthi docom araili, co m-ba samalta re sraitsligidh crandcha comairdi eter da lini lanfotu do tighibh taeibhshlemhnu & do caprachaib comdluta claraidh inn aen na rigbaili romor in clardroichet comard comdluith coimreidh coimdiriuch dorighnedh do ruadh-crandgail na slegh slinngorm leo, eter na da scellbolg dluithe deghcoirigthe batar do clarscíathaib moraib aladhbreacaip da gach leith dibh adiu & anall.
Co cingfitis ríghna rotroma, nó seisi sloigh romoir, no assain fo n-eiredaibh fortha on aircenn co araill don cath cechtarda can scainredh gan fannughadh, can fescred fortha ar a cruas & ar a caiti ro congbait a n-iriella i n-dornoib na n-deglaech, & ar a sonairte ro saidhit & ar a daingne ro dingit a slenna & a fograinne i cnesaib crechtnaighthi na curadh comnart do cechtar in da leithi, go ro dailit luirecha tonnaidh ocus deocha dianbais i m-beolaibh sochaidhe ettarru, gurro trasccrait ilmhile re h-edh n-athgairit for in lathair sin leo.
Do ronait ochra ammalta i cosmailius bili bernaig do bordaibh in catha cechtarda 'arsin, uair gach airm i m-bitis na treinfir talchara & na milid mormenmnacha & na h-erredha aigh & na galgata gaisccidh in n-airenachaibh na cath no bristis bernada mora, & no bertis tolga aidbli isin cath for a n-inchaib, co n-ascnaitis airenaighi na cath i n-glacaib araili amal renna mara for tír no tiri for muir.
No mudhaigtis dano treinfir tabarta na tolg sin focetoir i crislaigibh na cath n-eachtrann, co n-dunta in scellbolg sciath daraneisi co tairsedh riaghail dromann an sceith for airenaigibh na cath isin coir cetna doridhisi.
Ro bai cach uile co coimdichra fo coimfeidm isin cath o sin immach, ar ro cotar uile airenaigi inn imairicc, & occbaidh inn imbuailti for imbirt a claidem & a l-laigen & a n-gunfainni niadh & a l-loirgfertus catha ann.
Ro cotar na curaidh ba coimnesamh doib da culaibh for a slegaib senta & for a ruadhgaib remra romora & for a manaisib fata faebracha, & cach oen nach rainicc imbualadh no imguin occo ro gabsat for tuargain a m-bidbad da trealmaib diubraicti darcenn a carat & a coimmiled, co m-ba samalta re h-aireccur cetha cloichsnechta for cumhtaighibh cloch no claraidh comtuaircnech na liacc lamh & na cloch n-glaice, & na crunncloch as na taiblib, & na n-uballmell iarnaidhe dar tulaib na sciath & dar lannaibh na luirech & dar circhimhsaibh na cathbarr.
Ba samalta re h-ordaibh urshlaide for inneoin trici & treisi, bailce & brigmaire beimonn na claidem claislethan & tuairgnighe na tuagh n-daingen n-defaebrach & tromsliustan na lorgfertus catha dar bilib na sciath, dar formnaib na fer, dar leicnib na laech, dar ochurchimsaib na n-assan iarnaidhe in gach cern & in gach cuil don cath.
Ba samalta re bolgaib sidi icc seited bolgfadhach & seitfedhach & uffolgach na n-anradh ic urgabhail a n-anala & ic a telcon doridisi, re tricci na m-beimenn & re dlus a n-imbualta & re h-aidhbhliu na fedmann no fuilngitis in gach aird don cath.
Ba samalta re solusnellgail ciach ica toccbail in n-airde re teas n-greini a tus laithi solusta samhraidh in brat-nellgal oeingheal atracht uasu do cailc na sciath scamanta 'arna scris d'faebraip na tuagh & na claidem & arna seitedh inn urarda do sheitfedhaigh & d'analfadhaigh na laechraide & na fer fortren ic fulang na n-anforlann & ic imluadh a n-gnim n-gaisccidh isin cath.
Ba samalta re saignenaibh tentidhe tre nellaibh urettroma aeoir sidedha na saiget solustae, gristaitnem & taidlenach na tuag & na claidem & na n-arm n-aith n-urnocht ica n-imluadh & ica n-imclaechladh os cennaib na curadh, a rigthib na rigmiled, & a l-lamaib na laechraide, re luas na m-beimmenn & re bailce inn imbualta & re h-imfoicsi na toccbal & na tairnemh.
Ba samalta re h-imaithigedh & re siubal na saithe m-bech os a m-bechlannaib i l-ló ainli inn imaithiged imdluith imfoccus no bidh immosech suas & anuas os a cennaib, ed ón cobrada na sciath & cira na cathbarr & slenna na sleg & cinn na craisech & faeburoghadha na tuagh & blaga na claidem combriste ic diansceinmnech & ic dianleimnech i n-urarda suas & ic prap-tintodh anuas ina frithseol cetna doridisi 'arna combrudh uile tre airsidheact na n-anradh i m-medon in mórchatha.
Ba samalta re slamaib snechtaidhe ic snighi no re tuighe rigbaile romoir ic a scuabadh ina dluithibh deilighthe re gaith roitrein amal ro snigset monga & fuilt & ulchae & trillsi na trenfer do corraib na tuagh & d'uigib na claidem & do cennaib na craisech & do slennaibh aithi ochurgera na slegh sliptha & do rennaib na ruadhghai.
Ba samalta re sruithlinntip abannshleibi ic siledh tre caraidh cloch srotha & srebana na fola flannruaidhe ic tepersin tre drolaib na luirech a cnescorpaib na curad isin cath.
I S dichra neimhiarmartach ro feradh an cath iarsin.
Ro ba neimneach in comrac, roba cruaidh in comthuargain & in coimhchrectnugudh & in coimcherpadh & in coimcheppad do ronsat curaidh in catha cechtarda ic gabail a fedmann catha forru.
Ní rabatar gairi catha occo osin immach.
Ni ro sinnit stuic na sturgana no adurca aigh nó cuirn comairc no cuslenna catha leo, o rancatar a fedmanna catha for na curadaibh occo, ar ro bai a n-obair & a feidm ic a fulang.
Atcluinti ann cena neithi imdha agmura adhuathmura aili.
Atcluinti ann am tulguba na sciath & clobeimnech na claidem & fidren na fogadh faebrach & scretgaire na slegh slipta & sibhsanach na saighet.
Atcluinti ann briscbruar & bresmadhmann na n-arm n-aichtidhi n-urnocht ic a m-brudh & ic a minugudh i l-lamaib na laechraidhe.
Atchluinti ann fetgairi na slegh ic a sadudh & feoil-beimenna na tuagh ic a tairnemh & sustgal & urshlaide na loirg-fertus catha ic a n-imluadh.
Atcluinti ann coicetal na claidem claislethan coilgdírech re tulaibh & re bilibh & re bordaibh na sciath scellbolgach, re drolaib & re dualaibh & re slabradhaib na luirech, re claraibh & re cimsaib na cathbarr, re fiaclaibh fer & re cnamaib curadh & re muinelmeidhibh miledh.
Atcluinti ann cubranach & bolgfarnach na fola flannruaidhe ic tepersin 'na taesccaibh & icc snighi 'na sruthanaibh a h-aladaibh & a crechtaibh na curadh ar slechtaib na n-arm.
Atcluinti ann srengal na luirech ic a m-blogadh & ic a m-bretcadh, & echrais na n-anradh ic a n-imbirt, masladach & tusledach na trenfer trascairte, & lecraide na laech ic furmiudh na m-beimenn, & cnetach na fer ic a fulang.
Atcluinti an claignech na cenn ica claidhbed, & ruchtgal na muinel & na meidhedh dar éis na cenn, & faisbedgarnach na m-bruinnech & na m-bronnann daréis a n-inne & a n-inathraigh, & carnfadhach na curadh ic etarscaradh re n-anmannaib & ic blasachtaig bais.
Atcluinti ann bodurfuamann compur na triath & na trenfer ic tuitim i crislaigaibh a sciath, & blaidredhach na sciath ic a scoltad fotha.
Atcluinti ann uchbadhach & accaine na n-occlaech ocus seitfedach na senoiri & geran na n-galgat & cuadan na curadh & muirni na miled & uilg tuilg na trenfer ic dith a nert, & ic sarughad a n-glond gaisccidh & ic fortamlughadh co forranach forta, & ic fulang a n-anforlainn romoir.
Atcluinti ann allgotha móra arda allmurda na n-uasal & na n-airdrig & na n-armann ic fubtadh a m-bidbad & ic gresacht a muintire im calma do denam.
I S annsin ro gab Cesair dano for toccbail a gnim rigda os aird isin cath o 'tconnairc a fedmanna catha for cach.
Ro lin bruth & brigh, & faelscadh & dasacht & confadh & mire menman & aiccentae é o' tconnairc in cath ic a congbhail ina agaid, cona bai a samail acht amail innister in Badhbh catha do beith cona sraighlibh fuilidhibh ina laim i timcill na cath ic aslach inn imairicc for na slógaib.
Ba h-amlaid sin do Cesair trena muintir & ina timcell, ar ni fagbaiti nach n-uresbaidh fair i tús nó a n-deiridh, no i m-beind no i medhon no i cúil nó i ceirn nó i n-aird nó in-aircinn nó inn airenach don cath, acht atar le lucht cach inaidh dib-sin as ettarra a n-aenar no bidh, & se gan anadh gan airisemh o tus co deiredh in catha, ic drud & ic dinge & ic dluthughadh na slogh isin irgail, ic nertadh na nía, ic laidedh na laech, ic gresacht na n-galgat, ic muilliudh na miledh, ic brosdad na m-buidhen, ic urail inn anta, ic tennadh in tairismhi, ic aslach na h-innsaigthe; co tabradh som fuilled morneirt & calmatais i m-menmandaibh a miledh & a n-aiccentaib a óccláech tresin n-greasachtbrostad sin, ge m-ba dichra duthrachtach no beitis reimi ic slaigi a n-escarat & icc airlech a m-bidbad.
No bidh can airisemh dano ag adhmoladh a n-imbualta, & icc brethugudh for a n-gnimaibh gaiscidh, ocus ic mes a m-builled & a m-bemenn, & ic sirtincaisin a claidemh, dus cia dib isa claidem ba cróderg uili d'fuil no ba dercc rinn no faebur nammae, nó cia dib no laccadh a feidm catha, no cia no tennadh ara omun-sumh & ara uráilemh, nó cia dibh isa claidem no ferad in crecht, nó cia do beradh an beim co furmiudh, nó cia no fuirmedh in beim da m-bítis a righthe for comboccadh & for crithnugudh o dornchor in claidim co a gualainn.
In drem ann dano isa claidhbhi no maelta nó isa h-airm no briste no dhailedh Cesair focetoir a n-daethain airm gan uiresbaid doib.
In drem ghonta nó bidh icon imbualad & a sreabana cro & a taescca fola ic tepersin dar a crechtaibh dos-roichedh Cesair ocus no druidedh a bassa fri belaibh a n-alad noco roichedh uadh a n-daethain sop ocus inrech da n-étaighib inntu.
In dream dno uilimarbta ann, immorro, no brostaigedh mileda úaru ina n-inadhaib, & na milidh na freccratais a gut-som nó a forcongra fochetoir immi sin no gressadh-sum & no imáinedh reimhi iat de urlannaib a sleg noco n-gabtais áit inn imairicc.
No mhuinedh & no suaicentaighedh na saerclanna & raigne na Roman dóibh.
No tairmisccedh impo daesccursluagh & daine dinnimhe dereoile do marbadh.
No asslaighedh & no urailedh fortho immorro lucht cadais & ceimend n-onorach & sil righ & rodaine in t-senaidh do mudugadh, ar as trena n-díthugudh ro sail-siumh righi & flaithius d'fogbail do fein & da muintir.
Do ghnidh buidechus mor & do beiredh moladh adbal for in dreim no diubraictis cinnu a carut co forníata uatha ar tabairt aichne fortha, & siat fein ar na n-dicendadh-side ar son escarat, ar ni finntais sochaidhe dib cia frisi fertais a comlann, ar no ditnitis na sceith & na luirecha & na cathbharra iat, conidh arna marbadh & arna fodhbughadh do beirtis aichne for cennaib a carat & for a collaibh nochta ina fiadnaisi.
Ba h-aicher ainmin anacarthach ainseircc ro feradh in caitgleo-sin muintire Poimp & Cesair.
Rob amhnus inn imguin.
Roba tric in t-imbualadh.
Rob imluath inn imdeghail.
Roba garb in galach.
Roba mor miceill.
Roba borb brathamail in commarbadh & in comhmudughadh ro bai for maigh na Tesaili an uair-sin leo.
Mor corp saerclannda soicineoil do comartatar claidhmhi claislethna curadh ettarra.
Mór laech luthmur laimtenach ro letrait do laignib lethanglassaibh etarru.
Mor cnes curad ro cerbbait do saigtibh snasta a sithbacaibh etarra.
Mor taeb treinfer ro tollait do slegaib slipta slinnlethna etarra.
Mor n-dromcla n-deglaech ro daingin-tuairgit do liaccaibh lamh & do loirgfertsibh catha eturra.
Mor milidh merdana mórmenmnach ro mudaighit do manaisibh murnechaibh etarra.
Mor fer firduilech foirniata ro foirrgit co forranach tre imforcraidh in eccomlainn etarra.
Mor m-buiden m-brigach m-borrfadach ro fostait i m-buailibh bais & inn ithlannaib ecca etarru.
Mor n-airdrígh n-uasal n-oirdnidhe forar' h-imredh midhiach ettarru.
Mor n-deighfer fial forusta forbfaili ro chotar d'aittib urgranna anaipche ettorru.
Mor n-occlaech alainn agedchain, & mór senlaech sirduilech?
serbsrón do rochratar i n-othurligib ecca ettarra.
Mor rig rogarg rodiumsach, & mor tuisech tenn talcur tairismech isa meic & isa h-úi & isa carait & isa comshloinntigh ro comhdigbait immailli friu fein ettarru.
Ro fasatar ocus ro forbretar iaram cuirp & cinn & colla na Románach sochenelach i m-medhon in armaigh iarsin, co m-batar 'na carnaib & 'na cnoctulcaib comarda & 'na n-druimnibh & 'na n-dumadhaibh dimóra ann can cummusc daerchlann no daescurslógh no daine n-dereoile forra, acht madh fir-frema dilsi na Roman fein amain do neoch as rigda & as saire & as soichenelciu tainic riam dib im sil Reim & Romail & Iuin, Uuilt & Mair & Mairc & Meteill & Sill & Scip & Caitt & Cuir & Camill & Catrin & Corpin: im sil Faib & Vair & Antoin & Luig & Lucil & Torquait diumsaigh, & im sil na rigflaithe Romanach arcena & na n-deigfer n-dingmála ro chinsett o Aeneas mac Anacis & o Asccan mac Aeneása anuas cusin aimsir sin in air moir i muigh na Tesali.
Acht cena gérbo imda cuirp deglaech & colla saerclann ina faenlighi for muigh na Tesali isin uair-sin, araisin roba suaichnid airerda corp inn oenocclaigh ic fagbail bais ettarru, & as allata mormenmnach ro cuaidh docum n-écca ed ón Doimit tuiseach cathrach Corpin isin Etail.
Lainfear gradha & cuingid comairle don airdrigh ed ón do Poimp, eside, intan tainic Cesair for tosach a shlogaid isin Etail.
Ro fobair an fer sin a caistiall do congbhail ina aghaid & gan gialladh do etir & gan a ríarugudh, co n-deachaidh Cesair ar eiccin for an caistiall, go rabatar a aittrepaidh & Domit fén for a commus.
Co tucc Cesair a sáiri dó, & gur' leicc imshlan uadh é dochom a tigerna fein.
Tarla Cesair annsin cuici dano & Domit for anamthaigh ina freslighi isin ármaigh, & crechta letarta fata fiartarstna mora tairis & tregmadhae doimne difhulaing & mersce dileigis ann, & se fein ic a imbirt ocus ic a fothraccadh isna linntip dubfolae & isna h-aibnib cro batar fo cosaibh na curadh isin chath.
Tencais Cesair fair, & anais os a cinn isin cath, & asbert fris: ‘Sirsan duit beith amlaidh sin, a Doimit,’ ol Cesair; ‘as failidh linn do scaradh re coimitecht & re comairle Poimp, ocus in cathughad do gnim darteis festu.’
‘I S failid lim-sa dano,’ for Domit, ‘tocht saor docum bais amal teigim, & Poimp ina tigerna damh, & t'facbail-si dar m'eisi gan clodh catha for mo cairdibh beos.’
I S inuechtain ro fogluais a beolu frisin m-becc n-urlabra-sin intan ro línsat dorcata an bais a rusca & dus-fainic in suan suthain & dubchotludh iarnaidhe inn ecca, & ro scar a ainim re a corp, & fuair bas ar maig na Tesaile amlaidh-sin.
I S truag tra ro bas isin cath 'arsin.
Rob imda ann fuaim saigte re setnaigh saerclann, & fuaim claidib ic a clannadh i corp, & fuaim sleigi ic a sadudh i slis, & fuaim tuaighi icc tesccadh treinfir, & fuaim biaili ic brudh bidbadh, & fuaim luirgi re luirigh, & fuaim cloichi re cathbarr, ocus mell dar mallainn miledh.
Rob imda ann dano sceith ic a scoltadh, & targa ic a tesccad, & luirecha daingne ic a n-dianscailedh, ocus asana iarnaide ic a n-athcuma, & cathbairr ic a combrudh, ocus caithcreasa ic a cruaidhletradh, & claicne curad ic a claidhmedh.
Rob imdha ann dano meidhi maelderga, & eirrsci omha úirtescdha, & aladha obela oslaicthi, & crechta urae ainmesardha & tregmada doimne dileigis, & letartha fata fiarcamma, & fuasmada garbta gaibtecha, & beimenna tuitmi, & builledha marbta, & gona bais.
Rob imdha ann dano cuirp cirrthi, & cnis cerbta, & taoib tolla, & laich lonna letartha, & lama leonta, & cind combristi, ocus oicc athgaiti, ocus milidh marbta, & galgata gonta, & anraidh 'arna n-airlech, & colla curadh i cosair cro.
Rob imdha ann dano fir i faenligibh, ocus aighthi frengbana fuataite, & gnuisi galgat icc glassadh, ocus baill basda ic bidgarnaig, ocus suile ic a saebad, ocus beoil bana ic blasachtaigh, ocus meidheda saerchlann ic snighi, & scamana tescta ic tobruchtaigh, ocus cinn chruinne i coimrith, & ruip reptha ic ruchtaigh, ocus uchtbruinnedha echda ic a n-urtoccbail, ocus cridhedha tolla ic tepersin, ocus lama letartae ic leimnech, & bonnchosa bana barbardhae ic brebgail.
Rob imda ann dano deghlaeich ic dula re h-aididh n-anapaigh, ocus drochdhiach ar degduine, ocus airrlech namhat ar collaib righ.
Rob imdha ann dano aidedha ecnecha anaichinta, ocus ernaile imdha étualaing ica n-imbirt for anradaibh.
Robtar ile na h-asrusa ecca, ocus robtar saini na sligthi bais ro batar re curadaib an catha & re n-occaibh na h-imgonai annsin, uair drong mor ann & as amlaidh no bitis ic gnim in imairicc, & na slega & na claidhmhi comtarsna trempo.
Drong mór aile ann dano, & as amlaidh no bitis ic gnim in imairicc, & iat 'na suidhe & a cossa 'arna tesccadh fotho i comarda fri bordchimsaibh a l-luirech.
Drong mór aili ann dano, ocus as amlaid no bitis, ocus iat 'na sesamh ocus a n-inathraighi for ochursnam re a cosaibh, ocus iat icc tuinnsiumh ocus ic saltarnaigh fortha.
Drong mor aile ann dano, ocus is amlaid no bitis, ocus siat 'na sesam ar tesccadh a l-lamh ocus a m-ball dib co talam, & iat icc suinnenaigh a m-bidbadh da n-gúaillibh ocus da cosaibh, ar ni bidh cumang imghona no imbuailti aili occo.
Drong mór aili et cetera, ocus claidhmi a m-bidbad arna clannadh ina cráesaib ocus iatt ic comhchoccnamh na claidem ocus icc atchur a n-anmann imailli friu dara m-belaib seachtair.
Drong mór aile et cetera, ocus iat ic fuirmiudh in beime ocus iat fein ic comthuitim docomh láir leis.
Drong mór et cetera, & iat ic tobruchtadh fo cassail i m-bronn & arm a namat i n-áinfhecht dar a m-bruinnibh sechtair.
Drong mór aili et cetera & a taescca folu & a sreaba cro icc snighi asa corpaiph, & ni praipiti no antais don imbualadh fos noco b-faccbadh a fuil ocus a nert ocus a n-ainim i n-aeinfecht iat.
Drong mór aili et cetera, ocus iat ina lighi co landluith re lar, & airm a namhat & a slegha saidhti trena corpaibh, co n-gabtais in talam-tuinide trempo.
Drong mór aili et cetera, & a l-lamha dessa icon imbualadh ocus a l-lamha cléa icc congbail a n-inni & a n-inathraigh inntu.
Drong mór aili et cetera, & iat fein ic dul docum bhais, & iat ic aichne a n-inaid catha do congbail da macaibh & da m-braithribh dar a n-eisi.
Drong mor aile, ocus as amlaidh no bitis, o tecmaitis a caruit ocus a coibnestu i cindcomair friu, intan ro soiched co a n-airlech ocus co fodbadh occo, no diubraictis cinnu a carut i ciana uatha, co m-badh lughaiti badh nar no badh meabul leo fodbadh na corp, o na tabairti aichni for a cendaibh occo.
Drong mór ailiu ann dano, is ed do beiredh an t-ircar doconaigh doib, co m-bitis ic airlech & ic fodbadh corp a n-aithriuch fodein, ocus o na taircced leo cind a n-aithri d'folach do bertis testa an talman do lucht a fiadnaisiu nach cuirp carutt itir no bitis ica fodbadh occo.
Uair sochaide cusa tarla i cinncomair friss isin cath mór-sa maighe na Tesaili a athair no a mac no a brathair no a cliamain no a com-chatharrda.
Conidh airisin ro faccsatt auctair na Roman ocus lucht cummae in sceoil-si comraic an cathu can a n-aisneis ocus gan a n-innisin, co suaicnidh.
I S tre cell & tre comairli dano ro faccsat na h-auctair cetnu righpersannu na Roman can suaicintugudh a n-gnimradh isin cath, fobith na bad leabur cuimnighthi folad da clannaibh daneis an scél-su, na ro eirged misccais ocus miduthracht ina cridhibh etarru fein, intan atcluinfitis a n-aithri ocus a m-braithri do commarbad araili i comraictib in cathae sae.
